## 🗄️ 第二部分：完整数据模型（DDL + SQLAlchemy 映射）

### 1. `models/comment.py` —— 评论核心表（含您文档中全部字段）
```python
from sqlalchemy import Column, String, Integer, DateTime, UUID, Text, Enum
from app.models.base import Base
import enum

class CommentStatus(str, enum.Enum):
    NEW = "NEW"
    ANALYZED = "ANALYZED"
    REPLIED = "REPLIED"
    IGNORED = "IGNORED"
    CONVERTED_DM = "CONVERTED_DM"

class Comment(Base):
    __tablename__ = "comments"
    
    id = Column(UUID, primary_key=True)
    platform = Column(String(30))                # 微信/抖音/视频号...
    account_id = Column(UUID)
    post_id = Column(String(128))
    user_id = Column(String(128))
    nickname = Column(String(255))
    content = Column(Text)
    comment_type = Column(String(20))
    status = Column(Enum(CommentStatus), default=CommentStatus.NEW)
    ai_intent = Column(String(50))               # PRICE/BUY/COMPARE/SPAM/CHAT
    ai_value_level = Column(String(10))          # A/B/C/D
    ai_score = Column(Integer)
    created_at = Column(DateTime)
    updated_at = Column(DateTime)
```

### 2. `models/task.py` —— 统一任务表（含优先级/重试）
```python
class Task(Base):
    __tablename__ = "tasks"
    
    id = Column(UUID, primary_key=True)
    task_type = Column(String(50))               # SEND_MESSAGE / SEND_IMAGE / SYNC_CONTACT
    target_id = Column(UUID)
    priority = Column(Integer, default=50)       # 0~100
    status = Column(String(20), default="pending")
    retry = Column(Integer, default=0)
    execute_at = Column(DateTime)
    created_at = Column(DateTime)
```

### 3. `models/customer.py` —— 客户表（含 profile JSONB）
```python
from sqlalchemy.dialects.postgresql import JSONB

class Customer(Base):
    __tablename__ = "customers"
    
    id = Column(UUID, primary_key=True)
    name = Column(String(100))
    phone = Column(String(50))
    source_platform = Column(String(32))
    source_account = Column(UUID)
    level = Column(String(20))
    deal_score = Column(Integer, default=0)
    tags = Column(JSONB, default=list)
    profile = Column(JSONB, default=dict)        # {budget, city, interest, stage}
    created_at = Column(DateTime)
```

### 4. `models/account.py` —— 账号池表
```python
class Account(Base):
    __tablename__ = "accounts"
    
    id = Column(UUID, primary_key=True)
    platform = Column(String(32))
    nickname = Column(String(100))
    status = Column(String(20), default="ACTIVE")  # ACTIVE/PAUSED/LIMITED/BANNED
    access_token = Column(Text)
    refresh_token = Column(Text)
    daily_limit = Column(Integer, default=500)
    today_sent = Column(Integer, default=0)
    last_active_at = Column(DateTime)
    created_at = Column(DateTime)
```

## 🧠 第三部分：核心运行时完整代码（`core/` 所有类）

### 1. `core/event.py` —— 统一事件协议
```python
import uuid
import time
from dataclasses import dataclass, field

@dataclass
class Event:
    user: str
    content: str
    platform: str
    account_id: str = None
    event_id: str = field(default_factory=lambda: str(uuid.uuid4()))
    timestamp: float = field(default_factory=time.time)
```

### 2. `core/state.py` —— 唯一状态内核（生产级Redis版本）
```python
import json
from app.utils.redis_client import redis_client

class StateKernel:
    @staticmethod
    def _key(user: str) -> str:
        return f"waos:state:{user}"
    
    @staticmethod
    def get(user: str) -> dict:
        data = redis_client.get(StateKernel._key(user))
        if data:
            return json.loads(data)
        return {"score": 0, "stage": "cold", "chat_count": 0}
    
    @staticmethod
    def update(user: str, patch: dict) -> dict:
        current = StateKernel.get(user)
        current.update(patch)
        current["score"] = max(0, min(100, current.get("score", 0)))
        redis_client.setex(StateKernel._key(user), 86400 * 30, json.dumps(current))
        return current
```

### 3. `core/crm.py` —— 生命周期CRM（含正负反馈）
```python
class CRM:
    @staticmethod
    def update(state: dict, msg: str) -> dict:
        score = state.get("score", 0)
        
        if any(kw in msg for kw in ["多少钱", "报价", "价格", "成交"]):
            score += 20
        if any(kw in msg for kw in ["再看看", "不需要", "太贵"]):
            score -= 10
        
        score = max(0, min(100, score))
        stage = "HOT" if score > 80 else "WARM" if score > 50 else "COLD"
        return {"score": score, "stage": stage}
```

### 4. `core/strategy.py` —— 单脑多策略路由器
```python
class StrategyRouter:
    @staticmethod
    def route(state: dict) -> str:
        score = state.get("score", 0)
        if score > 80: return "CLOSER_STRATEGY"
        elif score > 50: return "NURTURE_STRATEGY"
        else: return "FRIEND_STRATEGY"
```

### 5. `core/persona.py` —— 参数化Persona
```python
class Persona:
    @staticmethod
    def build(state: dict, strategy: str) -> dict:
        score = state.get("score", 0)
        return {
            "strategy": strategy,
            "tone": "professional" if score > 50 else "friendly",
            "pressure": min(score / 100, 0.9),
            "max_length": 150 if strategy == "FRIEND_STRATEGY" else 300,
            "use_case": strategy == "CLOSER_STRATEGY"
        }
```

### 6. `core/ai.py` + `core/constraint.py` + `core/safety.py`
```python
# ai.py
class AI:
    @staticmethod
    def run(msg: str, state: dict, persona: dict) -> str:
        strategy = persona["strategy"]
        if strategy == "CLOSER_STRATEGY":
            raw = "我帮您做一个最优成交方案"
        elif strategy == "NURTURE_STRATEGY":
            raw = "我帮您对比一下配置区别"
        else:
            raw = "哈哈这个挺有意思的"
        return Constraint.apply(raw)

# constraint.py
class Constraint:
    @staticmethod
    def apply(text: str) -> str:
        if len(text) > 300: text = text[:300]
        if "转账" in text: return "具体细节我们走正规流程沟通"
        return text

# safety.py
class Safety:
    BANNED = ["刷单", "诈骗", "色情"]
    @staticmethod
    def filter(text: str) -> str:
        for w in Safety.BANNED:
            if w in text: return "抱歉，这个我帮不上忙"
        return text
```

### 7. `core/rhythm.py` —— 统一节奏控制
```python
import time, random
class Rhythm:
    @staticmethod
    def apply():
        time.sleep(random.uniform(1.5, 4.5))
```

### 8. `core/priority.py` —— 优先级引擎公式
```python
class PriorityEngine:
    @staticmethod
    def calculate(value_score: int, customer_score: int, intent_score: int, activity_score: int) -> int:
        return int(value_score * 0.4 + customer_score * 0.3 + intent_score * 0.2 + activity_score * 0.1)
```

### 9. `core/pipeline.py` —— 单入口主流程（完整闭环）
```python
from app.core.event import Event
from app.core.state import StateKernel
from app.core.crm import CRM
from app.core.strategy import StrategyRouter
from app.core.persona import Persona
from app.core.ai import AI
from app.core.safety import Safety
from app.core.rhythm import Rhythm
from app.core.dedup import Dedup
from app.core.rate_limiter import RateLimiter
from app.adapters.base import BaseAdapter
from app.utils.logger import logger

def pipeline(event: Event, adapter: BaseAdapter):
    user = event.user
    
    # 1. 幂等
    if not Dedup.check(event.event_id): return
    # 2. 限流
    if not RateLimiter.allow(user):
        adapter.send(user, "请勿频繁发送")
        return
    
    try:
        state = StateKernel.get(user)
        crm_data = CRM.update(state, event.content)
        strategy = StrategyRouter.route(crm_data)
        persona = Persona.build(crm_data, strategy)
        reply = AI.run(event.content, crm_data, persona)
        reply = Safety.filter(reply)
        Rhythm.apply()
        adapter.send(user, reply)
        StateKernel.update(user, crm_data)
        logger.info({"event_id": event.event_id, "user": user, "reply": reply[:50]})
    except Exception as e:
        adapter.send(user, "系统繁忙，稍后回复")
        logger.error({"event_id": event.event_id, "error": str(e)})
```

## 🔌 第四部分：Adapter 完整实现（`adapters/`）

### `adapters/base.py`
```python
from abc import ABC, abstractmethod

class BaseAdapter(ABC):
    @abstractmethod
    def send(self, user: str, msg: str) -> dict:
        pass
```

### `adapters/wechat.py` —— ClawBot 真实适配
```python
from app.adapters.base import BaseAdapter

class WeChatAdapter(BaseAdapter):
    def __init__(self, clawbot_api_url: str = None):
        self.api_url = clawbot_api_url or "http://clawbot.local"
    
    def send(self, user: str, msg: str) -> dict:
        # 真实替换为 requests.post(f"{self.api_url}/send", json={...})
        print(f"[WX] to {user}: {msg}")
        return {"code": 0, "msg": "sent"}
```

### `adapters/clawbot/connector.py` —— 登录稳定层
```python
class ClawBotConnector:
    async def login(self, account_id: str) -> str:
        # 调用外部API获取token
        return "mock_token"
    
    async def send_text(self, to: str, content: str):
        pass
```

# 🔧 WAOS 系统修复补丁包 vFinal（全版块一次性交付）

---

## 📦 修复包 1：架构分层与 Pipeline 异步化（版块一）

### 🔴 问题诊断
- Pipeline 同步阻塞，AI 调用 5 秒会卡死 Worker 循环。
- 无超时熔断，AI 连续失败会导致雪崩。
- Pipeline 直接依赖 Adapter，违反依赖倒置。

### ✅ 修复方案
1. `pipeline` 全异步化（`async def`）+ `asyncio.timeout(10)`。
2. 引入简单熔断器（连续失败 5 次 → 10 秒内直接走 Fallback，不调 AI）。
3. Pipeline 只产出 `Action`，由外层 Dispatcher 路由到 Adapter（解耦）。

### 📄 修复后代码：`backend/app/core/pipeline.py`
```python
import asyncio
import time
from typing import Optional
from app.core.event import Event
from app.core.state import StateKernel
from app.core.crm import CRM
from app.core.strategy import StrategyRouter
from app.core.persona import Persona
from app.core.ai import AI
from app.core.safety import Safety
from app.core.rhythm import Rhythm
from app.core.dedup import Dedup
from app.core.rate_limiter import RateLimiter
from app.core.action import SendMessageAction  # 新增：动作对象
from app.utils.logger import logger

# --- 简单熔断器（内存版，生产可迁 Redis） ---
class CircuitBreaker:
    def __init__(self, failure_threshold=5, timeout=10):
        self.failure_threshold = failure_threshold
        self.timeout = timeout
        self.failure_count = 0
        self.last_failure_time = 0
        self.state = "CLOSED"  # CLOSED / OPEN / HALF_OPEN

    def allow(self) -> bool:
        if self.state == "OPEN":
            if time.time() - self.last_failure_time > self.timeout:
                self.state = "HALF_OPEN"
                return True
            return False
        return True

    def record_success(self):
        self.failure_count = 0
        self.state = "CLOSED"

    def record_failure(self):
        self.failure_count += 1
        self.last_failure_time = time.time()
        if self.failure_count >= self.failure_threshold:
            self.state = "OPEN"

_circuit_breaker = CircuitBreaker()

# --- 主流水线（异步 + 超时） ---
async def pipeline(event: Event) -> Optional[SendMessageAction]:
    """
    单入口主流程：Event -> Action
    返回 Action 对象，由上层 Dispatcher 执行发送
    """
    user = event.user

    # 1. 幂等检查
    if not Dedup.check(event.event_id):
        logger.warning(f"Duplicate event: {event.event_id}")
        return None

    # 2. 限流
    if not RateLimiter.allow(user):
        logger.warning(f"Rate limited: {user}")
        return SendMessageAction(user, "您发送消息太快了，请稍后再试。")

    # 3. 熔断器检查（防止 AI 雪崩）
    if not _circuit_breaker.allow():
        logger.warning(f"Circuit breaker OPEN for {user}, using fallback")
        return SendMessageAction(user, "系统繁忙，我稍后回复您。")

    try:
        # 4. 执行核心逻辑（带 10 秒超时）
        async def _core():
            state = StateKernel.get(user)
            # CRM 更新（含时间衰减）
            crm_data = CRM.update(state, event.content, event.timestamp)
            # 策略路由（传入 intent）
            intent = IntentClassifier.classify(event.content)  # 新增轻量分类
            strategy = StrategyRouter.route(crm_data, intent)
            # Persona 构建
            persona = Persona.build(crm_data, strategy)
            # AI 生成（含成本控制）
            reply = await AI.run_async(event.content, crm_data, persona, intent)
            # 安全过滤
            reply = Safety.filter(reply)
            # 节奏控制
            Rhythm.apply()
            # 状态持久化（异步写 PG + 更新 Redis）
            StateKernel.update(user, crm_data)
            return reply

        reply = await asyncio.wait_for(_core(), timeout=10.0)
        _circuit_breaker.record_success()

        # 5. 日志
        logger.info({
            "event_id": event.event_id,
            "user": user,
            "reply": reply[:50],
            "score": crm_data.get("score"),
            "stage": crm_data.get("stage")
        })

        return SendMessageAction(user, reply)

    except asyncio.TimeoutError:
        logger.error(f"Pipeline timeout for user {user}")
        _circuit_breaker.record_failure()
        return SendMessageAction(user, "系统处理超时，我稍后回复您。")

    except Exception as e:
        logger.error({"event_id": event.event_id, "error": str(e)})
        _circuit_breaker.record_failure()
        return SendMessageAction(user, "系统繁忙，我稍后回复您。")
```

### 📄 新增：`backend/app/core/action.py`
```python
from dataclasses import dataclass

@dataclass
class SendMessageAction:
    user: str
    content: str
```

### 📄 修改：`backend/app/worker/event_consumer.py`（消费循环调用 Dispatcher）
```python
async def consume_loop():
    while True:
        events = redis.xreadgroup(...)
        for event in events:
            action = await pipeline(event)
            if action:
                # 由 Dispatcher 路由到具体 Adapter
                await dispatcher.dispatch(action)
            redis.xack(...)
```

## 📦 修复包 2：状态管理原子性与时间衰减（版块二）

### 🔴 问题诊断
- Redis GET→SET 并发写覆盖。
- 无时间衰减，旧分数永久有效。
- Redis 与 PG 数据不一致。

### ✅ 修复方案
1. 用 Redis **Lua 脚本**实现原子性读写。
2. CRM 更新时加入时间衰减因子：`score *= (0.98 ** days_since_last_contact)`。
3. 策略：**PG 为主，Redis 为缓存**。StateKernel.update 先异步写 PG（或同步写，但用连接池），再刷新 Redis。

### 📄 修复后代码：`backend/app/core/state.py`
```python
import json
import time
from app.utils.redis_client import redis_client
from app.models.customer import Customer  # SQLAlchemy model
from app.db.session import SessionLocal

class StateKernel:
    @staticmethod
    def _key(user: str) -> str:
        return f"waos:state:{user}"

    # --- Lua 脚本：原子性读-改-写 ---
    _LUA_UPDATE_SCRIPT = """
    local key = KEYS[1]
    local patch = cjson.decode(ARGV[1])
    local ttl = tonumber(ARGV[2])
    
    -- 读取当前状态
    local current_str = redis.call('GET', key)
    local current = {}
    if current_str then
        current = cjson.decode(current_str)
    else
        current = {score = 0, stage = 'cold', chat_count = 0}
    end
    
    -- 应用 patch
    for k, v in pairs(patch) do
        current[k] = v
    end
    
    -- 边界保护
    current.score = math.max(0, math.min(100, current.score))
    
    -- 写回
    redis.call('SETEX', key, ttl, cjson.encode(current))
    
    return cjson.encode(current)
    """
    _LUA_UPDATE = redis_client.register_script(_LUA_UPDATE_SCRIPT)

    @staticmethod
    def get(user: str) -> dict:
        data = redis_client.get(StateKernel._key(user))
        if data:
            return json.loads(data)
        # 缓存未命中，从 PG 回填
        db = SessionLocal()
        try:
            customer = db.query(Customer).filter_by(wx_id=user).first()
            if customer:
                state = {"score": customer.deal_score, "stage": customer.stage, "chat_count": 0}
                redis_client.setex(StateKernel._key(user), 86400 * 30, json.dumps(state))
                return state
        finally:
            db.close()
        return {"score": 0, "stage": "cold", "chat_count": 0}

    @staticmethod
    def update(user: str, patch: dict) -> dict:
        # 使用 Lua 脚本原子执行
        result = StateKernel._LUA_UPDATE(
            keys=[StateKernel._key(user)],
            args=[json.dumps(patch), str(86400 * 30)]
        )
        state = json.loads(result)
        # 异步写 PG（生产用消息队列或异步任务）
        # 这里简化：同步写，但用 upsert
        db = SessionLocal()
        try:
            customer = db.query(Customer).filter_by(wx_id=user).first()
            if not customer:
                customer = Customer(wx_id=user)
                db.add(customer)
            customer.deal_score = state["score"]
            customer.stage = state["stage"]
            customer.updated_at = time.time()
            db.commit()
        finally:
            db.close()
        return state
```

### 📄 修复后代码：`backend/app/core/crm.py`（加入时间衰减）
```python
import time
from datetime import datetime

class CRM:
    @staticmethod
    def update(state: dict, msg: str, event_timestamp: float) -> dict:
        score = state.get("score", 0)
        last_seen = state.get("last_seen", event_timestamp)

        # 1. 时间衰减（每天衰减 2%）
        days_diff = (event_timestamp - last_seen) / 86400
        if days_diff > 1:
            score = score * (0.98 ** days_diff)

        # 2. 行为加分/减分
        if any(kw in msg for kw in ["多少钱", "报价", "价格", "成交"]):
            score += 20
        if any(kw in msg for kw in ["再看看", "不需要", "太贵"]):
            score -= 10
        if any(kw in msg for kw in ["投诉", "退款", "差评"]):
            score = max(0, score - 30)  # 紧急负面

        score = max(0, min(100, score))
        stage = "HOT" if score > 80 else "WARM" if score > 50 else "COLD"

        # 3. 返回 patch（包含时间戳）
        return {
            "score": int(score),
            "stage": stage,
            "last_seen": event_timestamp
        }
```

---

## 📦 修复包 3：AI 决策链（意图路由 + 成本控制 + Persona 曲线）（版块三）

### 🔴 问题诊断
- Intent 被忽略，SPAM 可能误回。
- Persona pressure 曲线错误（高意向不该强压）。
- 无成本控制，每次调用 LLM。

### ✅ 修复方案
1. 增加轻量级 `IntentClassifier`（规则 + 简单模型），路由时优先处理 SPAM。
2. Persona pressure 改为倒 U 型曲线：`score 40~70 最高，>80 降低`。
3. `AI.run` 加入成本控制：PRICE/FAQ 走知识库，LOW_SCORE 走模板，仅 HIGH_VALUE 走 LLM。

### 📄 新增：`backend/app/core/intent.py`
```python
class IntentClassifier:
    INTENT_MAP = {
        "PRICE": ["多少钱", "报价", "价格", "怎么卖"],
        "BUY": ["下单", "购买", "怎么买"],
        "COMPARE": ["对比", "区别", "哪个好"],
        "AFTERSALE": ["售后", "保修", "维修"],
        "SPAM": ["刷单", "广告", "色情", "违法"],
        "CHAT": ["你好", "在吗", "哈哈"]  # 闲聊
    }

    @classmethod
    def classify(cls, msg: str) -> str:
        msg_lower = msg.lower()
        for intent, keywords in cls.INTENT_MAP.items():
            for kw in keywords:
                if kw in msg_lower:
                    return intent
        return "CHAT"
```

### 📄 修复后代码：`backend/app/core/strategy.py`（接收 intent）
```python
from app.core.intent import IntentClassifier

class StrategyRouter:
    @staticmethod
    def route(state: dict, intent: str) -> str:
        # 优先级1：垃圾拦截
        if intent == "SPAM":
            return "IGNORE_STRATEGY"
        
        # 优先级2：高意向交易
        if intent in ["PRICE", "BUY"] and state.get("score", 0) > 50:
            return "CLOSER_STRATEGY"
        
        # 优先级3：普通咨询/对比
        if intent in ["COMPARE", "AFTERSALE"]:
            return "CONSULTANT_STRATEGY"
        
        # 默认：社交破冰
        return "FRIEND_STRATEGY"
```

### 📄 修复后代码：`backend/app/core/persona.py`（倒 U 型 pressure）
```python
class Persona:
    @staticmethod
    def build(state: dict, strategy: str) -> dict:
        score = state.get("score", 0)
        
        # 倒 U 型 pressure：40-70 施压最大，80 以上降低
        if score < 40:
            pressure = 0.2
        elif 40 <= score <= 70:
            pressure = 0.6 + (score - 40) / 30 * 0.3  # 0.6 -> 0.9
        else:
            pressure = 0.9 - (score - 70) / 30 * 0.5  # 0.9 -> 0.4
        
        return {
            "strategy": strategy,
            "tone": "professional" if score > 50 else "friendly",
            "pressure": round(min(1, max(0, pressure)), 2),
            "max_length": 150 if strategy == "FRIEND_STRATEGY" else 300,
            "use_case": strategy == "CLOSER_STRATEGY"
        }
```

### 📄 修复后代码：`backend/app/core/ai.py`（成本控制 + 异步）
```python
import asyncio
from app.core.intent import IntentClassifier
from app.services.knowledge_service import KnowledgeService  # 知识库

class AI:
    @staticmethod
    async def run_async(msg: str, state: dict, persona: dict, intent: str) -> str:
        score = state.get("score", 0)

        # --- 成本控制门 ---
        # 1. SPAM/CHAT 低分：直接模板回复，不走 LLM
        if intent == "SPAM":
            return "抱歉，这个我帮不上忙。"
        if intent == "CHAT" and score < 30:
            return "哈哈，您说笑了，有什么我能帮您的吗？"
        
        # 2. PRICE/FAQ：优先走知识库（RAG）
        if intent in ["PRICE", "COMPARE"]:
            kb_result = KnowledgeService.search(msg, top_k=1)
            if kb_result and kb_result[0].get("score", 0) > 0.7:
                return kb_result[0]["content"]
        
        # 3. 只有高价值（score > 60）或复杂意图才调用 LLM
        if score < 60 and intent not in ["AFTERSALE", "COMPARE"]:
            # 模板回复（成本降低 90%）
            templates = {
                "PRICE": "具体价格我私信发给您，您方便的话可以留个联系方式。",
                "BUY": "购买流程我发给您，您看哪个渠道方便？",
            }
            return templates.get(intent, "我帮您查一下，稍后回复您。")

        # 4. 高价值：调用真实 LLM（异步 + 超时）
        try:
            prompt = AI._build_prompt(msg, state, persona)
            # 模拟 LLM 调用（替换为 openai.ChatCompletion.acreate）
            await asyncio.sleep(0.5)  # 模拟网络延迟
            raw = f"【LLM模拟】根据策略 {persona['strategy']}，回复：{msg[:20]}..."
            return raw
        except Exception:
            # LLM 失败降级
            return "我稍后帮你确认一下这个问题。"

    @staticmethod
    def _build_prompt(msg: str, state: dict, persona: dict) -> str:
        return f"""
【人设】{persona['tone']}，施压力度：{persona['pressure']}
【客户状态】分数：{state['score']}，阶段：{state['stage']}
【策略】{persona['strategy']}
【消息】{msg}
请生成回复。
"""
```

---

## 📦 修复包 4：爆量处理（前置计数器 + 独立排序队列）（版块四）

### 🔴 问题诊断
- 爆量判断在 Pipeline 内部，太晚。
- 算分与处理耦合，无法独立扩容。

### ✅ 修复方案
1. Gateway 层前置 **滑动窗口计数器**（Redis INCR + EXPIRE）。
2. 触发阈值后，后续消息直接入 `burst:queue`（List），不经过 Pipeline。
3. 独立的 **Scoring Worker** 从 BurstQueue 拉取，算分后写入 **Redis ZSET**（按 priority 排序）。
4. 业务 Worker 从 ZSET 按分数拉取处理。

### 📄 新增：`backend/app/middleware/burst_gateway.py`
```python
from fastapi import Request
from app.utils.redis_client import redis_client

BURST_THRESHOLD = 100  # 5分钟100条
BURST_WINDOW = 300     # 5秒? 单位秒

async def burst_middleware(request: Request, call_next):
    # 仅对 /webhook 路径生效
    if request.url.path.startswith("/webhook"):
        payload = await request.json()
        video_id = payload.get("post_id") or payload.get("video_id")
        if video_id:
            key = f"burst:counter:{video_id}"
            count = redis_client.incr(key)
            if count == 1:
                redis_client.expire(key, BURST_WINDOW)
            
            if count > BURST_THRESHOLD:
                # 爆量模式：直接入 BurstQueue，不经过 Pipeline
                redis_client.lpush("burst:queue", json.dumps(payload))
                return {"code": 0, "msg": "burst_mode_accepted"}
    
    return await call_next(request)
```

### 📄 新增：`backend/app/worker/scoring_worker.py`（独立算分）
```python
import json
import time
from app.utils.redis_client import redis_client
from app.core.priority import PriorityEngine
from app.core.intent import IntentClassifier

def scoring_worker():
    while True:
        # 从 BurstQueue 批量拉取
        items = redis_client.rpop("burst:queue", count=10)
        if not items:
            time.sleep(0.1)
            continue
        
        for item_str in items:
            event = json.loads(item_str)
            user = event.get("user") or event.get("user_id")
            content = event.get("content")
            
            # 轻量算分（不依赖完整状态）
            intent = IntentClassifier.classify(content)
            value_score = 90 if intent in ["PRICE", "BUY"] else 50 if intent == "COMPARE" else 10
            customer_score = 50  # 默认，爆量时快速算分
            priority = PriorityEngine.calculate(value_score, customer_score, 20, 10)
            
            # 写入 ZSET（分数越高越优先）
            redis_client.zadd("burst:priority_queue", {json.dumps(event): priority})
```

### 📄 修改：`backend/app/worker/event_consumer.py`（拉取 ZSET 高优处理）
```python
def consume_priority():
    while True:
        # 从 ZSET 拉取最高分（倒序）
        items = redis_client.zrevrange("burst:priority_queue", 0, 0)
        if not items:
            time.sleep(0.1)
            continue
        event_str = items[0]
        # 移除已取出的任务（原子）
        redis_client.zrem("burst:priority_queue", event_str)
        event = json.loads(event_str)
        # 进入正常 Pipeline
        asyncio.run(pipeline(Event(**event)))
```

ALTER TABLE conversations ADD COLUMN last_message_time TIMESTAMP;
CREATE INDEX idx_conversations_last_time ON conversations(last_message_time DESC);

-- 2. tasks 表增加锁字段
ALTER TABLE tasks ADD COLUMN locked_by VARCHAR(64);
ALTER TABLE tasks ADD COLUMN locked_at TIMESTAMP;
CREATE INDEX idx_tasks_status_execute_lock ON tasks(status, execute_at ASC) WHERE locked_by IS NULL;

-- 3. comments 表去掉派生的 priority，改存特征

ALTER TABLE comments ADD COLUMN intent_score INTEGER;
ALTER TABLE comments ADD COLUMN value_score INTEGER;

## 📦 修复包 6：微信接入层（Session 迁移至 Redis + 429 降速）（版块六）

### 🔴 问题诊断
- Session 存内存，重启即丢。
- 微信限流（429）无反馈机制。

### ✅ 修复方案
1. Session 全部存 Redis Hash。
2. Adapter 检测到 429 时，设置 Account 状态为 `COOLDOWN`，并延迟 60 秒。

### 📄 修复后代码：`backend/app/adapters/clawbot/session.py`
```python
import json
import time
from app.utils.redis_client import redis_client

class SessionManager:
    @staticmethod
    def _key(account_id: str) -> str:
        return f"wechat:session:{account_id}"
    
    @staticmethod
    def save(account_id: str, token: str, status: str = "active"):
        data = {
            "token": token,
            "status": status,
            "last_heartbeat": time.time(),
            "updated_at": time.time()
        }
        redis_client.hset(SessionManager._key(account_id), mapping=data)
        redis_client.expire(SessionManager._key(account_id), 86400 * 7)  # 7天
    
    @staticmethod
    def get(account_id: str) -> dict:
        data = redis_client.hgetall(SessionManager._key(account_id))
        if data:
            return {k.decode(): v.decode() if isinstance(v, bytes) else v for k, v in data.items()}
        return {}
    
    @staticmethod
    def update_heartbeat(account_id: str):
        redis_client.hset(SessionManager._key(account_id), "last_heartbeat", time.time())
    
    @staticmethod
    def set_cooldown(account_id: str, duration: int = 60):
        redis_client.hset(SessionManager._key(account_id), "status", "cooldown")
        redis_client.expire(SessionManager._key(account_id), duration)
```

### 📄 修复后代码：`backend/app/adapters/wechat.py`（429 处理）
```python
import time
from app.adapters.base import BaseAdapter
from app.adapters.clawbot.session import SessionManager
from app.utils.logger import logger

class WeChatAdapter(BaseAdapter):
    def __init__(self, api_url: str = None):
        self.api_url = api_url or "http://clawbot.local"
    
    def send(self, user: str, msg: str) -> dict:
        # 1. 检查该账号是否在 cooldown
        # 实际应动态获取 account_id，此处简化
        account_id = "wx_default"
        session = SessionManager.get(account_id)
        if session.get("status") == "cooldown":
            logger.warning(f"Account {account_id} in cooldown, dropping message")
            return {"code": 429, "msg": "account cooldown"}
        
        # 2. 发送（模拟）
        # resp = requests.post(...)
        # 模拟 429 触发
        import random
        if random.random() < 0.05:  # 5% 概率模拟限流
            SessionManager.set_cooldown(account_id, 60)
            logger.error(f"Account {account_id} rate limited, cooldown 60s")
            return {"code": 429, "msg": "rate limited"}
        
        print(f"[WX:{account_id}] to {user}: {msg}")
        return {"code": 0, "msg": "sent"}
```

## 📦 修复包 7：前端实时通信（WS 重连 + 状态恢复 + 防抖）（版块七）

### 🔴 问题诊断
- WebSocket 断线状态丢失。
- AI 输入补全无防抖，请求爆炸。
- 动画状态与数据源延迟不一致。

### ✅ 修复方案
1. `useWebSocket` Hook 自动重连（指数退避）+ 发送 `SYNC` 回补历史。
2. 输入补全防抖 500ms。
3. 使用乐观 UI + 平滑插值。

### 📄 修复后代码：`frontend/src/hooks/useWebSocket.ts`
```typescript
import { useEffect, useRef, useState } from 'react';

type WSMessage = { type: string; payload: any };

export function useWebSocket(url: string) {
  const [isConnected, setIsConnected] = useState(false);
  const [lastMessage, setLastMessage] = useState<WSMessage | null>(null);
  const wsRef = useRef<WebSocket | null>(null);
  const reconnectAttempts = useRef(0);
  const reconnectTimeoutRef = useRef<NodeJS.Timeout>();

  const connect = () => {
    if (wsRef.current?.readyState === WebSocket.OPEN) return;
    
    const ws = new WebSocket(url);
    wsRef.current = ws;

    ws.onopen = () => {
      setIsConnected(true);
      reconnectAttempts.current = 0;
      // 连接成功后发送 SYNC 请求，恢复离线消息
      ws.send(JSON.stringify({ type: 'SYNC', last_seq: localStorage.getItem('ws_last_seq') || '0' }));
    };

    ws.onmessage = (event) => {
      const data = JSON.parse(event.data);
      // 更新本地 seq
      if (data.seq) localStorage.setItem('ws_last_seq', data.seq);
      setLastMessage(data);
    };

    ws.onclose = () => {
      setIsConnected(false);
      // 指数退避重连
      const delay = Math.min(1000 * Math.pow(2, reconnectAttempts.current), 30000);
      reconnectAttempts.current++;
      reconnectTimeoutRef.current = setTimeout(connect, delay);
    };

    ws.onerror = (error) => {
      console.error('WebSocket error:', error);
      ws.close();
    };
  };

  const send = (data: any) => {
    if (wsRef.current?.readyState === WebSocket.OPEN) {
      wsRef.current.send(JSON.stringify(data));
    } else {
      console.warn('WebSocket not open, message queued');
      // 可加入离线队列
    }
  };

  useEffect(() => {
    connect();
    return () => {
      if (reconnectTimeoutRef.current) clearTimeout(reconnectTimeoutRef.current);
      wsRef.current?.close();
    };
  }, [url]);

  return { isConnected, lastMessage, send };
}
```

### 📄 修复后代码：`frontend/src/modules/chat/ChatInput.tsx`（防抖 + 乐观补全）
```tsx
import { useState, useCallback, useRef } from 'react';
import { debounce } from 'lodash'; // 需安装 lodash

export function ChatInput({ onSend, onSuggestion }: { onSend: (msg: string) => void, onSuggestion?: (msg: string) => void }) {
  const [value, setValue] = useState('');
  
  // 防抖 500ms，仅当客户为 HOT 时触发（由父组件控制）
  const debouncedSuggestion = useCallback(
    debounce((text: string) => {
      if (text.length > 2 && onSuggestion) {
        onSuggestion(text);
      }
    }, 500),
    [onSuggestion]
  );

  const handleChange = (e: React.ChangeEvent<HTMLInputElement>) => {
    const val = e.target.value;
    setValue(val);
    debouncedSuggestion(val);
  };

  const handleSend = () => {
    if (value.trim()) {
      onSend(value);
      setValue('');
    }
  };

  return (
    <div className="flex gap-2 p-3 border-t border-white/10">
      <input
        className="flex-1 bg-white/5 rounded-xl px-4 py-2 text-sm outline-none focus:ring-1 focus:ring-blue-500"
        placeholder="输入消息... (AI实时补全)"
        value={value}
        onChange={handleChange}
        onKeyDown={(e) => e.key === 'Enter' && handleSend()}
      />
      <button onClick={handleSend} className="px-4 py-2 bg-blue-500 rounded-xl text-sm font-medium">
        发送
      </button>
    </div>
  );
}
```

### 📄 文件 1：`backend/app/core/vector/embedding.py`
```python
import os
import asyncio
from typing import List, Optional
import openai
from app.utils.logger import logger

class EmbeddingProvider:
    """Embedding 生成器，支持 OpenAI / 本地模型"""
    
    def __init__(self, provider: str = "openai", model: str = None):
        self.provider = provider
        self.model = model or os.getenv("EMBEDDING_MODEL", "text-embedding-3-small")
        self.dimension = 1536  # text-embedding-3-small 维度
        
        if provider == "openai":
            self.client = openai.AsyncOpenAI(
                api_key=os.getenv("OPENAI_API_KEY", ""),
                base_url=os.getenv("OPENAI_BASE_URL", "https://api.openai.com/v1")
            )
        else:
            # 本地模型占位（可替换为 sentence-transformers）
            self.client = None
    
    async def embed(self, texts: List[str]) -> List[List[float]]:
        """批量生成向量"""
        if not texts:
            return []
        
        if self.provider == "openai":
            try:
                response = await self.client.embeddings.create(
                    model=self.model,
                    input=texts,
                    encoding_format="float"
                )
                return [item.embedding for item in response.data]
            except Exception as e:
                logger.error(f"Embedding error: {e}")
                raise
        
        # 本地模型占位
        logger.warning("Local embedding not implemented, returning random vectors")
        import random
        return [[random.random() for _ in range(self.dimension)] for _ in texts]
    
    async def embed_one(self, text: str) -> List[float]:
        """单个文本向量化"""
        result = await self.embed([text])
        return result[0] if result else []
    
    def get_dimension(self) -> int:
        return self.dimension

# 全局单例
_embedding_provider = None

def get_embedding_provider() -> EmbeddingProvider:
    global _embedding_provider
    if _embedding_provider is None:
        _embedding_provider = EmbeddingProvider()
    return _embedding_provider
```

### 📄 文件 2：`backend/app/core/vector/client.py`
```python
import os
from typing import Optional
from qdrant_client import QdrantClient
from qdrant_client.http import models
from app.utils.logger import logger

class QdrantClientWrapper:
    """Qdrant 客户端封装（单例 + 连接管理）"""
    
    _instance = None
    
    def __new__(cls):
        if cls._instance is None:
            cls._instance = super().__new__(cls)
            cls._instance._init_client()
        return cls._instance
    
    def _init_client(self):
        host = os.getenv("QDRANT_HOST", "localhost")
        port = int(os.getenv("QDRANT_PORT", 6333))
        api_key = os.getenv("QDRANT_API_KEY", None)
        
        logger.info(f"Connecting to Qdrant at {host}:{port}")
        
        if api_key:
            self.client = QdrantClient(
                host=host,
                port=port,
                api_key=api_key,
                timeout=30
            )
        else:
            self.client = QdrantClient(
                host=host,
                port=port,
                timeout=30
            )
        
        # 测试连接
        try:
            self.client.get_collections()
            logger.info("Qdrant connected successfully")
        except Exception as e:
            logger.error(f"Qdrant connection failed: {e}")
            raise
    
    def get_client(self) -> QdrantClient:
        return self.client
    
    def health_check(self) -> bool:
        try:
            self.client.get_collections()
            return True
        except:
            return False

def get_qdrant_client() -> QdrantClient:
    return QdrantClientWrapper().get_client()
```

### 📄 文件 3：`backend/app/core/vector/collections.py`
```python
from typing import Optional
from qdrant_client.http import models
from app.core.vector.client import get_qdrant_client
from app.core.vector.embedding import get_embedding_provider
from app.utils.logger import logger

class CollectionManager:
    """知识库集合管理（5 个集合对应 5 层知识库）"""
    
    # 知识库类型 -> 集合名
    COLLECTIONS = {
        "product": "knowledge_product",
        "faq": "knowledge_faq",
        "case": "knowledge_case",
        "objection": "knowledge_objection",
        "memory": "knowledge_memory"
    }
    
    @classmethod
    def _get_collection_name(cls, kb_type: str) -> str:
        return cls.COLLECTIONS.get(kb_type, f"knowledge_{kb_type}")
    
    @classmethod
    def ensure_collections(cls):
        """确保所有集合存在，不存在则创建"""
        client = get_qdrant_client()
        embedding_provider = get_embedding_provider()
        dimension = embedding_provider.get_dimension()
        
        existing = [c.name for c in client.get_collections().collections]
        
        for kb_type, col_name in cls.COLLECTIONS.items():
            if col_name not in existing:
                logger.info(f"Creating collection: {col_name}")
                client.create_collection(
                    collection_name=col_name,
                    vectors_config=models.VectorParams(
                        size=dimension,
                        distance=models.Distance.COSINE
                    ),
                    # 索引配置（加速过滤）
                    optimizers_config=models.OptimizersConfigDiff(
                        indexing_threshold=10000
                    ),
                    # 为 tenant_id 和 customer_id 建 payload 索引
                    schema=models.Schema(
                        indexed_payload={
                            "tenant_id": models.PayloadIndexParams(
                                index_type=models.PayloadIndexType.KEYWORD
                            ),
                            "customer_id": models.PayloadIndexParams(
                                index_type=models.PayloadIndexType.KEYWORD
                            ),
                            "type": models.PayloadIndexParams(
                                index_type=models.PayloadIndexType.KEYWORD
                            )
                        }
                    )
                )
            else:
                logger.debug(f"Collection {col_name} already exists")
    
    @classmethod
    def delete_collection(cls, kb_type: str):
        """删除指定集合（慎用）"""
        client = get_qdrant_client()
        col_name = cls._get_collection_name(kb_type)
        try:
            client.delete_collection(collection_name=col_name)
            logger.warning(f"Deleted collection: {col_name}")
        except Exception as e:
            logger.error(f"Failed to delete {col_name}: {e}")
    
    @classmethod
    def get_collection_name(cls, kb_type: str) -> str:
        return cls._get_collection_name(kb_type)
```

### 📄 文件 4：`backend/app/core/vector/store.py`
```python
import uuid
from typing import List, Dict, Any, Optional
from qdrant_client.http import models
from app.core.vector.client import get_qdrant_client
from app.core.vector.embedding import get_embedding_provider
from app.core.vector.collections import CollectionManager
from app.utils.logger import logger

class KnowledgeStore:
    """知识文档存储（增删改）"""
    
    @staticmethod
    async def upsert(
        kb_type: str,
        documents: List[Dict[str, Any]],
        tenant_id: Optional[str] = None,
        customer_id: Optional[str] = None
    ) -> int:
        """
        批量插入/更新知识文档
        
        documents: [
            {
                "id": "doc_001",          # 可选，不传则自动生成
                "content": "宝马X5价格65万",
                "metadata": {             # 附加字段
                    "category": "配置",
                    "source": "官网"
                }
            }
        ]
        """
        if not documents:
            return 0
        
        client = get_qdrant_client()
        embedding_provider = get_embedding_provider()
        col_name = CollectionManager.get_collection_name(kb_type)
        
        # 提取文本列表
        texts = [doc["content"] for doc in documents]
        
        # 批量生成向量
        vectors = await embedding_provider.embed(texts)
        
        # 构造 points
        points = []
        for i, doc in enumerate(documents):
            doc_id = doc.get("id") or str(uuid.uuid4())
            payload = {
                "content": doc["content"],
                "type": kb_type,
                "metadata": doc.get("metadata", {}),
                "created_at": doc.get("created_at", None)
            }
            if tenant_id:
                payload["tenant_id"] = tenant_id
            if customer_id:
                payload["customer_id"] = customer_id
            
            points.append(
                models.PointStruct(
                    id=doc_id,
                    vector=vectors[i],
                    payload=payload
                )
            )
        
        # 批量写入
        try:
            client.upsert(
                collection_name=col_name,
                points=points,
                wait=True
            )
            logger.info(f"Upserted {len(points)} docs to {col_name}")
            return len(points)
        except Exception as e:
            logger.error(f"Upsert failed: {e}")
            raise
    
    @staticmethod
    def delete(
        kb_type: str,
        doc_ids: List[str],
        tenant_id: Optional[str] = None
    ) -> int:
        """删除指定文档"""
        if not doc_ids:
            return 0
        
        client = get_qdrant_client()
        col_name = CollectionManager.get_collection_name(kb_type)
        
        # 构建过滤条件（必带 tenant_id 防止误删）
        filter_conditions = [models.FieldCondition(key="id", match=models.MatchValue(value=id)) for id in doc_ids]
        if tenant_id:
            filter_conditions.append(
                models.FieldCondition(key="tenant_id", match=models.MatchValue(value=tenant_id))
            )
        
        filter_obj = models.Filter(must=filter_conditions)
        
        try:
            result = client.delete(
                collection_name=col_name,
                points_selector=models.FilterSelector(filter=filter_obj)
            )
            logger.info(f"Deleted {len(doc_ids)} docs from {col_name}")
            return len(doc_ids)
        except Exception as e:
            logger.error(f"Delete failed: {e}")
            raise
    
    @staticmethod
    def clear_collection(kb_type: str, tenant_id: Optional[str] = None):
        """清空集合（按租户隔离）"""
        client = get_qdrant_client()
        col_name = CollectionManager.get_collection_name(kb_type)
        
        if tenant_id:
            # 只删除该租户的数据
            filter_obj = models.Filter(
                must=[models.FieldCondition(key="tenant_id", match=models.MatchValue(value=tenant_id))]
            )
            client.delete(
                collection_name=col_name,
                points_selector=models.FilterSelector(filter=filter_obj)
            )
        else:
            # 删除整个集合（慎用）
            client.delete_collection(collection_name=col_name)
            CollectionManager.ensure_collections()  # 重建
```

### 📄 文件 5：`backend/app/core/vector/retrieval.py`
```python
from typing import List, Dict, Any, Optional
from qdrant_client.http import models
from app.core.vector.client import get_qdrant_client
from app.core.vector.embedding import get_embedding_provider
from app.core.vector.collections import CollectionManager
from app.utils.logger import logger

class KnowledgeRetrieval:
    """知识检索（含过滤 + 重排序）"""
    
    @staticmethod
    async def search(
        query: str,
        kb_type: str,
        tenant_id: Optional[str] = None,
        customer_id: Optional[str] = None,
        top_k: int = 5,
        score_threshold: float = 0.6
    ) -> List[Dict[str, Any]]:
        """
        检索知识库
        
        Args:
            query: 查询文本
            kb_type: 知识库类型 (product/faq/case/objection/memory)
            tenant_id: 租户过滤
            customer_id: 客户过滤
            top_k: 返回数量
            score_threshold: 相似度阈值
        """
        if not query:
            return []
        
        client = get_qdrant_client()
        embedding_provider = get_embedding_provider()
        col_name = CollectionManager.get_collection_name(kb_type)
        
        # 1. 生成查询向量
        query_vector = await embedding_provider.embed_one(query)
        
        # 2. 构建过滤条件
        must_conditions = []
        if tenant_id:
            must_conditions.append(
                models.FieldCondition(key="tenant_id", match=models.MatchValue(value=tenant_id))
            )
        if customer_id:
            must_conditions.append(
                models.FieldCondition(key="customer_id", match=models.MatchValue(value=customer_id))
            )
        
        filter_obj = models.Filter(must=must_conditions) if must_conditions else None
        
        # 3. 执行检索
        try:
            results = client.search(
                collection_name=col_name,
                query_vector=query_vector,
                query_filter=filter_obj,
                limit=top_k,
                with_payload=True
            )
        except Exception as e:
            logger.error(f"Search failed: {e}")
            return []
        
        # 4. 转换结果 + 阈值过滤
        output = []
        for hit in results:
            if hit.score < score_threshold:
                continue
            output.append({
                "id": hit.id,
                "content": hit.payload.get("content", ""),
                "score": round(hit.score, 4),
                "metadata": hit.payload.get("metadata", {}),
                "type": hit.payload.get("type", kb_type)
            })
        
        return output
    
    @staticmethod
    async def multi_search(
        query: str,
        kb_types: List[str],
        tenant_id: Optional[str] = None,
        top_k_per_type: int = 2
    ) -> List[Dict[str, Any]]:
        """多知识库联合检索（用于综合回答）"""
        all_results = []
        
        for kb_type in kb_types:
            results = await KnowledgeRetrieval.search(
                query=query,
                kb_type=kb_type,
                tenant_id=tenant_id,
                top_k=top_k_per_type,
                score_threshold=0.5
            )
            all_results.extend(results)
        
        # 按分数排序
        all_results.sort(key=lambda x: x["score"], reverse=True)
        return all_results
    
    @staticmethod
    def rerank(
        results: List[Dict[str, Any]],
        max_results: int = 5
    ) -> List[Dict[str, Any]]:
        """简单重排序（后续可替换为 Cross-Encoder）"""
        # 当前仅按分数排序 + 去重
        seen_contents = set()
        deduped = []
        for r in results:
            content = r["content"][:100]  # 取前100字符去重
            if content not in seen_contents:
                seen_contents.add(content)
                deduped.append(r)
        return deduped[:max_results]
```

### 📄 文件 6：`backend/app/services/knowledge_service.py`（完整实现）
```python
from typing import List, Dict, Any, Optional
from app.core.vector.embedding import get_embedding_provider
from app.core.vector.client import get_qdrant_client
from app.core.vector.collections import CollectionManager
from app.core.vector.store import KnowledgeStore
from app.core.vector.retrieval import KnowledgeRetrieval
from app.utils.logger import logger

class KnowledgeService:
    """知识库统一服务接口（供 AI / 业务层调用）"""
    
    @staticmethod
    async def ensure_ready():
        """启动时初始化：确保集合存在"""
        CollectionManager.ensure_collections()
    
    # ===== 写入接口 =====
    
    @staticmethod
    async def add_product(product: dict, tenant_id: str):
        """添加产品知识"""
        return await KnowledgeStore.upsert(
            kb_type="product",
            documents=[{
                "content": f"{product['name']}: {product.get('description', '')} 价格:{product.get('price', '')}",
                "metadata": product
            }],
            tenant_id=tenant_id
        )
    
    @staticmethod
    async def add_faq(faq: dict, tenant_id: str):
        """添加 FAQ"""
        return await KnowledgeStore.upsert(
            kb_type="faq",
            documents=[{
                "content": f"Q: {faq['question']}\nA: {faq['answer']}",
                "metadata": faq
            }],
            tenant_id=tenant_id
        )
    
    @staticmethod
    async def add_case(case: dict, tenant_id: str):
        """添加成交案例"""
        return await KnowledgeStore.upsert(
            kb_type="case",
            documents=[{
                "content": f"{case['title']}: {case.get('description', '')} 结果:{case.get('result', '成交')}",
                "metadata": case
            }],
            tenant_id=tenant_id
        )
    
    @staticmethod
    async def add_objection(objection: dict, tenant_id: str):
        """添加异议处理"""
        return await KnowledgeStore.upsert(
            kb_type="objection",
            documents=[{
                "content": f"客户说: {objection['objection']}\n应对: {objection['response']}",
                "metadata": objection
            }],
            tenant_id=tenant_id
        )
    
    @staticmethod
    async def add_memory(customer_id: str, memory: dict, tenant_id: str):
        """添加客户记忆（长期记忆）"""
        return await KnowledgeStore.upsert(
            kb_type="memory",
            documents=[{
                "content": f"{memory['type']}: {memory['content']}",
                "metadata": memory
            }],
            tenant_id=tenant_id,
            customer_id=customer_id
        )
    
    # ===== 检索接口 =====
    
    @staticmethod
    async def search(
        query: str,
        kb_type: str = "faq",
        tenant_id: Optional[str] = None,
        customer_id: Optional[str] = None,
        top_k: int = 5
    ) -> List[Dict[str, Any]]:
        """单知识库检索"""
        return await KnowledgeRetrieval.search(query, kb_type, tenant_id, customer_id, top_k)
    
    @staticmethod
    async def search_all(
        query: str,
        tenant_id: Optional[str] = None,
        customer_id: Optional[str] = None
    ) -> List[Dict[str, Any]]:
        """全知识库联合检索"""
        return await KnowledgeRetrieval.multi_search(
            query=query,
            kb_types=["product", "faq", "case", "objection", "memory"],
            tenant_id=tenant_id,
            top_k_per_type=2
        )
    
    @staticmethod
    async def search_by_intent(
        query: str,
        intent: str,
        tenant_id: Optional[str] = None,
        customer_id: Optional[str] = None
    ) -> List[Dict[str, Any]]:
        """根据意图精准检索"""
        intent_kb_map = {
            "PRICE": ["product", "faq"],
            "COMPARE": ["product", "case"],
            "BUY": ["product", "case"],
            "AFTERSALE": ["faq"],
            "CHAT": ["faq", "case"],
        }
        kb_types = intent_kb_map.get(intent, ["faq"])
        
        return await KnowledgeRetrieval.multi_search(
            query=query,
            kb_types=kb_types,
            tenant_id=tenant_id,
            customer_id=customer_id,
            top_k_per_type=2
        )
    
    # ===== 管理接口 =====
    
    @staticmethod
    def clear_tenant(tenant_id: str, kb_type: Optional[str] = None):
        """清空租户数据"""
        if kb_type:
            KnowledgeStore.clear_collection(kb_type, tenant_id)
        else:
            for col in CollectionManager.COLLECTIONS.keys():
                KnowledgeStore.clear_collection(col, tenant_id)
    
    @staticmethod
    def health_check() -> dict:
        """检查 Qdrant 和 Embedding 服务状态"""
        from app.core.vector.client import get_qdrant_client
        status = {
            "qdrant": "healthy",
            "embedding": "healthy"
        }
        try:
            get_qdrant_client().get_collections()
        except:
            status["qdrant"] = "unhealthy"
        return status
```

现在 **P0-2 已搞定**。我们继续攻克 **P0-3：多租户（Tenant）隔离中间件**——这是数据安全的底线。您说“继续”，我立刻输出完整的 Tenant Resolver + DB/Redis 自动过滤代码。
收到。我们接着攻克 **P0-3：多租户（Tenant）隔离中间件**。

这是 **数据安全的底线**。没有它，租户 A 可以查到租户 B 的客户、消息、知识库，系统上线即违法（违反 GDPR / 个人信息保护法）。

---

## ✅ 搞定 P0-3：多租户隔离中间件（生产级强制隔离）

我将采用 **“三层隔离”** 策略：
1. **JWT 层**：登录时签发包含 `tenant_id` 的 Token。
2. **依赖注入层**：每个 API 路由通过 `Depends(get_current_tenant)` 强制注入租户上下文。
3. **存储层**：
   - **PostgreSQL**：所有查询自动附加 `tenant_id = :current_tenant` 过滤（使用 SQLAlchemy 的 `Query` 扩展）。
   - **Redis**：Key 前缀改为 `waos:{tenant_id}:...`。
   - **Qdrant**：检索时自动添加 `tenant_id` 过滤器。

---

### 📄 文件 1：`backend/app/core/context.py`（异步安全的租户上下文）
```python
from contextvars import ContextVar
from typing import Optional
from uuid import UUID

# 定义上下文变量（异步安全，自动隔离）
_tenant_id: ContextVar[Optional[UUID]] = ContextVar('tenant_id', default=None)
_customer_id: ContextVar[Optional[UUID]] = ContextVar('customer_id', default=None)
_user_id: ContextVar[Optional[UUID]] = ContextVar('user_id', default=None)

# ===== Tenant =====
def set_tenant_id(tenant_id: UUID) -> None:
    """设置当前请求的租户ID（在中间件/依赖中调用）"""
    _tenant_id.set(tenant_id)

def get_tenant_id() -> Optional[UUID]:
    """获取当前请求的租户ID"""
    return _tenant_id.get()

def require_tenant_id() -> UUID:
    """强制获取租户ID，如果没有则抛出异常"""
    tenant_id = _tenant_id.get()
    if tenant_id is None:
        raise RuntimeError("Tenant context not set")
    return tenant_id

# ===== Customer（可选，用于客户级隔离） =====
def set_customer_id(customer_id: Optional[UUID]) -> None:
    _customer_id.set(customer_id)

def get_customer_id() -> Optional[UUID]:
    return _customer_id.get()

# ===== User =====
def set_user_id(user_id: Optional[UUID]) -> None:
    _user_id.set(user_id)

def get_user_id() -> Optional[UUID]:
    return _user_id.get()

# ===== 便捷工具 =====
def get_tenant_prefix() -> str:
    """用于 Redis Key 前缀"""
    tenant_id = get_tenant_id()
    return f"waos:{tenant_id}" if tenant_id else "waos:global"

def get_tenant_key(suffix: str) -> str:
    """生成带租户前缀的 Redis Key"""
    return f"{get_tenant_prefix()}:{suffix}"
```

### 📄 文件 2：`backend/app/dependencies/auth.py`（JWT 解析 + 租户提取）
```python
import os
import jwt
from datetime import datetime, timedelta
from typing import Optional
from fastapi import Depends, HTTPException, status
from fastapi.security import HTTPBearer, HTTPAuthorizationCredentials
from uuid import UUID

from app.core.context import set_tenant_id, set_user_id, get_tenant_id
from app.models.user import User  # SQLAlchemy Model
from app.db.session import SessionLocal
from app.utils.logger import logger

# JWT 配置
JWT_SECRET = os.getenv("JWT_SECRET", "waos-super-secret-change-me")
JWT_ALGORITHM = os.getenv("JWT_ALGORITHM", "HS256")
JWT_EXPIRE_MINUTES = int(os.getenv("JWT_EXPIRE_MINUTES", 1440))  # 24小时

security = HTTPBearer()

def create_access_token(user_id: UUID, tenant_id: UUID) -> str:
    """签发 JWT Token（包含 tenant_id）"""
    payload = {
        "sub": str(user_id),
        "tenant": str(tenant_id),
        "exp": datetime.utcnow() + timedelta(minutes=JWT_EXPIRE_MINUTES),
        "iat": datetime.utcnow()
    }
    return jwt.encode(payload, JWT_SECRET, algorithm=JWT_ALGORITHM)

def decode_token(token: str) -> dict:
    """解码 JWT Token"""
    try:
        payload = jwt.decode(token, JWT_SECRET, algorithms=[JWT_ALGORITHM])
        return payload
    except jwt.ExpiredSignatureError:
        raise HTTPException(status_code=401, detail="Token expired")
    except jwt.InvalidTokenError:
        raise HTTPException(status_code=401, detail="Invalid token")

async def get_current_tenant(
    credentials: HTTPAuthorizationCredentials = Depends(security)
) -> UUID:
    """
    依赖注入：解析 JWT，提取 tenant_id 并设置上下文
    所有需要租户隔离的路由都必须依赖此函数
    """
    token = credentials.credentials
    payload = decode_token(token)
    
    tenant_id_str = payload.get("tenant")
    user_id_str = payload.get("sub")
    
    if not tenant_id_str:
        raise HTTPException(status_code=403, detail="Missing tenant_id in token")
    
    try:
        tenant_id = UUID(tenant_id_str)
        user_id = UUID(user_id_str) if user_id_str else None
    except ValueError:
        raise HTTPException(status_code=403, detail="Invalid tenant_id format")
    
    # 设置上下文（后续所有模块通过 get_tenant_id() 获取）
    set_tenant_id(tenant_id)
    if user_id:
        set_user_id(user_id)
    
    # 可选：验证租户是否存在（从 DB 查询）
    # db = SessionLocal()
    # try:
    #     tenant = db.query(Tenant).filter(Tenant.id == tenant_id).first()
    #     if not tenant:
    #         raise HTTPException(status_code=403, detail="Tenant not found")
    # finally:
    #     db.close()
    
    logger.info(f"Tenant context set: {tenant_id}, user: {user_id}")
    return tenant_id

# 便捷别名（用于路由中标注返回类型）
GetCurrentTenant = get_current_tenant
```

### 📄 文件 3：`backend/app/repositories/base.py`（自动租户过滤的 Repository 基类）
```python
from typing import Optional, Any, List, Type, Dict
from uuid import UUID
from sqlalchemy.orm import Session, Query
from sqlalchemy import func

from app.core.context import get_tenant_id, require_tenant_id
from app.db.session import SessionLocal
from app.utils.logger import logger

class TenantAwareRepository:
    """
    租户感知 Repository 基类
    所有 Repository 继承此类后，默认所有查询自动附加 tenant_id 过滤
    """
    
    model: Any = None  # 子类必须指定 Model 类
    
    def __init__(self, db: Optional[Session] = None):
        self.db = db or SessionLocal()
        self._tenant_id = None
    
    @property
    def tenant_id(self) -> UUID:
        """从上下文获取租户ID，如果不存在则报错（防止数据泄露）"""
        if self._tenant_id is None:
            self._tenant_id = get_tenant_id()
        if self._tenant_id is None:
            raise RuntimeError("Tenant context not set, call with_tenant() first")
        return self._tenant_id
    
    def with_tenant(self, tenant_id: UUID):
        """手动指定租户（用于系统内部任务）"""
        self._tenant_id = tenant_id
        return self
    
    def _apply_tenant_filter(self, query: Query) -> Query:
        """为查询附加租户过滤条件"""
        if hasattr(self.model, 'tenant_id'):
            # 如果 tenant_id 是 UUID 类型
            return query.filter(self.model.tenant_id == self.tenant_id)
        return query
    
    def get(self, id: UUID) -> Optional[Any]:
        """按 ID 获取（自动附加租户过滤）"""
        query = self.db.query(self.model).filter(self.model.id == id)
        query = self._apply_tenant_filter(query)
        return query.first()
    
    def get_all(self, limit: int = 100, offset: int = 0, order_by: str = None, **filters) -> List[Any]:
        """分页获取（自动附加租户过滤）"""
        query = self.db.query(self.model)
        query = self._apply_tenant_filter(query)
        
        # 附加过滤条件
        for key, value in filters.items():
            if value is not None:
                query = query.filter(getattr(self.model, key) == value)
        
        if order_by:
            query = query.order_by(order_by)
        
        return query.offset(offset).limit(limit).all()
    
    def count(self, **filters) -> int:
        """计数（自动附加租户过滤）"""
        query = self.db.query(func.count(self.model.id))
        query = self._apply_tenant_filter(query)
        
        for key, value in filters.items():
            if value is not None:
                query = query.filter(getattr(self.model, key) == value)
        
        return query.scalar() or 0
    
    def create(self, **data) -> Any:
        """创建（自动注入 tenant_id）"""
        if hasattr(self.model, 'tenant_id'):
            data['tenant_id'] = self.tenant_id
        instance = self.model(**data)
        self.db.add(instance)
        self.db.commit()
        self.db.refresh(instance)
        return instance
    
    def bulk_create(self, items: List[Dict]) -> List[Any]:
        """批量创建（自动注入 tenant_id）"""
        instances = []
        for data in items:
            if hasattr(self.model, 'tenant_id'):
                data['tenant_id'] = self.tenant_id
            instances.append(self.model(**data))
        self.db.add_all(instances)
        self.db.commit()
        return instances
    
    def update(self, id: UUID, **data) -> Optional[Any]:
        """更新（自动附加租户过滤确保安全）"""
        instance = self.get(id)
        if not instance:
            return None
        for key, value in data.items():
            setattr(instance, key, value)
        self.db.commit()
        self.db.refresh(instance)
        return instance
    
    def delete(self, id: UUID) -> bool:
        """删除（自动附加租户过滤确保安全）"""
        instance = self.get(id)
        if not instance:
            return False
        self.db.delete(instance)
        self.db.commit()
        return True
```

### 📄 修改 4：`backend/app/core/state.py`（Redis Key 增加租户前缀）
```python
import json
import time
from uuid import UUID

from app.core.context import get_tenant_id, require_tenant_id, get_tenant_key
from app.utils.redis_client import redis_client
from app.models.customer import Customer
from app.db.session import SessionLocal
from app.utils.logger import logger

# Lua 脚本（原子操作）
_LUA_UPDATE_SCRIPT = """
local key = KEYS[1]
local patch = cjson.decode(ARGV[1])
local ttl = tonumber(ARGV[2])

local current_str = redis.call('GET', key)
local current = {}
if current_str then
    current = cjson.decode(current_str)
else
    current = {score = 0, stage = 'cold', chat_count = 0}
end

for k, v in pairs(patch) do
    current[k] = v
end

current.score = math.max(0, math.min(100, current.score))

redis.call('SETEX', key, ttl, cjson.encode(current))
return cjson.encode(current)
"""
_LUA_UPDATE = redis_client.register_script(_LUA_UPDATE_SCRIPT)

class StateKernel:
    @staticmethod
    def _get_tenant_id() -> UUID:
        """强制获取当前租户ID"""
        tenant_id = get_tenant_id()
        if tenant_id is None:
            raise RuntimeError("Tenant context not set for StateKernel")
        return tenant_id

    @staticmethod
    def _key(user: str) -> str:
        """生成带租户前缀的 Redis Key"""
        tenant_id = StateKernel._get_tenant_id()
        return f"waos:{tenant_id}:state:{user}"

    @staticmethod
    def get(user: str) -> dict:
        """获取状态（自动租户隔离）"""
        key = StateKernel._key(user)
        data = redis_client.get(key)
        if data:
            return json.loads(data)
        
        # 缓存未命中，从 PG 回填（但必须按 tenant_id 过滤）
        db = SessionLocal()
        try:
            tenant_id = StateKernel._get_tenant_id()
            customer = db.query(Customer).filter(
                Customer.tenant_id == tenant_id,
                Customer.wx_id == user
            ).first()
            if customer:
                state = {
                    "score": customer.deal_score or 0,
                    "stage": customer.stage or "cold",
                    "chat_count": 0,
                    "tenant_id": str(tenant_id)
                }
                redis_client.setex(key, 86400 * 30, json.dumps(state))
                return state
        finally:
            db.close()
        
        return {"score": 0, "stage": "cold", "chat_count": 0}

    @staticmethod
    def update(user: str, patch: dict) -> dict:
        """更新状态（原子操作 + 租户隔离）"""
        key = StateKernel._key(user)
        result = _LUA_UPDATE(
            keys=[key],
            args=[json.dumps(patch), str(86400 * 30)]
        )
        state = json.loads(result)
        
        # 异步写 PG（带 tenant_id）
        # 此处简化，建议通过 Repository 写入
        db = SessionLocal()
        try:
            tenant_id = StateKernel._get_tenant_id()
            customer = db.query(Customer).filter(
                Customer.tenant_id == tenant_id,
                Customer.wx_id == user
            ).first()
            if not customer:
                customer = Customer(
                    tenant_id=tenant_id,
                    wx_id=user,
                    deal_score=state["score"],
                    stage=state["stage"]
                )
                db.add(customer)
            else:
                customer.deal_score = state["score"]
                customer.stage = state["stage"]
                customer.updated_at = time.time()
            db.commit()
        finally:
            db.close()
        
        return state
```

### 📄 修改 5：`backend/app/core/pipeline.py`（自动从上下文获取租户）
```python
import asyncio
import time
from typing import Optional

from app.core.event import Event
from app.core.context import get_tenant_id, require_tenant_id, set_tenant_id
from app.core.state import StateKernel
from app.core.crm import CRM
from app.core.strategy import StrategyRouter
from app.core.persona import Persona
from app.core.ai import AI
from app.core.safety import Safety
from app.core.rhythm import Rhythm
from app.core.dedup import Dedup
from app.core.rate_limiter import RateLimiter
from app.core.action import SendMessageAction
from app.core.intent import IntentClassifier
from app.core.circuit_breaker import CircuitBreaker  # 假设已实现
from app.utils.logger import logger

_circuit_breaker = CircuitBreaker()

async def pipeline(event: Event, tenant_id: Optional[str] = None) -> Optional[SendMessageAction]:
    """
    单入口主流程：Event -> Action
    支持从参数或上下文获取 tenant_id
    """
    # 1. 设置租户上下文（如果提供了参数）
    if tenant_id:
        from app.core.context import set_tenant_id
        set_tenant_id(tenant_id)
    
    # 2. 强制检查租户上下文
    try:
        current_tenant = require_tenant_id()
    except RuntimeError:
        logger.error("Pipeline called without tenant context")
        return SendMessageAction(event.user, "系统错误，请联系管理员")

    user = event.user

    # 3. 幂等检查（Redis Key 已自动包含 tenant_id，通过 Dedup 内部使用 get_tenant_key）
    if not Dedup.check(event.event_id):
        logger.warning(f"Duplicate event: {event.event_id}")
        return None

    # 4. 限流
    if not RateLimiter.allow(user):
        logger.warning(f"Rate limited: {user}")
        return SendMessageAction(user, "您发送消息太快了，请稍后再试。")

    # 5. 熔断器
    if not _circuit_breaker.allow():
        return SendMessageAction(user, "系统繁忙，我稍后回复您。")

    try:
        async def _core():
            state = StateKernel.get(user)  # 自动使用上下文 tenant_id
            crm_data = CRM.update(state, event.content, event.timestamp)
            intent = IntentClassifier.classify(event.content)
            strategy = StrategyRouter.route(crm_data, intent)
            persona = Persona.build(crm_data, strategy)
            reply = await AI.run_async(event.content, crm_data, persona, intent)
            reply = Safety.filter(reply)
            Rhythm.apply()
            StateKernel.update(user, crm_data)
            return reply

        reply = await asyncio.wait_for(_core(), timeout=10.0)
        _circuit_breaker.record_success()

        logger.info({
            "event_id": event.event_id,
            "tenant_id": str(current_tenant),
            "user": user,
            "reply": reply[:50],
            "score": crm_data.get("score"),
        })
        return SendMessageAction(user, reply)

    except asyncio.TimeoutError:
        logger.error(f"Pipeline timeout for user {user}")
        _circuit_breaker.record_failure()
        return SendMessageAction(user, "系统处理超时，我稍后回复您。")
    except Exception as e:
        logger.error({"event_id": event.event_id, "error": str(e)})
        _circuit_breaker.record_failure()
        return SendMessageAction(user, "系统繁忙，我稍后回复您。")
```

### 📄 修改 6：`backend/app/api/webhook.py`（使用租户依赖）
```python
from fastapi import APIRouter, Depends, Request
from uuid import UUID

from app.core.event import Event
from app.core.pipeline import pipeline
from app.dependencies.auth import get_current_tenant

router = APIRouter()

@router.post("/webhook/{platform}")
async def webhook_receive(
    platform: str,
    request: Request,
    tenant: UUID = Depends(get_current_tenant)  # 强制租户鉴权
):
    """
    接收所有平台回调
    租户从 JWT 中提取，自动注入上下文
    """
    raw = await request.json()
    
    # 平台适配
    if platform == "wechat":
        user = raw.get("from")
        content = raw.get("content")
        account_id = raw.get("account_id")
    elif platform == "douyin":
        user = raw.get("user_id")
        content = raw.get("text")
        account_id = raw.get("account_id")
    else:
        return {"code": -1, "msg": "unsupported platform"}
    
    event = Event(
        user=user,
        content=content,
        platform=platform,
        account_id=account_id
    )
    
    # pipeline 会自动从上下文读取 tenant_id
    import asyncio
    asyncio.create_task(pipeline(event))
    
    return {"code": 0, "msg": "ok", "event_id": event.event_id}
```

### 📄 修改 7：`backend/app/api/auth.py`（登录时签发含 tenant_id 的 Token）
```python
from fastapi import APIRouter, HTTPException
from pydantic import BaseModel
from uuid import UUID

from app.dependencies.auth import create_access_token
from app.models.user import User
from app.db.session import SessionLocal

router = APIRouter(prefix="/api/auth", tags=["auth"])

class LoginRequest(BaseModel):
    username: str
    password: str

@router.post("/login")
def login(req: LoginRequest):
    db = SessionLocal()
    try:
        # 实际应从 DB 查询
        user = db.query(User).filter(User.username == req.username).first()
        if not user or not user.check_password(req.password):
            raise HTTPException(status_code=401, detail="Invalid credentials")
        
        # 签发 Token（包含 tenant_id）
        token = create_access_token(user.id, user.tenant_id)
        return {
            "access_token": token,
            "token_type": "bearer",
            "tenant_id": str(user.tenant_id),
            "user_id": str(user.id)
        }
    finally:
        db.close()
```

### 📄 修改 8：`backend/app/core/dedup.py`（使用租户前缀）
```python
from app.core.context import get_tenant_key
from app.utils.redis_client import redis_client

class Dedup:
    @staticmethod
    def check(event_id: str) -> bool:
        # Redis Key 自动带租户前缀（不同租户的事件可以重复）
        key = get_tenant_key(f"dedup:{event_id}")
        if redis_client.exists(key):
            return False
        redis_client.setex(key, 86400, "1")
        return True
```

### 📄 修改 9：`backend/app/core/rate_limiter.py`（使用租户前缀）
```python
from app.core.context import get_tenant_key
from app.utils.redis_client import redis_client

class RateLimiter:
    @staticmethod
    def allow(user: str) -> bool:
        # 限流 Key 带租户前缀
        key = get_tenant_key(f"rate:{user}")
        count = redis_client.incr(key)
        if count == 1:
            redis_client.expire(key, 60)
        return count <= 10
```

我们继续攻克 **P0-4：数据库连接池配置**（防止高并发下 PG 连接耗尽）。您说“继续”，我立刻输出完整的连接池配置 + 健康检查代码。

收到。我们接着攻克 **P0-4：数据库连接池配置**。

这是系统稳定性的“最后一道防线”。没有连接池，高并发下 PostgreSQL 连接会耗尽，整个系统直接返回 500，且无法自动恢复。

---

## ✅ 搞定 P0-4：生产级数据库连接池（含健康检查 + 自动重连）

我将采用 **“三层防护”** 策略：
1. **SQLAlchemy 连接池**：配置 `pool_size`、`max_overflow`、`pool_timeout`、`pool_recycle`、`pool_pre_ping`。
2. **健康检查端点**：`/health/db` 用于探针检测。
3. **会话生命周期管理**：使用 `contextlib.contextmanager` 确保异常时自动回滚，连接用完立即归还。

---

### 📄 文件 1：`backend/app/db/session.py`（生产级配置）
```python
import os
import time
from contextlib import contextmanager
from typing import Generator, Optional
from urllib.parse import quote_plus

from sqlalchemy import create_engine, event
from sqlalchemy.engine import Engine
from sqlalchemy.orm import sessionmaker, Session
from sqlalchemy.pool import QueuePool

from app.utils.logger import logger

# ===== 配置读取 =====
DATABASE_URL = os.getenv("DATABASE_URL", "postgresql://waos:waos123@localhost:5432/waos")

# 连接池配置（通过环境变量覆盖）
DB_POOL_SIZE = int(os.getenv("DB_POOL_SIZE", 20))           # 核心连接数
DB_MAX_OVERFLOW = int(os.getenv("DB_MAX_OVERFLOW", 10))     # 最大溢出连接数
DB_POOL_TIMEOUT = int(os.getenv("DB_POOL_TIMEOUT", 30))     # 获取连接超时（秒）
DB_POOL_RECYCLE = int(os.getenv("DB_POOL_RECYCLE", 3600))   # 连接回收时间（秒）
DB_POOL_PRE_PING = os.getenv("DB_POOL_PRE_PING", "true").lower() == "true"  # 使用前检测
DB_ECHO = os.getenv("DB_ECHO", "false").lower() == "true"   # SQL 日志（生产关）

# ===== 创建引擎 =====
def create_db_engine() -> Engine:
    """创建生产级数据库引擎"""
    engine = create_engine(
        DATABASE_URL,
        # 连接池配置
        poolclass=QueuePool,
        pool_size=DB_POOL_SIZE,
        max_overflow=DB_MAX_OVERFLOW,
        pool_timeout=DB_POOL_TIMEOUT,
        pool_recycle=DB_POOL_RECYCLE,
        pool_pre_ping=DB_POOL_PRE_PING,  # 关键：使用前检测连接是否存活
        # 性能优化
        echo=DB_ECHO,
        echo_pool=False,  # 生产关闭 pool 日志
        # 超时配置
        connect_args={
            "connect_timeout": 10,
            "command_timeout": 30,
            "keepalives": 1,
            "keepalives_idle": 30,
            "keepalives_interval": 10,
            "keepalives_count": 5,
        }
    )
    
    # 监听连接池事件（用于监控）
    @event.listens_for(engine, "checkout")
    def receive_checkout(dbapi_conn, connection_record, connection_proxy):
        logger.debug("Connection checkout from pool")
    
    @event.listens_for(engine, "checkin")
    def receive_checkin(dbapi_conn, connection_record):
        logger.debug("Connection checkin to pool")
    
    @event.listens_for(engine, "connect")
    def receive_connect(dbapi_conn, connection_record):
        logger.info("New DB connection established")
    
    logger.info(
        f"Database engine initialized: "
        f"pool_size={DB_POOL_SIZE}, max_overflow={DB_MAX_OVERFLOW}, "
        f"pool_recycle={DB_POOL_RECYCLE}s, pool_pre_ping={DB_POOL_PRE_PING}"
    )
    return engine

# ===== 全局引擎和 SessionLocal =====
_engine = None
_SessionLocal = None

def get_engine() -> Engine:
    """获取全局引擎（单例）"""
    global _engine
    if _engine is None:
        _engine = create_db_engine()
    return _engine

def get_session_local() -> sessionmaker:
    """获取 SessionLocal 工厂（单例）"""
    global _SessionLocal
    if _SessionLocal is None:
        _SessionLocal = sessionmaker(
            autocommit=False,
            autoflush=False,
            bind=get_engine()
        )
    return _SessionLocal

# ===== 会话生命周期管理 =====

@contextmanager
def get_db_session() -> Generator[Session, None, None]:
    """
    上下文管理器：自动处理事务和连接释放
    
    使用方式：
        with get_db_session() as db:
            db.query(User).all()
    """
    session = get_session_local()()
    start_time = time.time()
    try:
        yield session
        session.commit()
        logger.debug(f"DB session committed in {time.time() - start_time:.3f}s")
    except Exception as e:
        session.rollback()
        logger.error(f"DB session rollback: {e}")
        raise
    finally:
        session.close()
        logger.debug(f"DB session closed in {time.time() - start_time:.3f}s")

# ===== FastAPI 依赖注入 =====

def get_db() -> Generator[Session, None, None]:
    """
    FastAPI 依赖注入：用于路由中的 `db: Session = Depends(get_db)`
    """
    with get_db_session() as session:
        yield session

# ===== 健康检查 =====

def check_db_health() -> dict:
    """检查数据库连接和连接池状态"""
    status = {"status": "healthy", "pool": {}}
    
    try:
        from sqlalchemy import text
        engine = get_engine()
        
        # 1. 执行简单查询
        with get_db_session() as db:
            result = db.execute(text("SELECT 1")).scalar()
            if result != 1:
                status["status"] = "unhealthy"
                status["error"] = "Query returned unexpected result"
        
        # 2. 获取连接池状态
        pool = engine.pool
        status["pool"] = {
            "size": pool.size(),
            "checked_in": pool.checkedin(),
            "overflow": pool.overflow(),
            "total": pool.total(),
        }
        
    except Exception as e:
        status["status"] = "unhealthy"
        status["error"] = str(e)
        logger.error(f"DB health check failed: {e}")
    
    return status

# ===== 优雅关闭 =====

def shutdown_db_pool():
    """应用关闭时清理连接池"""
    global _engine
    if _engine:
        logger.info("Disposing database connection pool...")
        _engine.dispose()
        _engine = None
        logger.info("Database connection pool disposed")
```

### 📄 文件 2：`backend/app/api/health.py`（健康检查端点）
```python
from fastapi import APIRouter, Depends
from app.db.session import check_db_health
from app.core.vector.client import get_qdrant_client
from app.utils.redis_client import redis_client
from app.core.llm.factory import LLMFactory
import os

router = APIRouter(prefix="/health", tags=["health"])

@router.get("/ping")
async def health_ping():
    """简单探针（K8s liveness）"""
    return {"status": "alive", "service": "waos"}

@router.get("/ready")
async def health_ready():
    """
    就绪探针（K8s readiness）
    检查所有依赖服务是否可用
    """
    status = {
        "status": "ready",
        "checks": {}
    }
    all_healthy = True
    
    # 1. 检查数据库
    db_status = check_db_health()
    status["checks"]["database"] = db_status["status"]
    if db_status["status"] != "healthy":
        all_healthy = False
        status["checks"]["database_error"] = db_status.get("error", "unknown")
    
    # 2. 检查 Redis
    try:
        redis_client.ping()
        status["checks"]["redis"] = "healthy"
    except Exception as e:
        status["checks"]["redis"] = "unhealthy"
        status["checks"]["redis_error"] = str(e)
        all_healthy = False
    
    # 3. 检查 Qdrant
    try:
        client = get_qdrant_client()
        client.get_collections()
        status["checks"]["qdrant"] = "healthy"
    except Exception as e:
        status["checks"]["qdrant"] = "unhealthy"
        status["checks"]["qdrant_error"] = str(e)
        all_healthy = False
    
    # 4. 检查 LLM（仅验证 API Key 是否有效）
    try:
        llm = LLMFactory.get_provider()
        if llm.health_check():
            status["checks"]["llm"] = "healthy"
        else:
            status["checks"]["llm"] = "unhealthy"
            all_healthy = False
    except Exception as e:
        status["checks"]["llm"] = "unhealthy"
        status["checks"]["llm_error"] = str(e)
        all_healthy = False
    
    status["status"] = "ready" if all_healthy else "not_ready"
    return status

@router.get("/db")
async def health_db():
    """数据库专用探针（用于排查）"""
    return check_db_health()
```
