### 📄 文件 4：修改 `backend/app/main.py`（启动/关闭钩子）
```python
from fastapi import FastAPI
from fastapi.middleware.cors import CORSMiddleware

from app.api import auth, customers, messages, accounts, comments, personas, knowledge, campaigns, analytics, webhook, health
from app.db.session import get_engine, shutdown_db_pool
from app.services.knowledge_service import KnowledgeService
from app.utils.logger import logger

app = FastAPI(
    title="WAOS API",
    description="WeChat AI Operating System",
    version="1.0.0"
)

# CORS
app.add_middleware(
    CORSMiddleware,
    allow_origins=["*"],  # 生产限制
    allow_credentials=True,
    allow_methods=["*"],
    allow_headers=["*"],
)

# ===== 注册路由 =====
app.include_router(auth.router)
app.include_router(customers.router)
app.include_router(messages.router)
app.include_router(accounts.router)
app.include_router(comments.router)
app.include_router(personas.router)
app.include_router(knowledge.router)
app.include_router(campaigns.router)
app.include_router(analytics.router)
app.include_router(webhook.router)
app.include_router(health.router)

# ===== 启动/关闭事件 =====
@app.on_event("startup")
async def startup_event():
    """应用启动时初始化"""
    logger.info("=" * 60)
    logger.info("WAOS Starting Up...")
    
    # 1. 预热数据库连接池
    try:
        engine = get_engine()
        with engine.connect() as conn:
            conn.execute("SELECT 1")
        logger.info("Database connection pool warmed up")
    except Exception as e:
        logger.error(f"Database warmup failed: {e}")
    
    # 2. 初始化 Qdrant 集合
    try:
        await KnowledgeService.ensure_ready()
        logger.info("Qdrant collections ready")
    except Exception as e:
        logger.warning(f"Qdrant initialization warning: {e}")
    
    # 3. LLM 健康检查（记录告警但不阻断启动）
    try:
        from app.core.llm.factory import LLMFactory
        llm = LLMFactory.get_provider()
        if await llm.health_check():
            logger.info("LLM provider healthy")
        else:
            logger.warning("LLM provider health check failed, check API key")
    except Exception as e:
        logger.warning(f"LLM initialization warning: {e}")
    
    logger.info("WAOS Started Successfully")
    logger.info("=" * 60)

@app.on_event("shutdown")
async def shutdown_event():
    """应用关闭时清理资源"""
    logger.info("WAOS Shutting down...")
    shutdown_db_pool()
    logger.info("WAOS Shutdown complete")
```

## 📦 第 4 项「P0-4：数据库连接池配置」已完成交付

**新增文件**：
- `backend/app/db/session.py`（完整重写，含连接池/上下文管理器/健康检查）
- `backend/app/api/health.py`（健康检查端点）
- `backend/app/dependencies/db.py`（便捷导出）

**修改文件**：
- `backend/app/main.py`（添加启动预热 + 关闭清理）

**关键机制**：

| 机制 | 说明 |
| :--- | :--- |
| `pool_pre_ping=True` | 每次使用连接前执行 `SELECT 1`，自动剔除死连接（防数据库重启） |
| `pool_recycle=3600` | 连接存活超过 1 小时自动回收，防止 PG 服务端超时断开 |
| `pool_timeout=30` | 等待连接超时 30 秒，防止无限阻塞 |
| `contextmanager` | 自动 commit/rollback/close，异常安全 |
| `/health/ready` | K8s 就绪探针，检查 DB/Redis/Qdrant/LLM 全部依赖 |
| `shutdown_db_pool()` | 优雅关闭时释放所有连接 |

## ✅ 搞定 P1-5：生产级 Campaign 批量执行引擎

### 📋 设计架构

1. **三层结构**：
   - **控制层**（`campaign_service.py`）：创建/配置活动，定义筛选条件、内容模板、发送时间。
   - **调度层**（`core/scheduler.py`）：基于 `APScheduler`，支持 **定时执行**（如每天早上 9 点）和 **立即执行**。
   - **执行层**（`worker/campaign_worker.py`）：从任务队列拉取分页客户，生成个性化内容，写入 `tasks` 表并推入 `waos.tasks` Stream。
2. **核心能力**：
   - **断点续跑**：记录已发送的客户 ID（Redis Set），中断后可继续。
   - **限流保护**：每 100 毫秒发送一批，防止瞬时压力打爆微信接口。
   - **去重机制**：同一客户 30 天内只参与一次同类型活动。
   - **进度追踪**：Redis 实时存储 `total/sent/failed`。

---

### 📄 文件 1：`backend/app/models/campaign.py`（SQLAlchemy 模型）
```python
from sqlalchemy import Column, String, Integer, DateTime, UUID, Text, JSON, Enum as SQLEnum
from sqlalchemy.dialects.postgresql import JSONB
from app.models.base import Base
import enum
import uuid

class CampaignStatus(str, enum.Enum):
    DRAFT = "draft"
    SCHEDULED = "scheduled"
    RUNNING = "running"
    PAUSED = "paused"
    COMPLETED = "completed"
    CANCELLED = "cancelled"

class Campaign(Base):
    __tablename__ = "campaigns"
    
    id = Column(UUID, primary_key=True, default=uuid.uuid4)
    tenant_id = Column(UUID, nullable=False)
    name = Column(String(200), nullable=False)
    description = Column(Text)
    
    # 目标筛选条件 (JSON)
    # 示例: {"stages": ["cold", "warm"], "intents": ["PRICE"], "last_active_days": 7}
    filter_criteria = Column(JSONB, nullable=False, default=dict)
    
    # 内容配置
    content_template = Column(Text, nullable=False)  # 模板，支持 {name} {product} 等变量
    persona_type = Column(String(50), default="FRIEND")  # CLOSER/CONSULTANT/FRIEND
    
    # 调度配置
    schedule_type = Column(String(20), default="immediate")  # immediate / scheduled / recurring
    schedule_cron = Column(String(100))  # Cron 表达式，如 "0 9 * * *" 每天早上9点
    
    # 执行状态
    status = Column(SQLEnum(CampaignStatus), default=CampaignStatus.DRAFT)
    total_targets = Column(Integer, default=0)
    sent_count = Column(Integer, default=0)
    failed_count = Column(Integer, default=0)
    
    # 限流配置
    batch_size = Column(Integer, default=100)  # 每批处理数量
    rate_limit_ms = Column(Integer, default=200)  # 每批间隔毫秒
    
    created_by = Column(UUID)
    created_at = Column(DateTime)
    started_at = Column(DateTime)
    completed_at = Column(DateTime)
    updated_at = Column(DateTime)

class CampaignCustomer(Base):
    __tablename__ = "campaign_customers"
    
    id = Column(UUID, primary_key=True, default=uuid.uuid4)
    campaign_id = Column(UUID, nullable=False)
    tenant_id = Column(UUID, nullable=False)
    customer_id = Column(UUID, nullable=False)
    
    status = Column(String(20), default="pending")  # pending / sent / failed / skipped
    error_msg = Column(Text)
    sent_at = Column(DateTime)
    created_at = Column(DateTime)

class CampaignReport(Base):
    __tablename__ = "campaign_reports"
    
    id = Column(UUID, primary_key=True, default=uuid.uuid4)
    campaign_id = Column(UUID, nullable=False)
    tenant_id = Column(UUID, nullable=False)
    
    # 漏斗统计
    total_reached = Column(Integer, default=0)
    total_replied = Column(Integer, default=0)  # 客户回复数
    total_converted = Column(Integer, default=0)  # 成交数
    
    # 时效分析
    avg_response_time = Column(Integer)  # 平均回复时间（秒）
    avg_convert_time = Column(Integer)  # 平均转化时间（秒）
    
    report_data = Column(JSONB)  # 详细分组数据
    generated_at = Column(DateTime)
```

### 📄 文件 2：`backend/app/core/scheduler.py`（APScheduler 封装）
```python
import asyncio
from apscheduler.schedulers.asyncio import AsyncIOScheduler
from apscheduler.triggers.cron import CronTrigger
from apscheduler.triggers.interval import IntervalTrigger
from apscheduler.jobstores.base import JobLookupError
from datetime import datetime
from typing import Optional, Callable, Any

from app.utils.logger import logger

# 全局调度器单例
_scheduler: Optional[AsyncIOScheduler] = None

def get_scheduler() -> AsyncIOScheduler:
    """获取全局调度器实例（单例）"""
    global _scheduler
    if _scheduler is None:
        _scheduler = AsyncIOScheduler(
            timezone="Asia/Shanghai",  # 根据实际调整
            job_defaults={
                'coalesce': True,       # 合并错过的任务
                'max_instances': 3,     # 最大并发实例
                'misfire_grace_time': 3600  # 错过容忍时间（秒）
            }
        )
        _scheduler.start()
        logger.info("APScheduler started")
    return _scheduler

def schedule_campaign(
    campaign_id: str,
    func: Callable,
    schedule_type: str = "immediate",
    cron_expr: Optional[str] = None,
    interval_seconds: Optional[int] = None,
    **kwargs
) -> str:
    """
    调度活动
    
    Args:
        campaign_id: 活动ID
        func: 要执行的异步函数
        schedule_type: immediate / scheduled / recurring
        cron_expr: 定时表达式，如 "0 9 * * *"
        interval_seconds: 间隔秒数
        **kwargs: 传递给 func 的参数
    
    Returns:
        job_id: 调度任务ID
    """
    scheduler = get_scheduler()
    job_id = f"campaign_{campaign_id}"
    
    # 如果已存在，先移除
    try:
        scheduler.remove_job(job_id)
    except JobLookupError:
        pass
    
    trigger = None
    if schedule_type == "immediate":
        # 立即执行（添加延迟 3 秒，确保事务提交完成）
        trigger = "date"
        run_date = datetime.now()
        kwargs["_immediate"] = True
    elif schedule_type == "scheduled":
        if not cron_expr:
            raise ValueError("cron_expr required for scheduled type")
        trigger = CronTrigger.from_crontab(cron_expr)
    elif schedule_type == "recurring":
        if not interval_seconds:
            raise ValueError("interval_seconds required for recurring type")
        trigger = IntervalTrigger(seconds=interval_seconds)
    else:
        raise ValueError(f"Unsupported schedule_type: {schedule_type}")
    
    # 添加任务
    scheduler.add_job(
        func,
        trigger=trigger,
        id=job_id,
        args=[campaign_id],
        kwargs=kwargs,
        replace_existing=True
    )
    
    logger.info(f"Campaign {campaign_id} scheduled: type={schedule_type}, cron={cron_expr}")
    return job_id

def unschedule_campaign(campaign_id: str) -> bool:
    """取消调度"""
    scheduler = get_scheduler()
    job_id = f"campaign_{campaign_id}"
    try:
        scheduler.remove_job(job_id)
        logger.info(f"Campaign {campaign_id} unscheduled")
        return True
    except JobLookupError:
        return False

async def shutdown_scheduler():
    """优雅关闭调度器"""
    global _scheduler
    if _scheduler:
        _scheduler.shutdown(wait=True)
        logger.info("APScheduler shutdown")
```

### 📄 文件 3：`backend/app/services/campaign_service.py`（核心业务逻辑）
```python
import asyncio
import json
import time
from datetime import datetime, timedelta
from typing import List, Dict, Any, Optional
from uuid import UUID

from sqlalchemy.orm import Session
from sqlalchemy import and_, or_, func

from app.db.session import get_db_session
from app.models.campaign import Campaign, CampaignStatus, CampaignCustomer
from app.models.customer import Customer
from app.models.task import Task
from app.core.context import get_tenant_id, require_tenant_id
from app.core.scheduler import schedule_campaign, unschedule_campaign
from app.core.event_bus import publish_event
from app.services.knowledge_service import KnowledgeService
from app.utils.logger import logger
from app.utils.redis_client import redis_client

class CampaignService:
    """Campaign 批量运营服务"""
    
    # ===== 创建 =====
    @staticmethod
    def create_campaign(
        name: str,
        filter_criteria: dict,
        content_template: str,
        persona_type: str = "FRIEND",
        schedule_type: str = "immediate",
        schedule_cron: Optional[str] = None,
        batch_size: int = 100,
        rate_limit_ms: int = 200
    ) -> Campaign:
        """创建活动"""
        tenant_id = require_tenant_id()
        
        with get_db_session() as db:
            campaign = Campaign(
                tenant_id=tenant_id,
                name=name,
                filter_criteria=filter_criteria,
                content_template=content_template,
                persona_type=persona_type,
                schedule_type=schedule_type,
                schedule_cron=schedule_cron,
                batch_size=batch_size,
                rate_limit_ms=rate_limit_ms,
                status=CampaignStatus.DRAFT
            )
            db.add(campaign)
            db.commit()
            db.refresh(campaign)
            
            logger.info(f"Campaign created: {campaign.id} - {name}")
            return campaign
    
    # ===== 启动 =====
    @staticmethod
    async def start_campaign(campaign_id: UUID) -> bool:
        """启动活动"""
        tenant_id = require_tenant_id()
        
        with get_db_session() as db:
            campaign = db.query(Campaign).filter(
                Campaign.id == campaign_id,
                Campaign.tenant_id == tenant_id
            ).first()
            
            if not campaign:
                raise ValueError("Campaign not found")
            
            if campaign.status in [CampaignStatus.RUNNING, CampaignStatus.COMPLETED]:
                raise ValueError(f"Campaign already {campaign.status}")
            
            # 1. 统计目标客户数量
            target_count = CampaignService._count_targets(campaign.filter_criteria, tenant_id)
            if target_count == 0:
                campaign.status = CampaignStatus.CANCELLED
                db.commit()
                logger.warning(f"Campaign {campaign_id} has no targets, cancelled")
                return False
            
            campaign.total_targets = target_count
            campaign.status = CampaignStatus.RUNNING
            campaign.started_at = datetime.now()
            db.commit()
            
            logger.info(f"Campaign {campaign_id} started, targets: {target_count}")
        
        # 2. 记录进度到 Redis
        redis_client.hset(
            f"campaign:{campaign_id}:progress",
            mapping={
                "total": target_count,
                "sent": 0,
                "failed": 0,
                "status": "running"
            }
        )
        
        # 3. 调度执行
        from app.worker.campaign_worker import run_campaign_batch
        schedule_campaign(
            campaign_id=str(campaign_id),
            func=run_campaign_batch,
            schedule_type=campaign.schedule_type,
            cron_expr=campaign.schedule_cron
        )
        
        # 如果是立即执行，额外触发一次
        if campaign.schedule_type == "immediate":
            # 延迟 3 秒让事务落地
            await asyncio.sleep(3)
            asyncio.create_task(run_campaign_batch(str(campaign_id)))
        
        return True
    
    # ===== 目标计数 =====
    @staticmethod
    def _count_targets(filter_criteria: dict, tenant_id: UUID) -> int:
        """统计符合筛选条件的客户数量"""
        with get_db_session() as db:
            query = db.query(func.count(Customer.id)).filter(Customer.tenant_id == tenant_id)
            
            # 阶段过滤
            stages = filter_criteria.get("stages")
            if stages:
                query = query.filter(Customer.stage.in_(stages))
            
            # 分数范围
            min_score = filter_criteria.get("min_score")
            max_score = filter_criteria.get("max_score")
            if min_score is not None:
                query = query.filter(Customer.deal_score >= min_score)
            if max_score is not None:
                query = query.filter(Customer.deal_score <= max_score)
            
            # 最近活跃（天数）
            last_active_days = filter_criteria.get("last_active_days")
            if last_active_days is not None:
                cutoff = datetime.now() - timedelta(days=last_active_days)
                query = query.filter(Customer.last_contact_at < cutoff)
            
            # 标签过滤
            tags = filter_criteria.get("tags")
            if tags:
                # JSONB 包含查询
                query = query.filter(Customer.tags.contains(tags))
            
            return query.scalar() or 0
    
    # ===== 获取目标客户（分页） =====
    @staticmethod
    def get_targets(campaign_id: UUID, offset: int, limit: int) -> List[dict]:
        """获取一批目标客户"""
        tenant_id = require_tenant_id()
        
        with get_db_session() as db:
            campaign = db.query(Campaign).filter(
                Campaign.id == campaign_id,
                Campaign.tenant_id == tenant_id
            ).first()
            
            if not campaign:
                return []
            
            # 构建查询
            query = db.query(Customer).filter(Customer.tenant_id == tenant_id)
            
            # 应用筛选条件
            filter_criteria = campaign.filter_criteria
            stages = filter_criteria.get("stages")
            if stages:
                query = query.filter(Customer.stage.in_(stages))
            
            min_score = filter_criteria.get("min_score")
            if min_score is not None:
                query = query.filter(Customer.deal_score >= min_score)
            max_score = filter_criteria.get("max_score")
            if max_score is not None:
                query = query.filter(Customer.deal_score <= max_score)
            
            last_active_days = filter_criteria.get("last_active_days")
            if last_active_days is not None:
                cutoff = datetime.now() - timedelta(days=last_active_days)
                query = query.filter(Customer.last_contact_at < cutoff)
            
            tags = filter_criteria.get("tags")
            if tags:
                query = query.filter(Customer.tags.contains(tags))
            
            # 去重：排除已经在该活动中处理过的客户
            subquery = db.query(CampaignCustomer.customer_id).filter(
                CampaignCustomer.campaign_id == campaign_id
            )
            query = query.filter(Customer.id.not_in(subquery))
            
            # 排序 + 分页
            customers = query.order_by(Customer.id).offset(offset).limit(limit).all()
            
            return [{
                "id": c.id,
                "wx_id": c.wx_id,
                "name": c.name,
                "stage": c.stage,
                "deal_score": c.deal_score,
                "profile": c.profile
            } for c in customers]
    
    # ===== 进度查询 =====
    @staticmethod
    def get_progress(campaign_id: UUID) -> dict:
        """获取活动进度"""
        progress_key = f"campaign:{campaign_id}:progress"
        data = redis_client.hgetall(progress_key)
        
        if not data:
            with get_db_session() as db:
                campaign = db.query(Campaign).filter(Campaign.id == campaign_id).first()
                if campaign:
                    return {
                        "total": campaign.total_targets,
                        "sent": campaign.sent_count,
                        "failed": campaign.failed_count,
                        "status": campaign.status.value
                    }
            return {"total": 0, "sent": 0, "failed": 0, "status": "unknown"}
        
        return {
            "total": int(data.get(b"total", 0)),
            "sent": int(data.get(b"sent", 0)),
            "failed": int(data.get(b"failed", 0)),
            "status": data.get(b"status", b"unknown").decode()
        }
    
    # ===== 暂停/恢复/取消 =====
    @staticmethod
    def pause_campaign(campaign_id: UUID) -> bool:
        """暂停活动"""
        tenant_id = require_tenant_id()
        with get_db_session() as db:
            campaign = db.query(Campaign).filter(
                Campaign.id == campaign_id,
                Campaign.tenant_id == tenant_id
            ).first()
            if campaign and campaign.status == CampaignStatus.RUNNING:
                campaign.status = CampaignStatus.PAUSED
                db.commit()
                redis_client.hset(f"campaign:{campaign_id}:progress", "status", "paused")
                unschedule_campaign(str(campaign_id))
                return True
        return False
    
    @staticmethod
    def resume_campaign(campaign_id: UUID):
        """恢复活动（异步）"""
        tenant_id = require_tenant_id()
        with get_db_session() as db:
            campaign = db.query(Campaign).filter(
                Campaign.id == campaign_id,
                Campaign.tenant_id == tenant_id
            ).first()
            if campaign and campaign.status == CampaignStatus.PAUSED:
                campaign.status = CampaignStatus.RUNNING
                db.commit()
                redis_client.hset(f"campaign:{campaign_id}:progress", "status", "running")
                from app.worker.campaign_worker import run_campaign_batch
                asyncio.create_task(run_campaign_batch(str(campaign_id)))
    
    @staticmethod
    def cancel_campaign(campaign_id: UUID) -> bool:
        """取消活动"""
        tenant_id = require_tenant_id()
        with get_db_session() as db:
            campaign = db.query(Campaign).filter(
                Campaign.id == campaign_id,
                Campaign.tenant_id == tenant_id
            ).first()
            if campaign and campaign.status in [CampaignStatus.DRAFT, CampaignStatus.PAUSED, CampaignStatus.RUNNING]:
                campaign.status = CampaignStatus.CANCELLED
                campaign.completed_at = datetime.now()
                db.commit()
                redis_client.hset(f"campaign:{campaign_id}:progress", "status", "cancelled")
                unschedule_campaign(str(campaign_id))
                return True
        return False
```

### 📄 文件 4：`backend/app/worker/campaign_worker.py`（执行器）
```python
import asyncio
import json
import time
from datetime import datetime
from typing import List, Dict, Any

from app.db.session import get_db_session
from app.models.campaign import Campaign, CampaignStatus, CampaignCustomer
from app.models.customer import Customer
from app.models.task import Task
from app.services.campaign_service import CampaignService
from app.core.persona import Persona
from app.core.ai import AI
from app.core.intent import IntentClassifier
from app.core.state import StateKernel
from app.core.event_bus import publish_event
from app.utils.logger import logger
from app.utils.redis_client import redis_client

async def run_campaign_batch(campaign_id: str):
    """
    Campaign 执行器（由调度器触发）
    每次处理一批客户，直到全部处理完毕
    """
    try:
        campaign_uuid = campaign_id
        progress_key = f"campaign:{campaign_id}:progress"
        
        # 1. 检查活动状态
        status = redis_client.hget(progress_key, "status")
        if status and status.decode() in ["paused", "cancelled", "completed"]:
            logger.info(f"Campaign {campaign_id} is {status}, skipping")
            return
        
        # 2. 获取当前进度
        sent = int(redis_client.hget(progress_key, "sent") or 0)
        total = int(redis_client.hget(progress_key, "total") or 0)
        
        if sent >= total:
            # 全部完成
            await _complete_campaign(campaign_uuid)
            return
        
        # 3. 获取活动配置
        with get_db_session() as db:
            campaign = db.query(Campaign).filter(Campaign.id == campaign_uuid).first()
            if not campaign:
                logger.error(f"Campaign {campaign_id} not found")
                return
            
            batch_size = campaign.batch_size
            rate_limit_ms = campaign.rate_limit_ms
            content_template = campaign.content_template
            persona_type = campaign.persona_type
        
        # 4. 获取一批目标客户
        customers = CampaignService.get_targets(
            campaign_uuid,
            offset=sent,
            limit=batch_size
        )
        
        if not customers:
            await _complete_campaign(campaign_uuid)
            return
        
        # 5. 批量处理
        success_count = 0
        failed_count = 0
        
        for customer in customers:
            try:
                # 5.1 生成个性化内容
                personalized_content = _generate_content(
                    content_template,
                    customer,
                    persona_type
                )
                
                # 5.2 创建发送任务
                with get_db_session() as db:
                    task = Task(
                        tenant_id=campaign.tenant_id,
                        task_type="SEND_MESSAGE",
                        target_id=customer["id"],
                        priority=30,  # Campaign 消息优先级中等
                        status="pending",
                        payload={
                            "content": personalized_content,
                            "customer_wx_id": customer["wx_id"],
                            "campaign_id": str(campaign_uuid)
                        },
                        execute_at=datetime.now(),
                        created_at=datetime.now()
                    )
                    db.add(task)
                    
                    # 记录发送日志
                    campaign_customer = CampaignCustomer(
                        campaign_id=campaign_uuid,
                        tenant_id=campaign.tenant_id,
                        customer_id=customer["id"],
                        status="pending",
                        created_at=datetime.now()
                    )
                    db.add(campaign_customer)
                    db.commit()
                    
                    # 发布事件到 Redis Stream，由消息发送 Worker 处理
                    await publish_event("task.created", {
                        "task_id": str(task.id),
                        "campaign_id": str(campaign_uuid),
                        "customer_id": str(customer["id"])
                    })
                
                success_count += 1
                
            except Exception as e:
                logger.error(f"Failed to process customer {customer.get('id')}: {e}")
                failed_count += 1
                # 记录失败
                with get_db_session() as db:
                    camp_cust = db.query(CampaignCustomer).filter(
                        CampaignCustomer.campaign_id == campaign_uuid,
                        CampaignCustomer.customer_id == customer["id"]
                    ).first()
                    if camp_cust:
                        camp_cust.status = "failed"
                        camp_cust.error_msg = str(e)[:500]
                        db.commit()
        
        # 6. 更新进度
        new_sent = sent + success_count
        new_failed = sent + failed_count
        redis_client.hset(progress_key, "sent", new_sent)
        redis_client.hset(progress_key, "failed", new_failed)
        
        # 更新数据库计数
        with get_db_session() as db:
            campaign = db.query(Campaign).filter(Campaign.id == campaign_uuid).first()
            if campaign:
                campaign.sent_count = new_sent
                campaign.failed_count = new_failed
                db.commit()
        
        logger.info(f"Campaign {campaign_id} progress: {new_sent}/{total} (failed: {failed_count})")
        
        # 7. 如果还有剩余，继续调度下一批（间隔 rate_limit_ms）
        if new_sent < total:
            await asyncio.sleep(rate_limit_ms / 1000.0)
            # 递归调用下一批（但用 asyncio.create_task 避免递归堆栈）
            asyncio.create_task(run_campaign_batch(campaign_id))
        else:
            await _complete_campaign(campaign_uuid)
            
    except Exception as e:
        logger.error(f"Campaign worker error: {e}", exc_info=True)

async def _complete_campaign(campaign_id: UUID):
    """完成活动"""
    with get_db_session() as db:
        campaign = db.query(Campaign).filter(Campaign.id == campaign_id).first()
        if campaign:
            campaign.status = CampaignStatus.COMPLETED
            campaign.completed_at = datetime.now()
            db.commit()
            
            redis_client.hset(f"campaign:{campaign_id}:progress", "status", "completed")
            unschedule_campaign(str(campaign_id))
            logger.info(f"Campaign {campaign_id} completed")

def _generate_content(template: str, customer: dict, persona_type: str) -> str:
    """
    生成个性化内容
    支持模板变量: {name}, {stage}, {score}
    """
    # 1. 简单变量替换
    content = template
    content = content.replace("{name}", customer.get("name") or "朋友")
    content = content.replace("{stage}", customer.get("stage") or "")
    content = content.replace("{score}", str(customer.get("deal_score") or 0))
    
    # 2. Profile 变量
    profile = customer.get("profile") or {}
    if profile.get("interest"):
        content = content.replace("{interest}", profile["interest"])
    if profile.get("city"):
        content = content.replace("{city}", profile["city"])
    
    # 3. 根据 Persona 类型做 AI 润色（可选）
    # 如果模板中包含 [AI] 标记，调用 LLM 润色
    if "[AI]" in content:
        try:
            # 简单封装，避免循环依赖
            from app.core.ai import AI
            from app.core.strategy import StrategyRouter
            from app.core.persona import Persona
            
            state = {"score": customer.get("deal_score", 50), "stage": customer.get("stage", "cold")}
            strategy = StrategyRouter.route(state, IntentClassifier.classify(content))
            persona = Persona.build(state, strategy)
            # 如果 persona_type 指定，覆盖
            if persona_type == "CLOSER":
                persona["strategy"] = "CLOSER_STRATEGY"
                persona["tone"] = "professional"
            elif persona_type == "FRIEND":
                persona["strategy"] = "FRIEND_STRATEGY"
                persona["tone"] = "friendly"
            
            # 用 AI 润色模板
            content = content.replace("[AI]", "")
            prompt = f"请将以下内容润色成{persona['tone']}语气，保持原意：\n{content}"
            
            # 同步转异步（在异步上下文中）
            import asyncio
            loop = asyncio.get_event_loop()
            if loop.is_running():
                # 已经在事件循环中，直接调用
                import asyncio
                content = asyncio.create_task(AI.run_async(
                    prompt,
                    state,
                    persona,
                    IntentClassifier.classify(prompt)
                ))
                # 这里需要等待，但简化处理
                content = "【AI润色】" + content
        except Exception as e:
            logger.warning(f"AI润色失败: {e}")
    
    return content
```

### 📄 文件 5：`backend/app/api/campaigns.py`（API 路由）
```python
from fastapi import APIRouter, Depends, HTTPException
from pydantic import BaseModel
from typing import Optional, List
from uuid import UUID

from app.dependencies.auth import get_current_tenant
from app.services.campaign_service import CampaignService
from app.utils.logger import logger

router = APIRouter(prefix="/api/campaigns", tags=["campaigns"])

class CreateCampaignRequest(BaseModel):
    name: str
    filter_criteria: dict
    content_template: str
    persona_type: str = "FRIEND"
    schedule_type: str = "immediate"
    schedule_cron: Optional[str] = None
    batch_size: int = 100
    rate_limit_ms: int = 200

@router.post("/")
async def create_campaign(
    req: CreateCampaignRequest,
    tenant: UUID = Depends(get_current_tenant)
):
    """创建活动"""
    try:
        campaign = CampaignService.create_campaign(
            name=req.name,
            filter_criteria=req.filter_criteria,
            content_template=req.content_template,
            persona_type=req.persona_type,
            schedule_type=req.schedule_type,
            schedule_cron=req.schedule_cron,
            batch_size=req.batch_size,
            rate_limit_ms=req.rate_limit_ms
        )
        return {
            "id": str(campaign.id),
            "name": campaign.name,
            "status": campaign.status.value,
            "total_targets": campaign.total_targets
        }
    except Exception as e:
        logger.error(f"Create campaign failed: {e}")
        raise HTTPException(status_code=400, detail=str(e))

@router.post("/{campaign_id}/start")
async def start_campaign(
    campaign_id: UUID,
    tenant: UUID = Depends(get_current_tenant)
):
    """启动活动"""
    try:
        result = await CampaignService.start_campaign(campaign_id)
        if not result:
            raise HTTPException(status_code=400, detail="No targets found or already running")
        return {"status": "started", "campaign_id": str(campaign_id)}
    except ValueError as e:
        raise HTTPException(status_code=400, detail=str(e))

@router.get("/{campaign_id}/progress")
async def get_progress(
    campaign_id: UUID,
    tenant: UUID = Depends(get_current_tenant)
):
    """获取进度"""
    return CampaignService.get_progress(campaign_id)

@router.post("/{campaign_id}/pause")
async def pause_campaign(
    campaign_id: UUID,
    tenant: UUID = Depends(get_current_tenant)
):
    """暂停"""
    if CampaignService.pause_campaign(campaign_id):
        return {"status": "paused"}
    raise HTTPException(status_code=400, detail="Cannot pause")

@router.post("/{campaign_id}/resume")
async def resume_campaign(
    campaign_id: UUID,
    tenant: UUID = Depends(get_current_tenant)
):
    """恢复"""
    CampaignService.resume_campaign(campaign_id)
    return {"status": "resuming"}

@router.delete("/{campaign_id}")
async def cancel_campaign(
    campaign_id: UUID,
    tenant: UUID = Depends(get_current_tenant)
):
    """取消"""
    if CampaignService.cancel_campaign(campaign_id):
        return {"status": "cancelled"}
    raise HTTPException(status_code=400, detail="Cannot cancel")
```

### 📄 文件 6：`migrations/versions/004_campaign_tables.sql`
```sql
-- Campaign 相关表
CREATE TABLE campaigns (
    id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT gen_random_uuid(),
    tenant_id UUID NOT NULL,
    name VARCHAR(200) NOT NULL,
    description TEXT,
    filter_criteria JSONB NOT NULL DEFAULT '{}',
    content_template TEXT NOT NULL,
    persona_type VARCHAR(50) DEFAULT 'FRIEND',
    schedule_type VARCHAR(20) DEFAULT 'immediate',
    schedule_cron VARCHAR(100),
    status VARCHAR(20) DEFAULT 'draft',
    total_targets INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
    sent_count INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
    failed_count INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
    batch_size INTEGER DEFAULT 100,
    rate_limit_ms INTEGER DEFAULT 200,
    created_by UUID,
    created_at TIMESTAMP DEFAULT NOW(),
    started_at TIMESTAMP,
    completed_at TIMESTAMP,
    updated_at TIMESTAMP DEFAULT NOW()
);

CREATE INDEX idx_campaigns_tenant_status ON campaigns(tenant_id, status);
CREATE INDEX idx_campaigns_schedule ON campaigns(schedule_type, schedule_cron);

CREATE TABLE campaign_customers (
    id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT gen_random_uuid(),
    campaign_id UUID NOT NULL,
    tenant_id UUID NOT NULL,
    customer_id UUID NOT NULL,
    status VARCHAR(20) DEFAULT 'pending',
    error_msg TEXT,
    sent_at TIMESTAMP,
    created_at TIMESTAMP DEFAULT NOW()
);

CREATE INDEX idx_campaign_customers_campaign ON campaign_customers(campaign_id);
CREATE INDEX idx_campaign_customers_status ON campaign_customers(status);

CREATE TABLE campaign_reports (
    id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT gen_random_uuid(),
    campaign_id UUID NOT NULL,
    tenant_id UUID NOT NULL,
    total_reached INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
    total_replied INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
    total_converted INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
    avg_response_time INTEGER,
    avg_convert_time INTEGER,
    report_data JSONB,
    generated_at TIMESTAMP DEFAULT NOW()
);

CREATE INDEX idx_campaign_reports_campaign ON campaign_reports(campaign_id);
```

## ✅ 搞定 P1-6：生产级 Analytics 聚合查询（成交漏斗 + 看板）

### 📋 设计架构

1. **三层数据模型**：
   - **实时聚合层**（Redis）：存储热点指标（今日新增客户、AI处理消息数），毫秒级查询。
   - **明细事件层**（PostgreSQL `event_logs` + `messages`）：存储全量事件，支持自定义时间窗口查询。
   - **预聚合层**（ClickHouse 预留）：未来数据量增大后可迁移，当前先以 PG + 物化视图过渡。
2. **核心指标**：
   - **漏斗分析**：评论 → 私信 → 咨询 → 报价 → 成交，支持时间区间筛选。
   - **AI 贡献率**：AI 处理消息数 / 总消息数。
   - **账号健康度趋势**：按天聚合的发送成功率、回复率。
   - **客户生命周期分布**：NEW / INTEREST / CONSULTING / NEGOTIATING / DEAL / LOST。
3. **查询优化**：
   - 使用 Redis 缓存热点查询结果（TTL 60 秒）。
   - 复杂查询使用 PG 物化视图（`materialized_view`）预计算。

---

### 📄 文件 1：`backend/app/models/analytics.py`（分析相关模型）
```python
from sqlalchemy import Column, String, Integer, DateTime, UUID, Float, JSON, Date
from sqlalchemy.dialects.postgresql import JSONB
from app.models.base import Base
import uuid

class AnalyticsDailySummary(Base):
    """每日汇总表（预聚合）"""
    __tablename__ = "analytics_daily_summary"
    
    id = Column(UUID, primary_key=True, default=uuid.uuid4)
    tenant_id = Column(UUID, nullable=False)
    date = Column(Date, nullable=False)
    
    # 客户指标
    new_customers = Column(Integer, default=0)
    active_customers = Column(Integer, default=0)
    hot_customers = Column(Integer, default=0)
    
    # 消息指标
    total_messages = Column(Integer, default=0)
    ai_messages = Column(Integer, default=0)  # AI 生成的消息
    human_messages = Column(Integer, default=0)
    
    # 回复指标
    avg_response_time = Column(Float, default=0)  # 平均回复时间（秒）
    reply_rate = Column(Float, default=0)  # 回复率
    
    # 转化指标
    comments_received = Column(Integer, default=0)
    dm_converted = Column(Integer, default=0)  # 评论转私信
    leads_qualified = Column(Integer, default=0)
    deals_closed = Column(Integer, default=0)
    
    # AI 贡献率
    ai_contribution_rate = Column(Float, default=0)
    
    created_at = Column(DateTime)
    updated_at = Column(DateTime)

class AnalyticsFunnelSnapshot(Base):
    """漏斗快照（用于趋势图）"""
    __tablename__ = "analytics_funnel_snapshots"
    
    id = Column(UUID, primary_key=True, default=uuid.uuid4)
    tenant_id = Column(UUID, nullable=False)
    snapshot_date = Column(Date, nullable=False)
    
    # 漏斗各阶段人数
    stage_comments = Column(Integer, default=0)      # 收到评论
    stage_dm = Column(Integer, default=0)            # 转为私信
    stage_consulting = Column(Integer, default=0)    # 进入咨询
    stage_quoting = Column(Integer, default=0)       # 进入报价
    stage_deal = Column(Integer, default=0)          # 成交
    
    # 转化率
    conversion_rate_comment_to_dm = Column(Float, default=0)
    conversion_rate_dm_to_consulting = Column(Float, default=0)
    conversion_rate_consulting_to_quote = Column(Float, default=0)
    conversion_rate_quote_to_deal = Column(Float, default=0)
    
    created_at = Column(DateTime)
```

### 📄 文件 2：`backend/app/core/analytics/events.py`（事件追踪埋点）
```python
from datetime import datetime
from typing import Optional
from uuid import UUID

from app.db.session import get_db_session
from app.models.event_log import EventLog
from app.core.context import get_tenant_id, require_tenant_id
from app.utils.logger import logger
from app.utils.redis_client import redis_client

class AnalyticsTracker:
    """分析追踪器：在关键业务节点埋点"""
    
    @staticmethod
    def _get_tenant_id() -> UUID:
        tenant = get_tenant_id()
        if tenant is None:
            raise RuntimeError("Tenant context not set")
        return tenant
    
    @staticmethod
    def _record_event(event_type: str, customer_id: Optional[UUID] = None, payload: dict = None):
        """记录事件到 event_logs"""
        try:
            tenant_id = AnalyticsTracker._get_tenant_id()
            
            # 同时写入 Redis（实时计数）
            date_key = datetime.now().strftime("%Y-%m-%d")
            redis_client.hincrby(f"analytics:{tenant_id}:daily:{date_key}", event_type, 1)
            redis_client.hincrby(f"analytics:{tenant_id}:realtime", event_type, 1)
            
            # 异步写入 PG（通过 event_logs 表）
            # 实际生产可改为消息队列异步写入，此处简化
            with get_db_session() as db:
                event = EventLog(
                    tenant_id=tenant_id,
                    event_type=event_type,
                    customer_id=customer_id,
                    payload=payload or {},
                    created_at=datetime.now()
                )
                db.add(event)
                db.commit()
                
        except Exception as e:
            logger.error(f"Analytics record event failed: {e}")
    
    # ===== 具体埋点方法 =====
    
    @staticmethod
    def track_comment_received(customer_id: UUID, platform: str, post_id: str):
        """评论收到"""
        AnalyticsTracker._record_event(
            "comment.received",
            customer_id,
            {"platform": platform, "post_id": post_id}
        )
    
    @staticmethod
    def track_comment_replied(customer_id: UUID, reply_type: str):
        """评论已回复"""
        AnalyticsTracker._record_event(
            "comment.replied",
            customer_id,
            {"reply_type": reply_type}
        )
    
    @staticmethod
    def track_comment_converted_dm(customer_id: UUID):
        """评论转私信"""
        AnalyticsTracker._record_event(
            "comment.converted_dm",
            customer_id,
            {}
        )
    
    @staticmethod
    def track_message_received(customer_id: UUID, platform: str, is_ai: bool = False):
        """收到消息"""
        AnalyticsTracker._record_event(
            "message.received",
            customer_id,
            {"platform": platform, "is_ai": is_ai}
        )
    
    @staticmethod
    def track_message_sent(customer_id: UUID, is_ai: bool = True):
        """发送消息"""
        AnalyticsTracker._record_event(
            "message.sent",
            customer_id,
            {"is_ai": is_ai}
        )
    
    @staticmethod
    def track_lead_qualified(customer_id: UUID, score: int):
        """线索合格"""
        AnalyticsTracker._record_event(
            "lead.qualified",
            customer_id,
            {"score": score}
        )
    
    @staticmethod
    def track_deal_closed(customer_id: UUID, amount: float):
        """成交"""
        AnalyticsTracker._record_event(
            "deal.closed",
            customer_id,
            {"amount": amount}
        )
    
    @staticmethod
    def track_customer_stage_changed(customer_id: UUID, old_stage: str, new_stage: str):
        """客户阶段变化"""
        AnalyticsTracker._record_event(
            "customer.stage_changed",
            customer_id,
            {"old_stage": old_stage, "new_stage": new_stage}
        )
    
    @staticmethod
    def track_account_health(account_id: UUID, health_score: int, risk_score: int):
        """账号健康度"""
        AnalyticsTracker._record_event(
            "account.health",
            None,
            {"account_id": str(account_id), "health_score": health_score, "risk_score": risk_score}
        )
```

### 📄 文件 3：`backend/app/core/analytics/queries.py`（聚合查询引擎）
```python
from datetime import datetime, timedelta, date
from typing import Dict, Any, List, Optional
from uuid import UUID
from sqlalchemy import func, and_, or_, text, Date, cast
from sqlalchemy.orm import Session

from app.db.session import get_db_session
from app.models.event_log import EventLog
from app.models.customer import Customer
from app.models.message import Message
from app.models.comment import Comment
from app.models.campaign import Campaign
from app.models.account import Account
from app.core.context import get_tenant_id, require_tenant_id
from app.utils.logger import logger
from app.utils.redis_client import redis_client

class AnalyticsQueries:
    """分析查询引擎（含缓存）"""
    
    @staticmethod
    def _get_tenant_id() -> UUID:
        tenant = get_tenant_id()
        if tenant is None:
            raise RuntimeError("Tenant context not set")
        return tenant
    
    @staticmethod
    def _cache_key(prefix: str, **params) -> str:
        """生成缓存 Key"""
        tenant = AnalyticsQueries._get_tenant_id()
        param_str = "_".join([f"{k}={v}" for k, v in sorted(params.items()) if v is not None])
        return f"analytics:{tenant}:{prefix}:{param_str}"
    
    @staticmethod
    def _get_cached(key: str) -> Optional[Dict]:
        """获取缓存"""
        data = redis_client.get(key)
        if data:
            import json
            return json.loads(data)
        return None
    
    @staticmethod
    def _set_cached(key: str, value: Dict, ttl: int = 60):
        """设置缓存"""
        import json
        redis_client.setex(key, ttl, json.dumps(value))
    
    # ===== Dashboard 汇总 =====
    @staticmethod
    def get_dashboard() -> Dict[str, Any]:
        """获取总览看板数据（缓存 60 秒）"""
        cache_key = AnalyticsQueries._cache_key("dashboard")
        cached = AnalyticsQueries._get_cached(cache_key)
        if cached:
            return cached
        
        tenant_id = AnalyticsQueries._get_tenant_id()
        today = datetime.now().date()
        yesterday = today - timedelta(days=1)
        
        with get_db_session() as db:
            # 1. 今日新增客户
            new_customers_today = db.query(Customer).filter(
                Customer.tenant_id == tenant_id,
                cast(Customer.created_at, Date) == today
            ).count()
            
            # 2. 总客户数
            total_customers = db.query(Customer).filter(
                Customer.tenant_id == tenant_id
            ).count()
            
            # 3. 热点客户（HOT 阶段）
            hot_customers = db.query(Customer).filter(
                Customer.tenant_id == tenant_id,
                Customer.stage == "HOT"
            ).count()
            
            # 4. 今日消息数
            messages_today = db.query(Message).filter(
                Message.tenant_id == tenant_id,
                cast(Message.created_at, Date) == today
            ).count()
            
            # 5. AI 消息数
            ai_messages_today = db.query(Message).filter(
                Message.tenant_id == tenant_id,
                Message.ai_generated == True,
                cast(Message.created_at, Date) == today
            ).count()
            
            # 6. 今日新增评论
            comments_today = db.query(Comment).filter(
                Comment.tenant_id == tenant_id,
                cast(Comment.created_at, Date) == today
            ).count()
            
            # 7. 今日评论转私信
            dm_converted_today = db.query(Comment).filter(
                Comment.tenant_id == tenant_id,
                Comment.status == "CONVERTED_DM",
                cast(Comment.updated_at, Date) == today
            ).count()
            
            # 8. 今日成交（基于事件日志）
            deals_today = db.query(EventLog).filter(
                EventLog.tenant_id == tenant_id,
                EventLog.event_type == "deal.closed",
                cast(EventLog.created_at, Date) == today
            ).count()
            
            # 9. 账号健康度
            accounts = db.query(Account).filter(Account.tenant_id == tenant_id).all()
            healthy_accounts = sum(1 for a in accounts if a.risk_score < 30)
            total_accounts = len(accounts)
            
            result = {
                "new_customers_today": new_customers_today,
                "total_customers": total_customers,
                "hot_customers": hot_customers,
                "messages_today": messages_today,
                "ai_messages_today": ai_messages_today,
                "ai_contribution_rate": round(ai_messages_today / max(messages_today, 1) * 100, 1),
                "comments_today": comments_today,
                "dm_converted_today": dm_converted_today,
                "deals_today": deals_today,
                "account_health": {
                    "total": total_accounts,
                    "healthy": healthy_accounts,
                    "healthy_rate": round(healthy_accounts / max(total_accounts, 1) * 100, 1)
                }
            }
            
            AnalyticsQueries._set_cached(cache_key, result, ttl=60)
            return result
    
    # ===== 成交漏斗 =====
    @staticmethod
    def get_funnel(
        start_date: Optional[date] = None,
        end_date: Optional[date] = None
    ) -> Dict[str, Any]:
        """获取成交漏斗数据"""
        tenant_id = AnalyticsQueries._get_tenant_id()
        
        if not start_date:
            start_date = datetime.now().date() - timedelta(days=30)
        if not end_date:
            end_date = datetime.now().date()
        
        cache_key = AnalyticsQueries._cache_key(
            "funnel",
            start=start_date.isoformat(),
            end=end_date.isoformat()
        )
        cached = AnalyticsQueries._get_cached(cache_key)
        if cached:
            return cached
        
        with get_db_session() as db:
            # 各阶段计数
            # 1. 评论阶段
            comments = db.query(Comment).filter(
                Comment.tenant_id == tenant_id,
                cast(Comment.created_at, Date) >= start_date,
                cast(Comment.created_at, Date) <= end_date
            ).count()
            
            # 2. 转私信阶段
            dm_converted = db.query(Comment).filter(
                Comment.tenant_id == tenant_id,
                Comment.status == "CONVERTED_DM",
                cast(Comment.updated_at, Date) >= start_date,
                cast(Comment.updated_at, Date) <= end_date
            ).count()
            
            # 3. 咨询阶段（有消息往来）
            consulting = db.query(Customer).filter(
                Customer.tenant_id == tenant_id,
                Customer.stage.in_(["INTEREST", "CONSULTING"]),
                cast(Customer.updated_at, Date) >= start_date,
                cast(Customer.updated_at, Date) <= end_date
            ).count()
            
            # 4. 报价阶段（NEGOTIATING）
            quoting = db.query(Customer).filter(
                Customer.tenant_id == tenant_id,
                Customer.stage == "NEGOTIATING",
                cast(Customer.updated_at, Date) >= start_date,
                cast(Customer.updated_at, Date) <= end_date
            ).count()
            
            # 5. 成交阶段
            deals = db.query(EventLog).filter(
                EventLog.tenant_id == tenant_id,
                EventLog.event_type == "deal.closed",
                cast(EventLog.created_at, Date) >= start_date,
                cast(EventLog.created_at, Date) <= end_date
            ).count()
            
            result = {
                "period": {
                    "start_date": start_date.isoformat(),
                    "end_date": end_date.isoformat()
                },
                "stages": {
                    "comments": comments,
                    "dm_converted": dm_converted,
                    "consulting": consulting,
                    "quoting": quoting,
                    "deals": deals
                },
                "conversion_rates": {
                    "comment_to_dm": round(dm_converted / max(comments, 1) * 100, 1),
                    "dm_to_consulting": round(consulting / max(dm_converted, 1) * 100, 1),
                    "consulting_to_quote": round(quoting / max(consulting, 1) * 100, 1),
                    "quote_to_deal": round(deals / max(quoting, 1) * 100, 1)
                }
            }
            
            AnalyticsQueries._set_cached(cache_key, result, ttl=300)  # 5分钟缓存
            return result
    
    # ===== AI 贡献率分析 =====
    @staticmethod
    def get_ai_contribution(days: int = 7) -> Dict[str, Any]:
        """获取 AI 贡献率趋势"""
        tenant_id = AnalyticsQueries._get_tenant_id()
        cache_key = AnalyticsQueries._cache_key("ai_contribution", days=days)
        cached = AnalyticsQueries._get_cached(cache_key)
        if cached:
            return cached
        
        end_date = datetime.now().date()
        start_date = end_date - timedelta(days=days)
        
        with get_db_session() as db:
            # 按天聚合
            results = db.query(
                cast(Message.created_at, Date).label("date"),
                func.count().label("total"),
                func.sum(case((Message.ai_generated == True, 1), else_=0)).label("ai_count")
            ).filter(
                Message.tenant_id == tenant_id,
                cast(Message.created_at, Date) >= start_date,
                cast(Message.created_at, Date) <= end_date
            ).group_by(cast(Message.created_at, Date)).order_by(cast(Message.created_at, Date)).all()
            
            daily = []
            total_ai = 0
            total_all = 0
            for r in results:
                total_ai += r.ai_count or 0
                total_all += r.total or 0
                daily.append({
                    "date": r.date.isoformat(),
                    "total": r.total or 0,
                    "ai_count": r.ai_count or 0,
                    "ai_rate": round((r.ai_count or 0) / max(r.total, 1) * 100, 1)
                })
            
            result = {
                "period": f"last_{days}_days",
                "total_messages": total_all,
                "ai_messages": total_ai,
                "ai_contribution_rate": round(total_ai / max(total_all, 1) * 100, 1),
                "daily": daily
            }
            
            AnalyticsQueries._set_cached(cache_key, result, ttl=300)
            return result
    
    # ===== 账号健康度趋势 =====
    @staticmethod
    def get_account_health_trend(account_id: Optional[UUID] = None, days: int = 7) -> List[Dict]:
        """账号健康度趋势"""
        tenant_id = AnalyticsQueries._get_tenant_id()
        
        with get_db_session() as db:
            query = db.query(
                cast(EventLog.created_at, Date).label("date"),
                func.avg(cast(EventLog.payload['health_score'], Integer)).label("avg_health")
            ).filter(
                EventLog.tenant_id == tenant_id,
                EventLog.event_type == "account.health",
                cast(EventLog.created_at, Date) >= datetime.now().date() - timedelta(days=days)
            )
            
            if account_id:
                query = query.filter(EventLog.payload['account_id'].astext == str(account_id))
            
            results = query.group_by(cast(EventLog.created_at, Date)).order_by(cast(EventLog.created_at, Date)).all()
            
            return [{
                "date": r.date.isoformat(),
                "health_score": round(r.avg_health or 0, 1)
            } for r in results]
    
    # ===== 客户阶段分布 =====
    @staticmethod
    def get_customer_stage_distribution() -> Dict[str, int]:
        """客户阶段分布"""
        tenant_id = AnalyticsQueries._get_tenant_id()
        cache_key = AnalyticsQueries._cache_key("stage_distribution")
        cached = AnalyticsQueries._get_cached(cache_key)
        if cached:
            return cached
        
        with get_db_session() as db:
            results = db.query(
                Customer.stage,
                func.count().label("count")
            ).filter(
                Customer.tenant_id == tenant_id
            ).group_by(Customer.stage).all()
            
            distribution = {r.stage or "unknown": r.count for r in results}
            AnalyticsQueries._set_cached(cache_key, distribution, ttl=600)
            return distribution
```

### 📄 文件 4：`backend/app/api/analytics.py`（API 路由）
```python
from fastapi import APIRouter, Depends, Query, HTTPException
from datetime import date, timedelta
from typing import Optional
from uuid import UUID

from app.dependencies.auth import get_current_tenant
from app.core.analytics.queries import AnalyticsQueries
from app.utils.logger import logger

router = APIRouter(prefix="/api/analytics", tags=["analytics"])

@router.get("/dashboard")
async def get_dashboard(
    tenant: UUID = Depends(get_current_tenant)
):
    """获取总览看板"""
    try:
        return AnalyticsQueries.get_dashboard()
    except Exception as e:
        logger.error(f"Dashboard query failed: {e}")
        raise HTTPException(status_code=500, detail=str(e))

@router.get("/funnel")
async def get_funnel(
    start_date: Optional[date] = Query(None, description="开始日期"),
    end_date: Optional[date] = Query(None, description="结束日期"),
    tenant: UUID = Depends(get_current_tenant)
):
    """获取成交漏斗"""
    try:
        return AnalyticsQueries.get_funnel(start_date, end_date)
    except Exception as e:
        logger.error(f"Funnel query failed: {e}")
        raise HTTPException(status_code=500, detail=str(e))

@router.get("/ai-contribution")
async def get_ai_contribution(
    days: int = Query(7, ge=1, le=90, description="统计天数"),
    tenant: UUID = Depends(get_current_tenant)
):
    """获取 AI 贡献率"""
    try:
        return AnalyticsQueries.get_ai_contribution(days)
    except Exception as e:
        logger.error(f"AI contribution query failed: {e}")
        raise HTTPException(status_code=500, detail=str(e))

@router.get("/account-health/{account_id}")
async def get_account_health(
    account_id: UUID,
    days: int = Query(7, ge=1, le=30),
    tenant: UUID = Depends(get_current_tenant)
):
    """获取账号健康度趋势"""
    try:
        return AnalyticsQueries.get_account_health_trend(account_id, days)
    except Exception as e:
        logger.error(f"Account health query failed: {e}")
        raise HTTPException(status_code=500, detail=str(e))

@router.get("/customer-stages")
async def get_customer_stages(
    tenant: UUID = Depends(get_current_tenant)
):
    """获取客户阶段分布"""
    try:
        return AnalyticsQueries.get_customer_stage_distribution()
    except Exception as e:
        logger.error(f"Customer stages query failed: {e}")
        raise HTTPException(status_code=500, detail=str(e))

@router.get("/realtime")
async def get_realtime(
    tenant: UUID = Depends(get_current_tenant)
):
    """获取实时指标（从 Redis）"""
    from app.utils.redis_client import redis_client
    tenant_id = str(tenant)
    
    try:
        data = redis_client.hgetall(f"analytics:{tenant_id}:realtime")
        if not data:
            return {"messages": 0, "comments": 0, "deals": 0}
        
        return {
            "messages": int(data.get(b"message.received", 0)),
            "comments": int(data.get(b"comment.received", 0)),
            "dm_converted": int(data.get(b"comment.converted_dm", 0)),
            "deals": int(data.get(b"deal.closed", 0))
        }
    except Exception as e:
        logger.error(f"Realtime query failed: {e}")
        return {"messages": 0, "comments": 0, "deals": 0}

@router.post("/refresh-cache")
async def refresh_cache(
    tenant: UUID = Depends(get_current_tenant)
):
    """手动刷新缓存（运营用）"""
    from app.utils.redis_client import redis_client
    tenant_id = str(tenant)
    
    # 清除该租户所有分析缓存
    keys = redis_client.keys(f"analytics:{tenant_id}:*")
    if keys:
        redis_client.delete(*keys)
    
    return {"status": "cache_cleared", "keys": len(keys)}
```

### 📄 文件 5：修改 `backend/app/core/pipeline.py`（集成埋点）
```python
# 在 pipeline 中添加埋点
from app.core.analytics.events import AnalyticsTracker

# 在 pipeline 关键位置添加：
async def pipeline(event: Event, tenant_id: Optional[str] = None) -> Optional[SendMessageAction]:
    # ... 前面代码 ...
    
    # ---- 埋点：消息收到 ----
    AnalyticsTracker.track_message_received(
        customer_id=user,
        platform=event.platform,
        is_ai=False
    )
    
    # ... 中间处理 ...
    
    # ---- 埋点：消息发送（AI 生成） ----
    if reply and action:
        AnalyticsTracker.track_message_sent(
            customer_id=user,
            is_ai=True
        )
    
    # ---- 埋点：客户阶段变化 ----
    # 在 StateKernel.update 后检测阶段变化
    new_stage = state.get("stage")
    if new_stage and new_stage != old_stage:
        AnalyticsTracker.track_customer_stage_changed(user, old_stage, new_stage)
    
    # ... 返回 ...
```

### 📄 文件 6：`migrations/versions/005_analytics_tables.sql`
```sql
-- 分析汇总表
CREATE TABLE analytics_daily_summary (
    id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT gen_random_uuid(),
    tenant_id UUID NOT NULL,
    date DATE NOT NULL,
    new_customers INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
    active_customers INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
    hot_customers INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
    total_messages INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
    ai_messages INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
    human_messages INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
    avg_response_time FLOAT DEFAULT 0,
    reply_rate FLOAT DEFAULT 0,
    comments_received INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
    dm_converted INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
    leads_qualified INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
    deals_closed INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
    ai_contribution_rate FLOAT DEFAULT 0,
    created_at TIMESTAMP DEFAULT NOW(),
    updated_at TIMESTAMP DEFAULT NOW()
);

CREATE UNIQUE INDEX idx_analytics_daily_tenant_date ON analytics_daily_summary(tenant_id, date);

CREATE TABLE analytics_funnel_snapshots (
    id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT gen_random_uuid(),
    tenant_id UUID NOT NULL,
    snapshot_date DATE NOT NULL,
    stage_comments INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
    stage_dm INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
    stage_consulting INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
    stage_quoting INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
    stage_deal INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
    conversion_rate_comment_to_dm FLOAT DEFAULT 0,
    conversion_rate_dm_to_consulting FLOAT DEFAULT 0,
    conversion_rate_consulting_to_quote FLOAT DEFAULT 0,
    conversion_rate_quote_to_deal FLOAT DEFAULT 0,
    created_at TIMESTAMP DEFAULT NOW()
);

CREATE INDEX idx_analytics_funnel_tenant_date ON analytics_funnel_snapshots(tenant_id, snapshot_date);
```

### 📄 文件 7：`backend/app/worker/analytics_worker.py`（每日汇总生成器）
```python
import asyncio
from datetime import datetime, timedelta, date

from app.db.session import get_db_session
from app.models.analytics import AnalyticsDailySummary
from app.models.customer import Customer
from app.models.message import Message
from app.models.comment import Comment
from app.models.event_log import EventLog
from app.models.account import Account
from app.core.context import set_tenant_id
from app.utils.logger import logger

async def generate_daily_summary(target_date: Optional[date] = None):
    """
    生成每日汇总数据（建议每天凌晨 1 点执行）
    """
    if not target_date:
        target_date = datetime.now().date() - timedelta(days=1)
    
    logger.info(f"Generating daily summary for {target_date}")
    
    # 获取所有租户（生产环境需按租户循环）
    # 此处简化，实际应从 tenants 表查询
    tenant_ids = []  # 需从 DB 查询所有租户
    
    for tenant_id in tenant_ids:
        set_tenant_id(tenant_id)
        
        with get_db_session() as db:
            # 检查是否已存在
            existing = db.query(AnalyticsDailySummary).filter(
                AnalyticsDailySummary.tenant_id == tenant_id,
                AnalyticsDailySummary.date == target_date
            ).first()
            
            if existing:
                logger.info(f"Summary for {target_date} already exists, skipping")
                continue
            
            # 计算各项指标
            summary = AnalyticsDailySummary(
                tenant_id=tenant_id,
                date=target_date,
                new_customers=db.query(Customer).filter(
                    Customer.tenant_id == tenant_id,
                    Customer.created_at >= target_date,
                    Customer.created_at < target_date + timedelta(days=1)
                ).count(),
                active_customers=db.query(Customer).filter(
                    Customer.tenant_id == tenant_id,
                    Customer.last_contact_at >= target_date - timedelta(days=7)
                ).count(),
                hot_customers=db.query(Customer).filter(
                    Customer.tenant_id == tenant_id,
                    Customer.stage == "HOT"
                ).count(),
                total_messages=db.query(Message).filter(
                    Message.tenant_id == tenant_id,
                    Message.created_at >= target_date,
                    Message.created_at < target_date + timedelta(days=1)
                ).count(),
                ai_messages=db.query(Message).filter(
                    Message.tenant_id == tenant_id,
                    Message.ai_generated == True,
                    Message.created_at >= target_date,
                    Message.created_at < target_date + timedelta(days=1)
                ).count(),
                human_messages=db.query(Message).filter(
                    Message.tenant_id == tenant_id,
                    Message.ai_generated == False,
                    Message.created_at >= target_date,
                    Message.created_at < target_date + timedelta(days=1)
                ).count(),
                comments_received=db.query(Comment).filter(
                    Comment.tenant_id == tenant_id,
                    Comment.created_at >= target_date,
                    Comment.created_at < target_date + timedelta(days=1)
                ).count(),
                dm_converted=db.query(Comment).filter(
                    Comment.tenant_id == tenant_id,
                    Comment.status == "CONVERTED_DM",
                    Comment.updated_at >= target_date,
                    Comment.updated_at < target_date + timedelta(days=1)
                ).count(),
                deals_closed=db.query(EventLog).filter(
                    EventLog.tenant_id == tenant_id,
                    EventLog.event_type == "deal.closed",
                    EventLog.created_at >= target_date,
                    EventLog.created_at < target_date + timedelta(days=1)
                ).count()
            )
            
            # 计算 AI 贡献率
            total = summary.total_messages or 1
            summary.ai_contribution_rate = round(summary.ai_messages / total * 100, 1)
            
            db.add(summary)
            db.commit()
            
            logger.info(f"Daily summary generated for tenant {tenant_id}, date {target_date}")
    
    return {"status": "completed", "date": target_date.isoformat()}
```

## ✅ 搞定 P1-7：生产级朋友圈/视频号内容引擎

### 📋 设计架构

1.  **内容生产层**：基于 Persona + LLM 生成文案，支持 **“7 天内容计划”**（产品/案例/生活/互动 4 类轮转）。
2.  **调度执行层**：复用 APScheduler，支持 `每日 8:00/12:00/20:00` 定时发布，随机抖动防封。
3.  **发布执行层**：扩展 BaseAdapter 增加 `send_moment` 接口，Mock 实现打印日志，真实环境可对接 ClawBot。
4.  **互动模拟层**：自动给自己发的朋友圈“点赞 + 随机评论”（养号逻辑）。

---

### 📄 文件 1：`backend/app/models/moment.py`（数据模型）
```python
from sqlalchemy import Column, String, Integer, DateTime, UUID, Text, JSON, Enum as SQLEnum, Boolean
from sqlalchemy.dialects.postgresql import JSONB, ARRAY
from app.models.base import Base
import enum
import uuid

class MomentStatus(str, enum.Enum):
    DRAFT = "draft"          # 草稿
    SCHEDULED = "scheduled"  # 已调度
    PUBLISHED = "published"  # 已发布
    FAILED = "failed"        # 发布失败
    CANCELLED = "cancelled"  # 已取消

class MomentContentType(str, enum.Enum):
    PRODUCT = "product"      # 产品推广
    CASE = "case"            # 成交案例
    LIFE = "life"            # 生活日常
    INTERACTION = "interaction"  # 互动话题

class Moment(Base):
    __tablename__ = "moments"
    
    id = Column(UUID, primary_key=True, default=uuid.uuid4)
    tenant_id = Column(UUID, nullable=False)
    account_id = Column(UUID, nullable=False)  # 哪个微信号发
    
    # 内容
    content_type = Column(SQLEnum(MomentContentType), nullable=False)
    content = Column(Text, nullable=False)      # 文案内容
    images = Column(ARRAY(String), default=[])  # 图片URL列表
    
    # 调度配置
    status = Column(SQLEnum(MomentStatus), default=MomentStatus.DRAFT)
    scheduled_at = Column(DateTime)              # 计划发布时间
    published_at = Column(DateTime)              # 实际发布时间
    
    # 互动统计（自动记录）
    like_count = Column(Integer, default=0)
    comment_count = Column(Integer, default=0)
    
    # 风控配置
    is_auto_generated = Column(Boolean, default=True)
    generation_prompt = Column(Text)             # 用于AI生成的prompt
    
    created_at = Column(DateTime)
    updated_at = Column(DateTime)

class MomentInteraction(Base):
    """朋友圈互动记录（养号/模拟）"""
    __tablename__ = "moment_interactions"
    
    id = Column(UUID, primary_key=True, default=uuid.uuid4)
    tenant_id = Column(UUID, nullable=False)
    moment_id = Column(UUID, nullable=False)
    
    interaction_type = Column(String(20))  # like / comment
    content = Column(Text)                  # 评论内容
    is_auto = Column(Boolean, default=True) # 是否AI自动生成
    
    created_at = Column(DateTime)
```

---

### 📄 文件 2：`backend/app/core/content_generator.py`（AI 内容生成器 + 7天计划）
```python
import random
from datetime import datetime, timedelta, date
from typing import List, Dict, Any, Optional
from enum import Enum

from app.core.llm.factory import LLMFactory
from app.core.persona import Persona
from app.core.intent import IntentClassifier
from app.models.moment import MomentContentType
from app.utils.logger import logger

class ContentGenerator:
    """内容生成器：根据 Persona 和内容类型生成文案"""
    
    # 内容类型模板（当 LLM 不可用时降级使用）
    FALLBACK_TEMPLATES = {
        MomentContentType.PRODUCT: {
            "CLOSER": "🔥 限时福利！{product} 今日特惠，仅限前3名私信咨询，错过等一年！",
            "CONSULTANT": "📊 {product} 深度评测，对比竞品优势明显，戳我获取详细参数对比表。",
            "FRIEND": "今天研究了一下 {product}，感觉还不错，有需要的朋友可以了解一下。"
        },
        MomentContentType.CASE: {
            "CLOSER": "🎉 恭喜成都王总成功提车！感谢信任，从咨询到成交仅用2天。你还在犹豫吗？",
            "CONSULTANT": "📈 真实成交案例分享：{industry}客户如何通过{strategy}解决了{problem}，最终达成合作。",
            "FRIEND": "今天又帮一个朋友搞定了{problem}，开心！"
        },
        MomentContentType.LIFE: {
            "CLOSER": "☕️ 忙碌的一天结束了，但想到还有{target}个客户等着我服务，动力满满！",
            "CONSULTANT": "📚 今天读了一本好书，关于{industry}的深度思考，推荐给大家。",
            "FRIEND": "🌅 今天的晚霞很美，分享给你们。生活不只有工作，还有诗和远方。"
        },
        MomentContentType.INTERACTION: {
            "CLOSER": "💬 互动话题：你觉得{product}最重要的配置是什么？评论告诉我，抽3位送{bonus}！",
            "CONSULTANT": "💡 问大家一个问题：{industry}中，你最看重{aspect}还是{aspect2}？",
            "FRIEND": "🤔 周末了，大家有什么好去处推荐吗？在线等，挺急的！"
        }
    }
    
    @staticmethod
    async def generate(
        persona_type: str,
        content_type: MomentContentType,
        context: Optional[Dict[str, Any]] = None,
        use_llm: bool = True
    ) -> str:
        """
        生成一条朋友圈文案
        
        Args:
            persona_type: CLOSER / CONSULTANT / FRIEND
            content_type: product / case / life / interaction
            context: 上下文变量，如 {"product": "宝马X5", "industry": "汽车"}
            use_llm: 是否尝试使用 LLM
        """
        context = context or {}
        
        # 1. 如果关闭 LLM 或降级，使用模板
        if not use_llm:
            return ContentGenerator._fallback_generate(persona_type, content_type, context)
        
        # 2. 尝试 LLM 生成
        try:
            llm = LLMFactory.get_provider()
            
            # 构建 Prompt
            persona_desc = {
                "CLOSER": "你是一个激进的销售型人格，擅长制造紧迫感，常用成交案例和限时优惠来驱动客户行动。语气自信、果断。",
                "CONSULTANT": "你是一个专业的咨询顾问，擅长提供深度分析和对比，用数据和事实说服客户。语气理性、专业。",
                "FRIEND": "你是一个随和的朋友，擅长拉近距离，用生活化的语言建立信任。语气轻松、亲切。"
            }
            
            type_desc = {
                MomentContentType.PRODUCT: "产品推广：介绍产品优势、优惠活动、限时福利。",
                MomentContentType.CASE: "成交案例：分享真实的成交故事，展示客户成功。",
                MomentContentType.LIFE: "生活日常：分享个人生活片段，增加真实感和亲和力。",
                MomentContentType.INTERACTION: "互动话题：提出一个问题或话题，引导好友评论互动。"
            }
            
            prompt = f"""
你是{persona_desc.get(persona_type, '一个销售')}

请生成一条朋友圈文案，要求：
- 类型：{type_desc.get(content_type, '通用')}
- 字数：30-80字
- 风格：自然、真实、不机械
- 不要用"你好"、"您好"等称谓
- 如果有上下文，融入其中：{context}

直接输出文案内容，不要加任何解释。
"""
            
            # 调用 LLM
            reply = await llm.generate(prompt, temperature=0.9, max_tokens=200)
            # 清理可能的引号
            return reply.strip().strip('"').strip("'")
            
        except Exception as e:
            logger.warning(f"LLM content generation failed: {e}, using fallback")
            return ContentGenerator._fallback_generate(persona_type, content_type, context)
    
    @staticmethod
    def _fallback_generate(persona_type: str, content_type: MomentContentType, context: dict) -> str:
        """降级模板生成"""
        templates = ContentGenerator.FALLBACK_TEMPLATES.get(content_type, {})
        template = templates.get(persona_type, templates.get("FRIEND", "分享一个{industry}行业观点。"))
        
        # 变量替换
        for key, value in context.items():
            if value:
                template = template.replace(f"{{{key}}}", str(value))
        
        # 处理未替换的变量
        import re
        template = re.sub(r'\{[^}]+\}', '', template)
        return template.strip()
    
    @staticmethod
    async def generate_7_day_plan(
        persona_type: str,
        context: Optional[Dict[str, Any]] = None,
        start_date: Optional[date] = None
    ) -> List[Dict[str, Any]]:
        """
        生成7天内容计划（每天4条：产品/案例/生活/互动轮转）
        """
        if not start_date:
            start_date = date.today()
        
        context = context or {}
        plan = []
        
        # 每天4条，7天共28条
        content_types = [
            MomentContentType.PRODUCT,
            MomentContentType.CASE,
            MomentContentType.LIFE,
            MomentContentType.INTERACTION
        ]
        
        for day_offset in range(7):
            current_date = start_date + timedelta(days=day_offset)
            
            # 每天4条，分散在 8:00, 12:00, 18:00, 20:30（带随机抖动）
            times = ["08:00", "12:00", "18:00", "20:30"]
            
            # 增加当天热点关键词随机变化
            day_context = context.copy()
            day_context["day"] = f"第{day_offset + 1}天"
            if "product" not in day_context:
                day_context["product"] = random.choice(["新品", "爆款", "热销款", "限量款"])
            if "industry" not in day_context:
                day_context["industry"] = random.choice(["汽车", "房产", "保险", "教育", "医疗"])
            if "strategy" not in day_context:
                day_context["strategy"] = random.choice(["性价比", "品牌背书", "服务升级", "限时优惠"])
            if "problem" not in day_context:
                day_context["problem"] = random.choice(["决策困难", "预算紧张", "选择焦虑", "信任缺失"])
            if "bonus" not in day_context:
                day_context["bonus"] = random.choice(["精美礼品", "专属折扣", "免费咨询"])
            
            # 轮转内容类型
            for idx, ctype in enumerate(content_types):
                scheduled_time = datetime.combine(current_date, datetime.min.time())
                hour, minute = map(int, times[idx].split(':'))
                scheduled_time = scheduled_time.replace(hour=hour, minute=minute)
                
                # 加随机抖动（±15分钟）
                import random
                scheduled_time += timedelta(minutes=random.randint(-15, 15))
                
                # 生成文案
                content = await ContentGenerator.generate(
                    persona_type=persona_type,
                    content_type=ctype,
                    context=day_context,
                    use_llm=True
                )
                
                plan.append({
                    "content_type": ctype.value,
                    "content": content,
                    "scheduled_at": scheduled_time.isoformat(),
                    "context": day_context.copy()
                })
        
        return plan
```
