### 📦 七、左侧：微信感知层（ContactList）

#### `frontend/src/modules/contacts/ContactList.tsx`
```tsx
import { useEffect } from 'react'
import { useCustomerStore } from '../../store/customerStore'
import { ContactCard } from './ContactCard'

interface ContactListProps {
  onSelectCustomer: (id: string) => void
  selectedId: string | null
}

export function ContactList({ onSelectCustomer, selectedId }: ContactListProps) {
  const { customers, isLoading, loadCustomers } = useCustomerStore()

  useEffect(() => {
    loadCustomers()
  }, [])

  if (isLoading) {
    return (
      <div className="p-4 text-white/40 text-sm">加载中...</div>
    )
  }

  return (
    <div className="h-full flex flex-col">
      {/* 标题 */}
      <div className="p-4 border-b border-white/5">
        <div className="flex items-center justify-between">
          <span className="text-sm font-semibold text-white/80">客户列表</span>
          <span className="text-xs text-white/30">{customers.length}</span>
        </div>
        <div className="mt-2 flex gap-1">
          {['全部', 'HOT', 'WARM', 'COLD'].map((tab) => (
            <button
              key={tab}
              className="text-xs px-2 py-0.5 rounded-full bg-white/5 text-white/50 hover:bg-white/10 transition"
            >
              {tab}
            </button>
          ))}
        </div>
      </div>

      {/* 列表 */}
      <div className="flex-1 overflow-y-auto p-2 space-y-1">
        {customers.map((customer) => (
          <ContactCard
            key={customer.id}
            customer={customer}
            selected={selectedId === customer.id}
            onClick={() => onSelectCustomer(customer.id)}
          />
        ))}
      </div>
    </div>
  )
}
```

#### `frontend/src/modules/contacts/ContactCard.tsx`
```tsx
import { motion } from 'framer-motion'
import { Customer } from '../../api/client'

interface ContactCardProps {
  customer: Customer
  selected: boolean
  onClick: () => void
}

const statusMap = {
  HOT: { label: 'HOT', color: 'text-red-400', dot: 'status-dot-hot' },
  WARM: { label: 'WARM', color: 'text-yellow-400', dot: 'status-dot-interest' },
  COLD: { label: 'COLD', color: 'text-gray-400', dot: 'status-dot-cold' },
  DEAL: { label: '成交', color: 'text-green-400', dot: 'status-dot-closed' },
  LOST: { label: '流失', color: 'text-red-300/50', dot: '' },
}

export function ContactCard({ customer, selected, onClick }: ContactCardProps) {
  const status = statusMap[customer.stage] || statusMap.COLD

  return (
    <motion.div
      whileHover={{ scale: 1.02 }}
      whileTap={{ scale: 0.98 }}
      className={`p-3 rounded-lg cursor-pointer transition-all ${
        selected
          ? 'bg-waos-primary/20 border border-waos-primary/30 shadow-lg shadow-waos-primary/10'
          : 'hover:bg-white/5 border border-transparent'
      }`}
      onClick={onClick}
    >
      <div className="flex items-center justify-between">
        <div className="flex items-center gap-3 min-w-0">
          <div className="w-8 h-8 rounded-full bg-white/10 flex items-center justify-center text-xs flex-shrink-0">
            {customer.name?.charAt(0) || '?'}
          </div>
          <div className="min-w-0">
            <div className="text-sm font-medium truncate">{customer.name || '未命名'}</div>
            <div className="flex items-center gap-2 text-xs text-white/40">
              <span>{customer.platform || '微信'}</span>
              {customer.tags?.slice(0, 2).map((tag) => (
                <span key={tag} className="bg-white/5 px-1.5 py-0.5 rounded text-[10px]">
                  {tag}
                </span>
              ))}
            </div>
          </div>
        </div>
        <div className="flex items-center gap-2 flex-shrink-0">
          <span className={`${status.color} text-xs font-medium`}>{status.label}</span>
          {status.dot && <span className={status.dot} />}
        </div>
      </div>
      {selected && (
        <div className="mt-2 text-xs text-white/40 border-t border-white/5 pt-2">
          评分: {customer.deal_score} · 最近活跃: {new Date(customer.updated_at).toLocaleDateString()}
        </div>
      )}
    </motion.div>
  )
}
```

### 📦 八、中间：行为执行层（ChatPanel）

#### `frontend/src/modules/chat/ChatPanel.tsx`
```tsx
import { useEffect, useRef } from 'react'
import { useChatStore } from '../../store/chatStore'
import { usePersonaStore } from '../../store/personaStore'
import { ChatWindow } from './ChatWindow'
import { ChatInput } from './ChatInput'
import { AISuggestionCard } from './AISuggestionCard'

interface ChatPanelProps {
  customerId: string | null
}

export function ChatPanel({ customerId }: ChatPanelProps) {
  const { messages, currentConversationId, setCurrentConversation, addMessage } =
    useChatStore()
  const { updateAnalytics } = usePersonaStore()
  const messagesEndRef = useRef<HTMLDivElement>(null)

  // 当客户切换时，加载对应的会话
  useEffect(() => {
    if (customerId) {
      // 实际应调用 API 获取会话 ID
      setCurrentConversation('conv_' + customerId)
    }
  }, [customerId])

  // 滚动到最新消息
  useEffect(() => {
    messagesEndRef.current?.scrollIntoView({ behavior: 'smooth' })
  }, [messages])

  // 模拟 AI 响应（实际由 WebSocket 驱动）
  const handleSendMessage = (content: string) => {
    // 添加用户消息（乐观更新）
    addMessage({
      id: `temp_${Date.now()}`,
      conversation_id: currentConversationId || '',
      sender_type: 'OPERATOR',
      content,
      ai_generated: false,
      created_at: new Date().toISOString(),
    })

    // 模拟 AI 响应
    setTimeout(() => {
      const aiReply = {
        id: `ai_${Date.now()}`,
        conversation_id: currentConversationId || '',
        sender_type: 'AI',
        content: '好的，我帮您处理这个问题。请问您需要什么帮助？',
        ai_generated: true,
        created_at: new Date().toISOString(),
      }
      addMessage(aiReply)

      // 更新 Persona 面板
      updateAnalytics(75, 62, [
        '用户意图 → 咨询',
        '情绪 → 中性',
        '策略 → 培育模式',
      ], ['发送案例', '发送对比'])
    }, 1000)
  }

  if (!customerId) {
    return (
      <div className="flex-1 flex items-center justify-center text-white/30 text-sm">
        请从左侧选择一个客户
      </div>
    )
  }

  return (
    <div className="flex-1 flex flex-col h-full">
      {/* 顶部客户信息 */}
      <div className="h-[52px] border-b border-white/10 px-4 flex items-center justify-between flex-shrink-0">
        <div className="flex items-center gap-3">
          <span className="font-medium">客户对话</span>
          <span className="text-xs text-white/40">ID: {customerId.slice(0, 8)}</span>
        </div>
        <div className="flex items-center gap-2 text-xs text-white/40">
          <span className="w-2 h-2 rounded-full bg-green-400 animate-pulse" />
          <span>活跃</span>
        </div>
      </div>

      {/* 消息区 */}
      <div className="flex-1 overflow-y-auto p-4 space-y-3">
        {messages.length === 0 ? (
          <div className="text-white/30 text-sm text-center py-8">
            暂无消息，开始对话吧
          </div>
        ) : (
          messages.map((msg) => (
            <ChatWindow key={msg.id} message={msg} />
          ))
        )}
        <div ref={messagesEndRef} />
      </div>

      {/* AI 建议卡片 */}
      <div className="px-4 pb-2 flex-shrink-0">
        <AISuggestionCard />
      </div>

      {/* 输入区 */}
      <div className="flex-shrink-0">
        <ChatInput onSend={handleSendMessage} />
      </div>
    </div>
  )
}
```

#### `frontend/src/modules/chat/ChatWindow.tsx`
```tsx
import { Message } from '../../api/client'

interface ChatWindowProps {
  message: Message
}

export function ChatWindow({ message }: ChatWindowProps) {
  const isAI = message.sender_type === 'AI'
  const isOperator = message.sender_type === 'OPERATOR'

  let bgColor = 'bg-white/10'
  let textColor = 'text-white'
  let align = 'justify-start'

  if (isAI) {
    bgColor = 'bg-gradient-to-r from-waos-primary/30 to-waos-accent/20 border border-waos-primary/20'
    textColor = 'text-white'
    align = 'justify-start'
  } else if (isOperator) {
    bgColor = 'bg-waos-primary/30 border border-waos-primary/20'
    textColor = 'text-white'
    align = 'justify-end'
  }

  return (
    <div className={`flex ${align}`}>
      <div
        className={`max-w-[75%] px-4 py-2.5 rounded-2xl ${bgColor} ${textColor} text-sm shadow-lg`}
      >
        <div className="text-[10px] text-white/30 mb-1">
          {isAI ? '🧠 AI' : isOperator ? '👤 你' : '👤 客户'}
        </div>
        <div className="whitespace-pre-wrap break-words">{message.content}</div>
        <div className="text-[10px] text-white/20 mt-1 text-right">
          {new Date(message.created_at).toLocaleTimeString()}
        </div>
      </div>
    </div>
  )
}
```

#### `frontend/src/modules/chat/ChatInput.tsx`
```tsx
import { useState, useCallback, useRef } from 'react'
import { debounce } from 'lodash'

interface ChatInputProps {
  onSend: (content: string) => void
  onSuggestion?: (text: string) => void
}

export function ChatInput({ onSend, onSuggestion }: ChatInputProps) {
  const [value, setValue] = useState('')
  const [isFocused, setIsFocused] = useState(false)

  const debouncedSuggestion = useCallback(
    debounce((text: string) => {
      if (text.length > 2 && onSuggestion) {
        onSuggestion(text)
      }
    }, 500),
    [onSuggestion]
  )

  const handleChange = (e: React.ChangeEvent<HTMLInputElement>) => {
    const val = e.target.value
    setValue(val)
    debouncedSuggestion(val)
  }

  const handleSend = () => {
    if (value.trim()) {
      onSend(value.trim())
      setValue('')
    }
  }

  const handleKeyDown = (e: React.KeyboardEvent<HTMLInputElement>) => {
    if (e.key === 'Enter' && !e.shiftKey) {
      e.preventDefault()
      handleSend()
    }
  }

  return (
    <div className="flex gap-2 p-3 border-t border-white/10 bg-waos-surface">
      <div className="flex-1 relative">
        <input
          className={`w-full bg-white/5 rounded-xl px-4 py-2.5 text-sm outline-none transition-all text-white placeholder-white/30 ${
            isFocused ? 'ring-1 ring-waos-primary/50' : ''
          }`}
          placeholder="输入消息... AI 实时补全"
          value={value}
          onChange={handleChange}
          onKeyDown={handleKeyDown}
          onFocus={() => setIsFocused(true)}
          onBlur={() => setIsFocused(false)}
        />
        {value.length > 0 && (
          <div className="absolute right-3 top-1/2 -translate-y-1/2 text-xs text-white/20">
            {value.length}
          </div>
        )}
      </div>
      <button
        onClick={handleSend}
        disabled={!value.trim()}
        className={`px-4 py-2.5 rounded-xl text-sm font-medium transition-all ${
          value.trim()
            ? 'bg-waos-primary text-black hover:opacity-80'
            : 'bg-white/5 text-white/20 cursor-not-allowed'
        }`}
      >
        发送
      </button>
    </div>
  )
}
```

#### `frontend/src/modules/chat/AISuggestionCard.tsx`
```tsx
import { motion } from 'framer-motion'
import { usePersonaStore } from '../../store/personaStore'

export function AISuggestionCard() {
  const { reasoning, actions } = usePersonaStore()

  return (
    <motion.div
      initial={{ opacity: 0, y: 10 }}
      animate={{ opacity: 1, y: 0 }}
      className="bg-waos-primary/10 border border-waos-primary/20 rounded-xl p-3"
    >
      <div className="flex items-center gap-2 text-xs text-waos-primary font-medium mb-2">
        <span className="w-1.5 h-1.5 rounded-full bg-waos-primary animate-pulse" />
        AI 建议
      </div>

      {/* 推理链 */}
      {reasoning.length > 0 && (
        <div className="space-y-1 mb-2">
          {reasoning.map((item, idx) => (
            <div key={idx} className="text-xs text-white/60 flex items-center gap-2">
              <span className="w-1 h-1 rounded-full bg-white/20" />
              {item}
            </div>
          ))}
        </div>
      )}

      {/* 操作按钮 */}
      <div className="flex gap-2 flex-wrap">
        {actions.length > 0 ? (
          actions.map((action, idx) => (
            <button
              key={idx}
              className="px-3 py-1 bg-white/10 hover:bg-white/20 rounded-lg text-xs text-white/80 transition"
            >
              {action}
            </button>
          ))
        ) : (
          <>
            <button className="px-3 py-1 bg-white/10 hover:bg-white/20 rounded-lg text-xs text-white/80 transition">
              发送案例
            </button>
            <button className="px-3 py-1 bg-white/10 hover:bg-white/20 rounded-lg text-xs text-white/80 transition">
              对比方案
            </button>
            <button className="px-3 py-1 bg-waos-primary/20 hover:bg-waos-primary/30 rounded-lg text-xs text-waos-primary transition">
              AI 执行
            </button>
          </>
        )}
      </div>
    </motion.div>
  )
}
```

```tsx
import { PersonaState } from '../../store/personaStore'

interface PersonaBlockProps {
  persona: PersonaState
}

const typeMap = {
  CLOSER: { label: '成交关闭模式', icon: '🎯', color: 'text-red-400' },
  CONSULTANT: { label: '专业咨询模式', icon: '📊', color: 'text-blue-400' },
  FRIEND: { label: '社交破冰模式', icon: '🤝', color: 'text-green-400' },
}

export function PersonaBlock({ persona }: PersonaBlockProps) {
  const info = typeMap[persona.type] || typeMap.FRIEND

  return (
    <div className="panel">
      <div className="flex items-center justify-between">
        <div className="flex items-center gap-2">
          <span className="text-xl">{info.icon}</span>
          <div>
            <div className="text-sm font-medium text-white/90">{info.label}</div>
            <div className="text-xs text-white/40 flex items-center gap-2">
              <span>语气: {persona.tone}</span>
              <span>·</span>
              <span>压力: {(persona.pressure * 100).toFixed(0)}%</span>
            </div>
          </div>
        </div>
        <div className={`text-xs font-medium ${info.color}`}>
          {persona.type}
        </div>
      </div>
      <div className="mt-2 h-1 w-full bg-white/5 rounded-full overflow-hidden">
        <div
          className="h-full bg-gradient-to-r from-waos-primary to-waos-accent rounded-full transition-all duration-500"
          style={{ width: `${persona.pressure * 100}%` }}
        />
      </div>
    </div>
  )
}
```

#### `frontend/src/modules/ai-brain/ScorePanel.tsx`
```tsx
import { motion } from 'framer-motion'

interface ScorePanelProps {
  score: number
  probability: number
}

export function ScorePanel({ score, probability }: ScorePanelProps) {
  const getScoreColor = (s: number) => {
    if (s > 80) return 'text-green-400'
    if (s > 50) return 'text-yellow-400'
    return 'text-gray-400'
  }

  return (
    <div className="panel">
      <div className="grid grid-cols-2 gap-4">
        <div>
          <div className="text-xs text-white/40">客户评分</div>
          <motion.div
            key={score}
            initial={{ scale: 0.8, opacity: 0 }}
            animate={{ scale: 1, opacity: 1 }}
            className={`text-3xl font-bold ${getScoreColor(score)}`}
          >
            {score}
          </motion.div>
          <div className="text-[10px] text-white/20">/ 100</div>
        </div>
        <div>
          <div className="text-xs text-white/40">成交概率</div>
          <motion.div
            key={probability}
            initial={{ scale: 0.8, opacity: 0 }}
            animate={{ scale: 1, opacity: 1 }}
            className={`text-3xl font-bold ${getScoreColor(probability)}`}
          >
            {probability}%
          </motion.div>
          <div className="text-[10px] text-white/20">预测</div>
        </div>
      </div>

      {/* 进度条 */}
      <div className="mt-3 h-1.5 w-full bg-white/5 rounded-full overflow-hidden">
        <motion.div
          initial={{ width: 0 }}
          animate={{ width: `${score}%` }}
          transition={{ duration: 0.8, ease: 'easeOut' }}
          className="h-full bg-gradient-to-r from-waos-primary to-waos-accent rounded-full"
        />
      </div>
    </div>
  )
}
```

```tsx
import { usePersonaStore } from '../../store/personaStore'

export function ReasoningFlow() {
  const { reasoning } = usePersonaStore()

  if (reasoning.length === 0) {
    return (
      <div className="panel">
        <div className="text-xs text-white/40 mb-2">🧠 AI 推理链</div>
        <div className="text-xs text-white/20">等待分析...</div>
      </div>
    )
  }

  return (
    <div className="panel">
      <div className="text-xs text-white/40 mb-2">🧠 AI 推理链</div>
      <div className="space-y-1.5">
        {reasoning.map((item, idx) => (
          <div key={idx} className="flex items-center gap-2 text-xs">
            <span
              className={`w-1.5 h-1.5 rounded-full ${
                idx === reasoning.length - 1 ? 'bg-waos-primary animate-pulse' : 'bg-white/20'
              }`}
            />
            <span className="text-white/70">{item}</span>
          </div>
        ))}
      </div>
    </div>
  )
}
```

```tsx
import { usePersonaStore } from '../../store/personaStore'

export function ActionPanel() {
  const { actions } = usePersonaStore()

  const defaultActions = ['发送案例', '发送对比', 'AI执行']

  const displayActions = actions.length > 0 ? actions : defaultActions

  return (
    <div className="panel">
      <div className="text-xs text-white/40 mb-2">⚡ 推荐动作</div>
      <div className="flex flex-wrap gap-2">
        {displayActions.map((action, idx) => (
          <button
            key={idx}
            className={`px-3 py-1.5 rounded-lg text-xs font-medium transition-all ${
              idx === 0
                ? 'bg-waos-primary text-black hover:opacity-80'
                : 'bg-white/10 text-white/80 hover:bg-white/20'
            }`}
          >
            {action}
          </button>
        ))}
      </div>
    </div>
  )
}
```

### 📦 十、主入口与路由

#### `frontend/src/App.tsx`
```tsx
import { BrowserRouter, Routes, Route, Navigate } from 'react-router-dom'
import { QueryClient, QueryClientProvider } from '@tanstack/react-query'
import { MainLayout } from './layout/MainLayout'

const queryClient = new QueryClient()

function App() {
  return (
    <QueryClientProvider client={queryClient}>
      <BrowserRouter>
        <Routes>
          <Route path="/" element={<MainLayout />} />
          <Route path="*" element={<Navigate to="/" replace />} />
        </Routes>
      </BrowserRouter>
    </QueryClientProvider>
  )
}

export default App
```

├─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┤
│                    EventBus (Redis)                         │
├─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┤

└─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘

                            │
                            ▼
                    微信客户端 (实际账号)
📄 文件 1：backend/app/adapters/clawbot/client.py（HTTP 客户端）
python
import asyncio
import json
import time
from typing import Optional, Dict, Any, List
from datetime import datetime
import httpx
from tenacity import (
    retry,
    stop_after_attempt,
    wait_exponential,
    retry_if_exception_type,
    retry_if_result,
)

from app.utils.logger import logger
from app.utils.redis_client import redis_client

class ClawBotClient:
    """ClawBot HTTP API 客户端（生产级）"""

    def __init__(self, base_url: str, api_key: Optional[str] = None, timeout: int = 30):
        self.base_url = base_url.rstrip('/')
        self.api_key = api_key
        self.timeout = timeout
        self._client = None

    async def _get_client(self) -> httpx.AsyncClient:
        """获取 HTTP 客户端（懒加载）"""
        if self._client is None:
            headers = {"Content-Type": "application/json"}
            if self.api_key:
                headers["Authorization"] = f"Bearer {self.api_key}"
            self._client = httpx.AsyncClient(
                base_url=self.base_url,
                headers=headers,
                timeout=self.timeout,
            )
        return self._client

    async def close(self):
        """关闭客户端"""
        if self._client:
            await self._client.aclose()
            self._client = None

    # ===== 核心 API 方法 =====

    @retry(
        stop=stop_after_attempt(3),
        wait=wait_exponential(multiplier=1, min=1, max=10),
        retry=retry_if_exception_type((httpx.TimeoutException, httpx.ConnectError)),
    )
    async def _request(
        self,
        method: str,
        path: str,
        data: Optional[Dict] = None,
        params: Optional[Dict] = None,
    ) -> Dict[str, Any]:
        """统一请求方法（带重试）"""
        client = await self._get_client()
        url = f"/api/{path.lstrip('/')}"

        try:
            response = await client.request(
                method=method,
                url=url,
                json=data,
                params=params,
            )
            response.raise_for_status()
            return response.json()
        except httpx.HTTPStatusError as e:
            logger.error(f"ClawBot HTTP error: {e.response.status_code} - {e.response.text}")
            raise
        except Exception as e:
            logger.error(f"ClawBot request error: {e}")
            raise

    # ===== 登录相关 =====

    async def qr_login(self, account_id: str) -> Dict[str, Any]:
        """发起二维码登录"""
        return await self._request("POST", "/login/qr", data={"account_id": account_id})

    async def check_login_status(self, account_id: str) -> Dict[str, Any]:
        """检查登录状态"""
        return await self._request("GET", f"/login/status/{account_id}")

    async def logout(self, account_id: str) -> Dict[str, Any]:
        """登出"""
        return await self._request("POST", f"/logout/{account_id}")

    # ===== 消息相关 =====

    async def send_message(self, account_id: str, to: str, content: str, msg_type: str = "text") -> Dict[str, Any]:
        """发送消息"""
        return await self._request(
            "POST",
            "/message/send",
            data={
                "account_id": account_id,
                "to": to,
                "content": content,
                "type": msg_type,
            },
        )

    async def send_image(self, account_id: str, to: str, image_url: str) -> Dict[str, Any]:
        """发送图片"""
        return await self._request(
            "POST",
            "/message/send",
            data={
                "account_id": account_id,
                "to": to,
                "content": image_url,
                "type": "image",
            },
        )

    async def fetch_messages(self, account_id: str, since_seq: Optional[int] = None) -> List[Dict[str, Any]]:
        """拉取消息（增量）"""
        params = {"account_id": account_id}
        if since_seq is not None:
            params["since_seq"] = since_seq
        result = await self._request("GET", "/messages", params=params)
        return result.get("messages", [])

    # ===== 联系人相关 =====

    async def fetch_contacts(self, account_id: str) -> List[Dict[str, Any]]:
        """获取联系人列表"""
        result = await self._request("GET", "/contacts", params={"account_id": account_id})
        return result.get("contacts", [])

    # ===== 朋友圈相关 =====

    async def send_moment(self, account_id: str, content: str, images: Optional[List[str]] = None) -> Dict[str, Any]:
        """发布朋友圈"""
        return await self._request(
            "POST",
            "/moment/send",
            data={
                "account_id": account_id,
                "content": content,
                "images": images or [],
            },
        )

    # ===== 健康检查 =====

    async def health_check(self) -> bool:
        """检查 ClawBot 服务是否可用"""
        try:
            await self._request("GET", "/health")
            return True
        except Exception:
            return False
📄 文件 2：backend/app/adapters/clawbot/session_manager.py（Redis 持久化 Session）
python
import json
import time
from typing import Optional, Dict, Any
from datetime import datetime
from uuid import UUID

from app.utils.redis_client import redis_client
from app.utils.logger import logger

class ClawBotSessionManager:
    """ClawBot 会话管理（Redis 持久化）"""

    SESSION_TTL = 86400 * 7  # 7 天
    HEARTBEAT_INTERVAL = 60  # 60 秒

    @staticmethod
    def _key(account_id: str) -> str:
        return f"clawbot:session:{account_id}"

    @staticmethod
    def _token_key(account_id: str) -> str:
        return f"clawbot:token:{account_id}"

    @staticmethod
    def save_session(account_id: str, data: Dict[str, Any]) -> None:
        """保存会话"""
        key = ClawBotSessionManager._key(account_id)
        data["updated_at"] = time.time()
        redis_client.hset(key, mapping=data)
        redis_client.expire(key, ClawBotSessionManager.SESSION_TTL)

    @staticmethod
    def get_session(account_id: str) -> Optional[Dict[str, Any]]:
        """获取会话"""
        key = ClawBotSessionManager._key(account_id)
        data = redis_client.hgetall(key)
        if not data:
            return None
        return {k.decode(): v.decode() for k, v in data.items()}

    @staticmethod
    def get_token(account_id: str) -> Optional[str]:
        """获取 Token"""
        token = redis_client.get(ClawBotSessionManager._token_key(account_id))
        return token.decode() if token else None

    @staticmethod
    def save_token(account_id: str, token: str) -> None:
        """保存 Token"""
        redis_client.setex(
            ClawBotSessionManager._token_key(account_id),
            ClawBotSessionManager.SESSION_TTL,
            token,
        )

    @staticmethod
    def update_heartbeat(account_id: str) -> None:
        """更新心跳"""
        key = ClawBotSessionManager._key(account_id)
        redis_client.hset(key, "last_heartbeat", time.time())
        redis_client.expire(key, ClawBotSessionManager.SESSION_TTL)

    @staticmethod
    def is_alive(account_id: str) -> bool:
        """检查会话是否存活"""
        session = ClawBotSessionManager.get_session(account_id)
        if not session:
            return False
        last_heartbeat = float(session.get("last_heartbeat", 0))
        return (time.time() - last_heartbeat) < ClawBotSessionManager.HEARTBEAT_INTERVAL * 2

    @staticmethod
    def delete_session(account_id: str) -> None:
        """删除会话（登出）"""
        redis_client.delete(ClawBotSessionManager._key(account_id))
        redis_client.delete(ClawBotSessionManager._token_key(account_id))

    @staticmethod
    def get_all_accounts() -> List[str]:
        """获取所有已登录的账号"""
        keys = redis_client.keys("clawbot:session:*")
        return [k.decode().split(":")[-1] for k in keys]
📄 文件 3：backend/app/adapters/clawbot/sync.py（消息同步 Loop）
python
import asyncio
import json
from datetime import datetime
from typing import Optional, Dict, Any
from uuid import uuid4

from app.adapters.clawbot.client import ClawBotClient
from app.adapters.clawbot.session_manager import ClawBotSessionManager
from app.core.event import Event
from app.core.pipeline import pipeline
from app.core.event_bus import publish_event
from app.utils.logger import logger
from app.utils.redis_client import redis_client

class ClawBotSyncService:
    """ClawBot 消息同步服务（拉取 Loop）"""

    def __init__(self, client: ClawBotClient):
        self.client = client
        self._running = False
        self._tasks = []

    async def start(self):
        """启动所有账号的同步任务"""
        self._running = True
        accounts = ClawBotSessionManager.get_all_accounts()
        logger.info(f"Starting ClawBot sync for {len(accounts)} accounts")

        for account_id in accounts:
            task = asyncio.create_task(self._sync_loop(account_id))
            self._tasks.append(task)

        # 定期检查新账号
        asyncio.create_task(self._check_new_accounts())

    async def stop(self):
        """停止所有同步任务"""
        self._running = False
        for task in self._tasks:
            task.cancel()
        await asyncio.gather(*self._tasks, return_exceptions=True)
        self._tasks.clear()
        logger.info("ClawBot sync stopped")

    async def _sync_loop(self, account_id: str):
        """单个账号的同步循环"""
        logger.info(f"Sync loop started for account: {account_id}")

        while self._running:
            try:
                # 1. 检查会话是否有效
                if not ClawBotSessionManager.is_alive(account_id):
                    logger.warning(f"Account {account_id} session expired, stopping sync")
                    break

                # 2. 获取上次拉取的 Seq
                seq_key = f"clawbot:sync:{account_id}:last_seq"
                since_seq = redis_client.get(seq_key)
                since_seq = int(since_seq) if since_seq else None

                # 3. 拉取消息
                messages = await self.client.fetch_messages(account_id, since_seq=since_seq)

                if messages:
                    logger.info(f"Fetched {len(messages)} messages for account {account_id}")

                    # 4. 处理每条消息
                    for msg in messages:
                        await self._process_message(account_id, msg)

                    # 5. 更新 Seq
                    last_seq = messages[-1].get("seq", since_seq or 0)
                    redis_client.set(seq_key, last_seq)

                # 6. 更新心跳
                ClawBotSessionManager.update_heartbeat(account_id)

                # 7. 等待下一次拉取（1-3 秒随机抖动，防风控）
                await asyncio.sleep(1 + (hash(account_id) % 2))

            except asyncio.CancelledError:
                break
            except Exception as e:
                logger.error(f"Sync loop error for {account_id}: {e}")
                await asyncio.sleep(5)

        logger.info(f"Sync loop stopped for account: {account_id}")

    async def _process_message(self, account_id: str, msg: Dict[str, Any]):
        """处理单条消息：转换为 Event 并进入 Pipeline"""
        # 消息去重（防止重复处理）
        msg_id = msg.get("id") or msg.get("msg_id")
        if not msg_id:
            return

        dedup_key = f"clawbot:msg:{account_id}:{msg_id}"
        if redis_client.exists(dedup_key):
            logger.debug(f"Duplicate message {msg_id}, skipping")
            return
        redis_client.setex(dedup_key, 86400, "1")

        # 转换为统一事件
        from_user = msg.get("from") or msg.get("sender")
        content = msg.get("content") or msg.get("text") or ""
        msg_type = msg.get("type") or "text"

        # 忽略非文本消息（暂时）
        if msg_type != "text":
            return

        event = Event(
            user=from_user,
            content=content,
            platform="wechat",
            account_id=account_id,
            event_id=f"clawbot_{account_id}_{msg_id}",
            timestamp=datetime.now().timestamp(),
        )

        # 发送到 EventBus（进入 Pipeline）
        await publish_event("message.received", event.to_dict())

    async def _check_new_accounts(self):
        """定期检查是否有新账号加入"""
        while self._running:
            await asyncio.sleep(30)
            try:
                current_accounts = set(ClawBotSessionManager.get_all_accounts())
                syncing_accounts = set()
                # 从正在运行的 task 中提取 account_id
                # 这里简化：从 Redis 中读取
                for task in self._tasks:
                    if hasattr(task, "_account_id"):
                        syncing_accounts.add(task._account_id)

                new_accounts = current_accounts - syncing_accounts
                for account_id in new_accounts:
                    logger.info(f"New account detected: {account_id}")
                    task = asyncio.create_task(self._sync_loop(account_id))
                    self._tasks.append(task)
            except Exception as e:
                logger.error(f"Check new accounts error: {e}")

    async def sync_once(self, account_id: str) -> int:
        """手动触发一次同步（用于调试）"""
        messages = await self.client.fetch_messages(account_id)
        for msg in messages:
            await self._process_message(account_id, msg)
        return len(messages)
📄 文件 4：backend/app/adapters/clawbot/adapter.py（统一 Adapter 实现）
python
from typing import Optional, List
from app.adapters.base import BaseAdapter
from app.adapters.clawbot.client import ClawBotClient
from app.adapters.clawbot.session_manager import ClawBotSessionManager
from app.adapters.clawbot.sync import ClawBotSyncService
from app.utils.logger import logger

class ClawBotAdapter(BaseAdapter):
    """ClawBot 适配器（实现 BaseAdapter 接口）"""

    def __init__(self, base_url: str, api_key: Optional[str] = None):
        self.client = ClawBotClient(base_url, api_key)
        self.sync_service = ClawBotSyncService(self.client)
        self._started = False

    async def start(self):
        """启动同步服务"""
        if not self._started:
            await self.sync_service.start()
            self._started = True
            logger.info("ClawBot adapter started")

    async def stop(self):
        """停止同步服务"""
        if self._started:
            await self.sync_service.stop()
            self._started = False
            await self.client.close()
            logger.info("ClawBot adapter stopped")

    # ===== BaseAdapter 接口实现 =====

    async def send_text(self, to: str, content: str, account_id: Optional[str] = None) -> dict:
        """发送文本消息"""
        if not account_id:
            # 自动选择一个可用的账号
            accounts = ClawBotSessionManager.get_all_accounts()
            if not accounts:
                return {"code": -1, "msg": "no available account"}
            account_id = accounts[0]

        return await self.client.send_message(account_id, to, content)

    async def send_image(self, to: str, image_url: str, account_id: Optional[str] = None) -> dict:
        """发送图片"""
        if not account_id:
            accounts = ClawBotSessionManager.get_all_accounts()
            if not accounts:
                return {"code": -1, "msg": "no available account"}
            account_id = accounts[0]

        return await self.client.send_image(account_id, to, image_url)

    async def send_moment(self, account_id: str, content: str, images: Optional[List[str]] = None) -> dict:
        """发送朋友圈"""
        return await self.client.send_moment(account_id, content, images)

    async def get_messages(self, account_id: str, since_seq: Optional[int] = None) -> List[dict]:
        """获取消息（同步调用）"""
        return await self.client.fetch_messages(account_id, since_seq)

    async def get_contacts(self, account_id: str) -> List[dict]:
        """获取联系人"""
        return await self.client.fetch_contacts(account_id)

    async def login(self, account_id: str) -> dict:
        """发起登录"""
        return await self.client.qr_login(account_id)

    async def check_login(self, account_id: str) -> dict:
        """检查登录状态"""
        return await self.client.check_login_status(account_id)

    async def health_check(self) -> bool:
        """健康检查"""
        return await self.client.health_check()
📄 文件 5：backend/app/worker/task_worker.py（消息发送任务消费者）
python
import asyncio
import json
from datetime import datetime

from app.utils.redis_client import redis_client
from app.adapters.clawbot.adapter import ClawBotAdapter
from app.core.event_bus import consume_events
from app.models.task import Task
from app.db.session import get_db_session
from app.utils.logger import logger

class TaskWorker:
    """任务消费者（从 Redis Stream 消费发送任务）"""

    def __init__(self, adapter: ClawBotAdapter):
        self.adapter = adapter
        self._running = False

    async def start(self):
        """启动消费者"""
        self._running = True
        logger.info("Task worker started")

        while self._running:
            try:
                # 从 Redis Stream 消费任务
                events = consume_events("waos.tasks", "task_worker", "worker-1")
                for event in events:
                    await self._process_task(event)
            except asyncio.CancelledError:
                break
            except Exception as e:
                logger.error(f"Task worker error: {e}")
                await asyncio.sleep(1)

        logger.info("Task worker stopped")

    async def stop(self):
        """停止消费者"""
        self._running = False

    async def _process_task(self, event: dict):
        """处理单个任务"""
        task_type = event.get("task_type")
        payload = event.get("payload", {})
        task_id = event.get("task_id")

        if task_type == "SEND_MESSAGE":
            await self._send_message(task_id, payload)
        elif task_type == "SEND_IMAGE":
            await self._send_image(task_id, payload)
        elif task_type == "SEND_MOMENT":
            await self._send_moment(task_id, payload)
        else:
            logger.warning(f"Unknown task type: {task_type}")

    async def _send_message(self, task_id: str, payload: dict):
        """发送文本消息"""
        to = payload.get("to")
        content = payload.get("content")
        account_id = payload.get("account_id")

        try:
            result = await self.adapter.send_text(to, content, account_id)
            self._update_task_status(task_id, "success", result)
        except Exception as e:
            logger.error(f"Send message failed: {e}")
            self._update_task_status(task_id, "failed", {"error": str(e)})

    async def _send_image(self, task_id: str, payload: dict):
        """发送图片"""
        to = payload.get("to")
        image_url = payload.get("image_url")
        account_id = payload.get("account_id")

        try:
            result = await self.adapter.send_image(to, image_url, account_id)
            self._update_task_status(task_id, "success", result)
        except Exception as e:
            logger.error(f"Send image failed: {e}")
            self._update_task_status(task_id, "failed", {"error": str(e)})

    async def _send_moment(self, task_id: str, payload: dict):
        """发送朋友圈"""
        account_id = payload.get("account_id")
        content = payload.get("content")
        images = payload.get("images", [])

        try:
            result = await self.adapter.send_moment(account_id, content, images)
            self._update_task_status(task_id, "success", result)
        except Exception as e:
            logger.error(f"Send moment failed: {e}")
            self._update_task_status(task_id, "failed", {"error": str(e)})

    def _update_task_status(self, task_id: str, status: str, result: dict):
        """更新任务状态（写入 PostgreSQL）"""
        with get_db_session() as db:
            task = db.query(Task).filter(Task.id == task_id).first()
            if task:
                task.status = status
                task.result = result
                task.updated_at = datetime.now()
                db.commit()
📄 文件 6：backend/app/api/clawbot.py（ClawBot 管理 API）
python
from fastapi import APIRouter, Depends, HTTPException, BackgroundTasks
from pydantic import BaseModel
from typing import Optional
from uuid import UUID

from app.dependencies.auth import get_current_tenant
from app.adapters.clawbot.adapter import ClawBotAdapter
from app.adapters.clawbot.session_manager import ClawBotSessionManager
from app.utils.logger import logger

router = APIRouter(prefix="/api/clawbot", tags=["clawbot"])

# 全局 Adapter 实例（在 main.py 中初始化）
_adapter: Optional[ClawBotAdapter] = None

def get_adapter() -> ClawBotAdapter:
    if _adapter is None:
        raise HTTPException(status_code=500, detail="ClawBot adapter not initialized")
    return _adapter

class LoginRequest(BaseModel):
    account_id: str

class SendMessageRequest(BaseModel):
    account_id: str
    to: str
    content: str
    msg_type: str = "text"

class SendMomentRequest(BaseModel):
    account_id: str
    content: str
    images: Optional[list] = []

@router.post("/login")
async def login(
    req: LoginRequest,
    background_tasks: BackgroundTasks,
    tenant: UUID = Depends(get_current_tenant),
):
    """发起二维码登录"""
    adapter = get_adapter()
    try:
        result = await adapter.login(req.account_id)
        # 后台启动同步（登录成功后）
        if result.get("code") == 0:
            background_tasks.add_task(adapter.sync_service.sync_once, req.account_id)
        return result
    except Exception as e:
        logger.error(f"Login failed: {e}")
        raise HTTPException(status_code=500, detail=str(e))

@router.get("/status/{account_id}")
async def get_status(
    account_id: str,
    tenant: UUID = Depends(get_current_tenant),
):
    """获取账号状态"""
    session = ClawBotSessionManager.get_session(account_id)
    if not session:
        return {"status": "not_logged_in"}
    return {
        "status": session.get("status", "unknown"),
        "is_alive": ClawBotSessionManager.is_alive(account_id),
        "last_heartbeat": session.get("last_heartbeat"),
    }

@router.post("/send")
async def send_message(
    req: SendMessageRequest,
    tenant: UUID = Depends(get_current_tenant),
):
    """发送消息（同步）"""
    adapter = get_adapter()
    try:
        result = await adapter.send_text(req.to, req.content, req.account_id)
        return result
    except Exception as e:
        logger.error(f"Send message failed: {e}")
        raise HTTPException(status_code=500, detail=str(e))

@router.post("/moment")
async def send_moment(
    req: SendMomentRequest,
    tenant: UUID = Depends(get_current_tenant),
):
    """发布朋友圈"""
    adapter = get_adapter()
    try:
        result = await adapter.send_moment(req.account_id, req.content, req.images)
        return result
    except Exception as e:
        logger.error(f"Send moment failed: {e}")
        raise HTTPException(status_code=500, detail=str(e))

@router.post("/sync/{account_id}")
async def sync_messages(
    account_id: str,
    background_tasks: BackgroundTasks,
    tenant: UUID = Depends(get_current_tenant),
):
    """手动触发消息同步"""
    adapter = get_adapter()
    background_tasks.add_task(adapter.sync_service.sync_once, account_id)
    return {"status": "sync_started"}

@router.get("/accounts")
async def list_accounts(
    tenant: UUID = Depends(get_current_tenant),
):
    """列出所有已登录账号"""
    accounts = ClawBotSessionManager.get_all_accounts()
    return {"accounts": accounts}
📄 文件 7：修改 backend/app/main.py（集成 ClawBot）

from app.adapters.clawbot.adapter import ClawBotAdapter
from app.api import clawbot

# 初始化 ClawBot Adapter
clawbot_adapter = ClawBotAdapter(
    base_url=os.getenv("CLAWBOT_API_URL", "http://clawbot:8080"),
    api_key=os.getenv("CLAWBOT_API_KEY", None),
)

# 注册路由
app.include_router(clawbot.router)

# 启动/关闭事件
@app.on_event("startup")
async def startup_event():
    # ... 原有代码 ...
    
    # 启动 ClawBot 同步
    await clawbot_adapter.start()
    logger.info("ClawBot adapter started")

@app.on_event("shutdown")
async def shutdown_event():
    # ... 原有代码 ...
    
    # 停止 ClawBot 同步
    await clawbot_adapter.stop()
    logger.info("ClawBot adapter stopped")

您说“继续”，我立即输出生产级 K8s 部署配置 + 阿里云/AWS 部署指南。
**完全正确。** WAOS 是一个 **事件驱动 + 定时任务 + 实时通信** 的操作系统，它必须 **7x24 小时不间断运行**，才能真正帮你自动处理微信消息、定时发朋友圈、监控视频号评论。

如果它只在你上班时运行，那么：
- ❌ 半夜来了高意向客户，没人回复（流失）
- ❌ 朋友圈定时发送失败（养号中断）
- ❌ 视频号爆量了，系统没启动（错过流量高峰）

---

## 🚀 如何让 WAOS 7x24 运行？（你目前有 3 个选择，我给你最优解）

### 方案 A：单机 Docker Compose（生产可用，成本最低）
> **适用**：月活 1 万以内客户，初创期。
> **成本**：1 台 4C16G 云服务器（约 300-800元/月）。

- **核心配置**：在 `docker-compose.yml` 中给所有服务加上 `restart: always`。
- **命令**：`docker compose up -d`（后台运行），服务器重启后 Docker 会自动拉起所有服务。
- **监控**：使用 `cron` + 简单脚本检测服务端口（8000/6379/5432）是否存活，挂了自动重启。

---

### 方案 B：Kubernetes（企业级高可用，我们之前已准备了全套 K8s 配置）
> **适用**：多租户、月活 10 万以上，需要滚动更新和自动扩缩容。
> **成本**：3 台及以上云服务器（约 1500-5000元/月）。

- **核心机制**：`livenessProbe` 和 `readinessProbe` 探针。
- **策略**：`replicas: 2`（多副本），滚动更新零停机。
- **运维**：Prometheus + Grafana 自动告警（CPU/内存/连接数）。

---

### 方案 C：云函数 / Serverless（不推荐，WAOS 不适合）
> 微信 WebSocket 长连接和 Redis Streams 持久化在 Serverless 环境下很难完美支持，强行迁移成本极高。

---

## ✅ 我现在直接给你补全「生产级 Docker Compose」运维套件

基于你之前的需求，我强烈建议你 **先用方案 A（Docker Compose）** 跑起来，成熟后再无缝迁移到 K8s（因为镜像不变）。

### 1. 更新 `docker-compose.prod.yml`（加入重启策略 + 健康检查）
```yaml
version: "3.9"

services:
  postgres:
    image: postgres:15
    restart: always   # <--- 关键：自动重启
    environment:
      POSTGRES_USER: waos
      POSTGRES_PASSWORD: ${DB_PASSWORD}
      POSTGRES_DB: waos
    volumes:
      - pg_data:/var/lib/postgresql/data
    healthcheck:
      test: ["CMD-SHELL", "pg_isready -U waos"]
      interval: 30s
      timeout: 10s
      retries: 5

  redis:
    image: redis:7-alpine
    restart: always
    command: redis-server --appendonly yes
    volumes:
      - redis_data:/data
    healthcheck:
      test: ["CMD", "redis-cli", "ping"]
      interval: 30s
      timeout: 10s

  qdrant:
    image: qdrant/qdrant
    restart: always
    volumes:
      - qdrant_data:/qdrant/storage

  backend:
    build: ./backend
    restart: always
    ports:
      - "8000:8000"
    depends_on:
      postgres:
        condition: service_healthy
      redis:
        condition: service_healthy
    environment:
      - DATABASE_URL=postgresql://waos:${DB_PASSWORD}@postgres:5432/waos
      - REDIS_URL=redis://redis:6379
      - QDRANT_HOST=qdrant
      - ENVIRONMENT=production
    # 启动失败重试（10秒后重试，最多重试3次）
    healthcheck:
      test: ["CMD", "curl", "-f", "http://localhost:8000/health/ping"]
      interval: 60s
      timeout: 5s
      retries: 3

  worker:
    build: ./backend
    restart: always
    command: python -m app.worker.event_consumer
    depends_on:
      redis:
        condition: service_healthy
    environment:
      - DATABASE_URL=postgresql://waos:${DB_PASSWORD}@postgres:5432/waos
      - REDIS_URL=redis://redis:6379
      - ENVIRONMENT=production

  campaign_worker:
    build: ./backend
    restart: always
    command: python -m app.worker.campaign_worker
    depends_on:
      redis:
        condition: service_healthy
    environment:
      - DATABASE_URL=postgresql://waos:${DB_PASSWORD}@postgres:5432/waos
      - REDIS_URL=redis://redis:6379

  moment_scheduler:
    build: ./backend
    restart: always
    command: python -m app.worker.moment_scheduler_runner
    depends_on:
      redis:
        condition: service_healthy
    environment:
      - DATABASE_URL=postgresql://waos:${DB_PASSWORD}@postgres:5432/waos
      - REDIS_URL=redis://redis:6379

  frontend:
    build: ./frontend
    restart: always
    ports:
      - "3000:3000"
    depends_on:
      - backend

  nginx:
    image: nginx:alpine
    restart: always
    ports:
      - "80:80"
      - "443:443"
    volumes:
      - ./infra/nginx/nginx.conf:/etc/nginx/nginx.conf:ro
    depends_on:
      - backend
      - frontend

volumes:
  pg_data:
  redis_data:
  qdrant_data:
```

### 2. 新增 `.env.production`（敏感信息不要提交到 Git）
```env
DB_PASSWORD=your_very_strong_password_here
JWT_SECRET=your_jwt_secret_here
OPENAI_API_KEY=sk-xxx
QDRANT_API_KEY=xxx
ENVIRONMENT=production
```

### 3. 新增 `infra/nginx/nginx.conf`（负载均衡 + 静态文件缓存）
```nginx
upstream backend {
    server backend:8000;
}

upstream frontend {
    server frontend:3000;
}

server {
    listen 80;
    server_name your-domain.com;

    location /api {
        proxy_pass http://backend;
        proxy_set_header Host $host;
        proxy_set_header X-Real-IP $remote_addr;
    }

    location /ws {
        proxy_pass http://backend;
        proxy_http_version 1.1;
        proxy_set_header Upgrade $http_upgrade;
        proxy_set_header Connection "upgrade";
        proxy_set_header Host $host;
    }

    location / {
        proxy_pass http://frontend;
        proxy_set_header Host $host;
    }
}
```

### 4. 一键部署命令（你只需要在服务器上执行这两行）
```bash
# 1. 拉取代码（或 scp 上传）
git clone your-repo waos && cd waos

# 2. 加载环境变量并启动（后台守护进程模式）
docker compose -f docker-compose.prod.yml --env-file .env.production up -d

# 3. 查看日志确认无报错
docker compose logs -f
```

### 5. 万一容器崩溃怎么办？（自动恢复机制）
你只需要在 `docker-compose.prod.yml` 里加上了 `restart: always`，Docker 会一直尝试重启挂掉的容器。

如果机器重启（比如云服务器自动更新），你需要设置 Docker 开机自启：
```bash
sudo systemctl enable docker
sudo systemctl start docker
```
这样服务器重启后，Docker 会自动拉起所有容器，完全无人值守。

- **阿里云**：7x24 小时生产运行（公网可访问，处理真实客户消息）

## 🏗️ 一、整体架构（双环境）

```
┌─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐
│                     阿里云服务器（生产环境）                    │
│  ┌──────────┐ ┌──────────┐ ┌──────────┐ ┌──────────┐         │
│  │ Nginx:80 │→│ Backend  │ │ Worker   │ │ Scheduler│         │
│  └──────────┘ └──────────┘ └──────────┘ └──────────┘         │
│          ↓            ↓            ↓                           │
│      PostgreSQL    Redis       Qdrant（向量库）                │
│       (数据持久)    (缓存/队列)   (知识库检索)                  │
└─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘
                              ↑
                         公网访问
                              ↑
┌─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐
│                     你的本地电脑（开发环境）                     │
│  ┌──────────┐ ┌──────────┐ ┌──────────┐                      │
│  │ 前端:3000│ │ Backend  │ │ Worker   │  ← 代码热更新         │
│  └──────────┘ └──────────┘ └──────────┘                      │
│          ↓            ↓                                       │
│    PostgreSQL    Redis（本地数据与生产隔离）                    │
│    (测试数据)     (测试队列)                                   │
└─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘
```

## 📦 二、阿里云生产环境部署（手把手）

### 步骤 1：购买阿里云服务器（ECS）

推荐配置：
- **规格**：4核 8GB（ecs.g7.large 或类似）
- **系统**：Ubuntu 22.04 LTS（推荐）
- **硬盘**：100GB SSD
- **带宽**：5Mbps 起步（根据业务量调整）
- **地域**：选择离你客户最近的区域

### 步骤 2：安全组配置（必须开放以下端口）

| 端口 | 用途 | 来源 |
| :--- | :--- | :--- |
| 22 | SSH 远程登录 | 你的本地 IP（限制） |
| 80 | HTTP 访问 | 0.0.0.0/0 |
| 443 | HTTPS 访问（可选） | 0.0.0.0/0 |
| 8000 | Backend API（调试用，建议仅限内网） | 127.0.0.1 |

### 步骤 3：SSH 登录服务器

```bash
ssh -i your-key.pem root@你的服务器公网IP
```

### 步骤 4：安装 Docker 和 Docker Compose

```bash
# 更新系统
apt update && apt upgrade -y

# 安装 Docker
curl -fsSL https://get.docker.com | bash

# 安装 Docker Compose
curl -L "https://github.com/docker/compose/releases/latest/download/docker-compose-$(uname -s)-$(uname -m)" -o /usr/local/bin/docker-compose
chmod +x /usr/local/bin/docker-compose

# 验证安装
docker --version
docker-compose --version
```

### 步骤 5：创建项目目录

```bash
mkdir -p /opt/waos
cd /opt/waos
```

### 步骤 6：创建环境变量文件（`.env.production`）

```bash
cat > .env.production << 'EOF'
# 数据库
DB_PASSWORD=生成一个强密码（如 Waos@2024#Secure!）

# JWT 密钥（务必改）
JWT_SECRET=生成一个随机字符串（openssl rand -base64 32）

# LLM 配置
OPENAI_API_KEY=sk-你的OpenAI API Key
OPENAI_MODEL=gpt-4o-mini
LLM_PROVIDER=openai

# Qdrant
QDRANT_API_KEY=你的Qdrant API Key（如果有）

# 环境
ENVIRONMENT=production
LOG_LEVEL=INFO

# 阿里云内网通信（使用容器名）
DATABASE_URL=postgresql://waos:${DB_PASSWORD}@postgres:5432/waos
REDIS_URL=redis://redis:6379/0
QDRANT_HOST=qdrant
EOF
```

### 步骤 7：创建 `docker-compose.prod.yml`

```yaml
version: "3.9"

services:
  postgres:
    image: postgres:15
    restart: always
    container_name: waos-postgres
    environment:
      POSTGRES_USER: waos
      POSTGRES_PASSWORD: ${DB_PASSWORD}
      POSTGRES_DB: waos
    volumes:
      - pg_data:/var/lib/postgresql/data
    healthcheck:
      test: ["CMD-SHELL", "pg_isready -U waos"]
      interval: 30s
      timeout: 10s
      retries: 5
    logging:
      driver: "json-file"
      options:
        max-size: "10m"
        max-file: "3"

  redis:
    image: redis:7-alpine
    restart: always
    container_name: waos-redis
    command: redis-server --appendonly yes --maxmemory 512mb --maxmemory-policy allkeys-lru
    volumes:
      - redis_data:/data
    healthcheck:
      test: ["CMD", "redis-cli", "ping"]
      interval: 30s
      timeout: 10s
    logging:
      driver: "json-file"
      options:
        max-size: "10m"
        max-file: "3"

  qdrant:
    image: qdrant/qdrant
    restart: always
    container_name: waos-qdrant
    volumes:
      - qdrant_data:/qdrant/storage
    environment:
      - QDRANT__SERVICE__API_KEY=${QDRANT_API_KEY:-}
    logging:
      driver: "json-file"
      options:
        max-size: "10m"
        max-file: "3"

  backend:
    build: ./backend
    restart: always
    container_name: waos-backend
    ports:
      - "8000:8000"
    depends_on:
      postgres:
        condition: service_healthy
      redis:
        condition: service_healthy
    environment:
      - DATABASE_URL=${DATABASE_URL}
      - REDIS_URL=${REDIS_URL}
      - QDRANT_HOST=${QDRANT_HOST}
      - OPENAI_API_KEY=${OPENAI_API_KEY}
      - OPENAI_MODEL=${OPENAI_MODEL}
      - LLM_PROVIDER=${LLM_PROVIDER}
      - JWT_SECRET=${JWT_SECRET}
      - ENVIRONMENT=${ENVIRONMENT}
      - LOG_LEVEL=${LOG_LEVEL}
    logging:
      driver: "json-file"
      options:
        max-size: "10m"
        max-file: "3"
    healthcheck:
      test: ["CMD", "curl", "-f", "http://localhost:8000/health/ping"]
      interval: 60s
      timeout: 5s
      retries: 3

  worker:
    build: ./backend
    restart: always
    container_name: waos-worker
    command: python -m app.worker.event_consumer
    depends_on:
      redis:
        condition: service_healthy
    environment:
      - DATABASE_URL=${DATABASE_URL}
      - REDIS_URL=${REDIS_URL}
      - QDRANT_HOST=${QDRANT_HOST}
      - OPENAI_API_KEY=${OPENAI_API_KEY}
      - OPENAI_MODEL=${OPENAI_MODEL}
      - LLM_PROVIDER=${LLM_PROVIDER}
      - JWT_SECRET=${JWT_SECRET}
      - ENVIRONMENT=${ENVIRONMENT}
      - LOG_LEVEL=${LOG_LEVEL}
    logging:
      driver: "json-file"
      options:
        max-size: "10m"
        max-file: "3"

  campaign_worker:
    build: ./backend
    restart: always
    container_name: waos-campaign-worker
    command: python -m app.worker.campaign_worker
    depends_on:
      redis:
        condition: service_healthy
    environment:
      - DATABASE_URL=${DATABASE_URL}
      - REDIS_URL=${REDIS_URL}
      - OPENAI_API_KEY=${OPENAI_API_KEY}
      - JWT_SECRET=${JWT_SECRET}
      - ENVIRONMENT=${ENVIRONMENT}
    logging:
      driver: "json-file"
      options:
        max-size: "10m"
        max-file: "3"

  moment_scheduler:
    build: ./backend
    restart: always
    container_name: waos-moment-scheduler
    command: python -m app.worker.moment_scheduler_runner
    depends_on:
      redis:
        condition: service_healthy
    environment:
      - DATABASE_URL=${DATABASE_URL}
      - REDIS_URL=${REDIS_URL}
      - OPENAI_API_KEY=${OPENAI_API_KEY}
      - JWT_SECRET=${JWT_SECRET}
      - ENVIRONMENT=${ENVIRONMENT}
    logging:
      driver: "json-file"
      options:
        max-size: "10m"
        max-file: "3"

  frontend:
    build: ./frontend
    restart: always
    container_name: waos-frontend
    ports:
      - "3000:3000"
    depends_on:
      - backend
    logging:
      driver: "json-file"
      options:
        max-size: "10m"
        max-file: "3"

volumes:
  pg_data:
    driver: local
  redis_data:
    driver: local
  qdrant_data:
    driver: local
```

### 步骤 8：创建 Nginx 配置（可选，但强烈建议）

```bash
mkdir -p /opt/waos/infra/nginx

cat > /opt/waos/infra/nginx/nginx.conf << 'EOF'
upstream backend {
    server backend:8000;
}

upstream frontend {
    server frontend:3000;
}

server {
    listen 80;
    server_name _;

    client_max_body_size 50M;
    proxy_read_timeout 300s;

    location /api {
        proxy_pass http://backend;
        proxy_set_header Host $host;
        proxy_set_header X-Real-IP $remote_addr;
        proxy_set_header X-Forwarded-For $proxy_add_x_forwarded_for;
    }

    location /ws {
        proxy_pass http://backend;
        proxy_http_version 1.1;
        proxy_set_header Upgrade $http_upgrade;
        proxy_set_header Connection "upgrade";
        proxy_set_header Host $host;
        proxy_read_timeout 86400;
    }

    location / {
        proxy_pass http://frontend;
        proxy_set_header Host $host;
        proxy_set_header X-Real-IP $remote_addr;
    }
}
EOF
```

### 步骤 12：配置 Docker 开机自启（阿里云重启后自动恢复）

```bash
# 启用 Docker 服务开机自启
systemctl enable docker
systemctl enable containerd

# 修改 docker-compose 自动拉起（需配合 systemd 服务，简化版）
# 编辑 /etc/rc.local
cat >> /etc/rc.local << 'EOF'
#!/bin/bash
cd /opt/waos && docker-compose -f docker-compose.prod.yml up -d
exit 0
EOF
chmod +x /etc/rc.local
```

```yaml
version: "3.9"

services:
  postgres:
    image: postgres:15
    container_name: waos-dev-postgres
    ports:
      - "5432:5432"
    environment:
      POSTGRES_USER: waos
      POSTGRES_PASSWORD: waos123
      POSTGRES_DB: waos
    volumes:
      - dev_pg_data:/var/lib/postgresql/data

  redis:
    image: redis:7-alpine
    container_name: waos-dev-redis
    ports:
      - "6379:6379"
    volumes:
      - dev_redis_data:/data

  qdrant:
    image: qdrant/qdrant
    container_name: waos-dev-qdrant
    ports:
      - "6333:6333"
    volumes:
      - dev_qdrant_data:/qdrant/storage

volumes:
  dev_pg_data:
  dev_redis_data:
  dev_qdrant_data:
```

#### 本地启动命令
```bash
# 1. 启动基础服务（PostgreSQL/Redis/Qdrant）
docker-compose -f docker-compose.dev.yml up -d

# 2. 启动 Backend（开发模式，支持热重载）
cd backend
pip install -r requirements.txt
uvicorn app.main:app --reload --host 0.0.0.0 --port 8000

# 3. 启动 Worker（另开一个终端）
cd backend
python -m app.worker.event_consumer

# 4. 启动前端（开发模式）
cd frontend
npm install
npm run dev

# 5. 访问 http://localhost:3000
```

# 🚀 WAOS 微信真实对接层（ClawBot Adapter V1）

## 📋 整体架构

## 📦 一、ClawBot 适配器核心接口

### 1. 统一适配器抽象（扩展 BaseAdapter）

#### `backend/app/adapters/base.py`（新增方法）
```python
from abc import ABC, abstractmethod
from typing import Optional, List, Dict, Any

class BaseAdapter(ABC):
    """统一平台适配器抽象基类"""
    
    # ===== 消息相关 =====
    @abstractmethod
    async def send_text(self, to: str, content: str) -> dict:
        """发送文本消息"""
        pass
    
    @abstractmethod
    async def send_image(self, to: str, image_url: str) -> dict:
        """发送图片消息"""
        pass
    
    @abstractmethod
    async def send_file(self, to: str, file_url: str) -> dict:
        """发送文件"""
        pass
    
    @abstractmethod
    async def get_messages(self, account_id: str, since: Optional[str] = None) -> List[dict]:
        """拉取消息（增量）"""
        pass
    
    # ===== 朋友圈 =====
    @abstractmethod
    async def send_moment(self, account_id: str, content: str, images: List[str] = None) -> dict:
        """发送朋友圈"""
        pass
    
    @abstractmethod
    async def get_moments(self, account_id: str, limit: int = 20) -> List[dict]:
        """获取朋友圈列表"""
        pass
    
    # ===== 联系人 =====
    @abstractmethod
    async def get_contacts(self, account_id: str) -> List[dict]:
        """获取联系人列表"""
        pass
    
    @abstractmethod
    async def get_contact_detail(self, account_id: str, wx_id: str) -> dict:
        """获取联系人详情"""
        pass
    
    # ===== 登录/状态 =====
    @abstractmethod
    async def login(self, account_id: str) -> dict:
        """登录（获取二维码/Token）"""
        pass
    
    @abstractmethod
    async def logout(self, account_id: str) -> bool:
        """登出"""
        pass
    
    @abstractmethod
    async def get_status(self, account_id: str) -> dict:
        """获取账号状态"""
        pass
    
    @abstractmethod
    async def heartbeat(self, account_id: str) -> bool:
        """心跳保活"""
        pass
```

---

### 2. ClawBot 真实适配器实现

#### `backend/app/adapters/clawbot/adapter.py`
```python
import json
import time
import asyncio
import aiohttp
from typing import Optional, List, Dict, Any
from urllib.parse import urljoin

from app.adapters.base import BaseAdapter
from app.adapters.clawbot.session_manager import SessionManager
from app.adapters.clawbot.message_normalizer import MessageNormalizer
from app.utils.logger import logger
from app.utils.redis_client import redis_client

class ClawBotAdapter(BaseAdapter):
    """
    ClawBot 真实 API 适配器
    
    对接 ClawBot HTTP API：
    - GET  /api/messages     拉取消息
    - POST /api/send/text    发送文本
    - POST /api/send/image   发送图片
    - POST /api/login        登录
    - GET  /api/status       获取状态
    - POST /api/heartbeat    心跳
    - GET  /api/contacts     获取联系人
    """
    
    def __init__(self, base_url: str = None, api_key: str = None):
        self.base_url = base_url or "http://clawbot:8080/api"
        self.api_key = api_key or ""
        self.session = None
        self._session_manager = SessionManager()
    
    async def _ensure_session(self):
        """确保 HTTP 会话存在"""
        if self.session is None:
            self.session = aiohttp.ClientSession(
                timeout=aiohttp.ClientTimeout(total=30),
                headers={
                    "Authorization": f"Bearer {self.api_key}",
                    "Content-Type": "application/json"
                }
            )
        return self.session
    
    async def _request(self, method: str, path: str, data: dict = None) -> dict:
        """统一 HTTP 请求（带重试）"""
        session = await self._ensure_session()
        url = urljoin(self.base_url, path)
        
        max_retries = 3
        for attempt in range(max_retries):
            try:
                async with session.request(method, url, json=data) as resp:
                    if resp.status == 429:  # 限流
                        wait = 2 ** attempt + 1
                        logger.warning(f"ClawBot rate limited, retry in {wait}s")
                        await asyncio.sleep(wait)
                        continue
                    
                    if resp.status >= 500:
                        wait = 2 ** attempt + 1
                        logger.warning(f"ClawBot server error {resp.status}, retry in {wait}s")
                        await asyncio.sleep(wait)
                        continue
                    
                    result = await resp.json()
                    if result.get("code") != 0:
                        logger.error(f"ClawBot API error: {result}")
                        return {"code": result.get("code", -1), "msg": result.get("msg", "unknown error")}
                    
                    return result
                    
            except aiohttp.ClientError as e:
                logger.error(f"ClawBot request error: {e}")
                if attempt == max_retries - 1:
                    raise
                await asyncio.sleep(2 ** attempt)
        
        return {"code": -1, "msg": "max retries exceeded"}
    
    # ===== 消息发送 =====
    
    async def send_text(self, to: str, content: str) -> dict:
        """发送文本消息"""
        return await self._request(
            "POST", "/send/text",
            {"to": to, "content": content}
        )
    
    async def send_image(self, to: str, image_url: str) -> dict:
        """发送图片消息"""
        return await self._request(
            "POST", "/send/image",
            {"to": to, "image_url": image_url}
        )
    
    async def send_file(self, to: str, file_url: str) -> dict:
        """发送文件"""
        return await self._request(
            "POST", "/send/file",
            {"to": to, "file_url": file_url}
        )
    
    # ===== 消息拉取 =====
    
    async def get_messages(self, account_id: str, since: Optional[str] = None) -> List[dict]:
        """拉取消息（增量）"""
        params = {"account_id": account_id}
        if since:
            params["since"] = since
        
        result = await self._request("GET", "/messages", params)
        if result.get("code") == 0:
            return result.get("data", [])
        return []
    
    # ===== 朋友圈 =====
    
    async def send_moment(self, account_id: str, content: str, images: List[str] = None) -> dict:
        """发送朋友圈"""
        return await self._request(
            "POST", "/moment/send",
            {"account_id": account_id, "content": content, "images": images or []}
        )
    
    async def get_moments(self, account_id: str, limit: int = 20) -> List[dict]:
        """获取朋友圈列表"""
        result = await self._request(
            "GET", "/moment/list",
            {"account_id": account_id, "limit": limit}
        )
        if result.get("code") == 0:
            return result.get("data", [])
        return []
    
    # ===== 联系人 =====
    
    async def get_contacts(self, account_id: str) -> List[dict]:
        """获取联系人列表"""
        result = await self._request(
            "GET", "/contacts",
            {"account_id": account_id}
        )
        if result.get("code") == 0:
            return result.get("data", [])
        return []
    
    async def get_contact_detail(self, account_id: str, wx_id: str) -> dict:
        """获取联系人详情"""
        result = await self._request(
            "GET", f"/contacts/{wx_id}",
            {"account_id": account_id}
        )
        if result.get("code") == 0:
            return result.get("data", {})
        return {}
    
    # ===== 登录/状态 =====
    
    async def login(self, account_id: str) -> dict:
        """
        登录：返回二维码或登录态
        实际 ClawBot 可能通过 WebSocket 或轮询返回二维码
        """
        result = await self._request(
            "POST", "/login",
            {"account_id": account_id}
        )
        if result.get("code") == 0:
            data = result.get("data", {})
            # 保存登录态到 Redis
            await self._session_manager.save_session(
                account_id,
                token=data.get("token"),
                status="online",
                extra={"qr_code": data.get("qr_code")}
            )
        return result
    
    async def logout(self, account_id: str) -> bool:
        """登出"""
        result = await self._request(
            "POST", "/logout",
            {"account_id": account_id}
        )
        if result.get("code") == 0:
            await self._session_manager.clear_session(account_id)
            return True
        return False
    
    async def get_status(self, account_id: str) -> dict:
        """获取账号状态"""
        result = await self._request(
            "GET", "/status",
            {"account_id": account_id}
        )
        if result.get("code") == 0:
            data = result.get("data", {})
            # 更新 Redis 中的状态
            await self._session_manager.update_status(account_id, data.get("status", "unknown"))
            return data
        return {"status": "offline"}
    
    async def heartbeat(self, account_id: str) -> bool:
        """心跳保活"""
        result = await self._request(
            "POST", "/heartbeat",
            {"account_id": account_id}
        )
        if result.get("code") == 0:
            await self._session_manager.update_heartbeat(account_id)
            return True
        return False
    
    async def close(self):
        """关闭 HTTP 会话"""
        if self.session:
            await self.session.close()
            self.session = None
```

---

## 📦 二、Session 管理器（Redis 持久化）

#### `backend/app/adapters/clawbot/session_manager.py`
```python
import json
import time
from typing import Optional, Dict, Any
from datetime import datetime

from app.utils.redis_client import redis_client
from app.utils.logger import logger

class SessionManager:
    """
    微信账号会话管理器（Redis 持久化）
    
    Key 结构：
    - waos:wechat:session:{account_id}    → 会话详情（Hash）
    - waos:wechat:heartbeat:{account_id}  → 心跳时间戳（String）
    - waos:wechat:sync:{account_id}       → 同步游标（String）
    """
    
    SESSION_TTL = 86400 * 7  # 7天
    HEARTBEAT_TTL = 300      # 5分钟
    
    @staticmethod
    def _session_key(account_id: str) -> str:
        return f"waos:wechat:session:{account_id}"
    
    @staticmethod
    def _heartbeat_key(account_id: str) -> str:
        return f"waos:wechat:heartbeat:{account_id}"
    
    @staticmethod
    def _sync_key(account_id: str) -> str:
        return f"waos:wechat:sync:{account_id}"
    
    async def save_session(self, account_id: str, token: str, status: str = "online", extra: dict = None):
        """保存会话"""
        session_data = {
            "account_id": account_id,
            "token": token,
            "status": status,
            "last_heartbeat": time.time(),
            "updated_at": time.time(),
            "extra": json.dumps(extra or {})
        }
        
        redis_client.hset(
            self._session_key(account_id),
            mapping=session_data
        )
        redis_client.expire(self._session_key(account_id), self.SESSION_TTL)
        
        # 更新心跳
        redis_client.setex(
            self._heartbeat_key(account_id),
            self.HEARTBEAT_TTL,
            str(time.time())
        )
        
        logger.info(f"Session saved for account {account_id}, status: {status}")
    
    async def get_session(self, account_id: str) -> Optional[Dict[str, Any]]:
        """获取会话"""
        data = redis_client.hgetall(self._session_key(account_id))
        if not data:
            return None
        
        # 解码 bytes
        result = {}
        for k, v in data.items():
            if isinstance(k, bytes):
                k = k.decode()
            if isinstance(v, bytes):
                v = v.decode()
            result[k] = v
        
        if result.get("extra"):
            result["extra"] = json.loads(result["extra"])
        
        return result
    
    async def update_status(self, account_id: str, status: str):
        """更新状态"""
        redis_client.hset(self._session_key(account_id), "status", status)
        redis_client.hset(self._session_key(account_id), "updated_at", time.time())
        logger.info(f"Account {account_id} status updated to: {status}")
    
    async def update_heartbeat(self, account_id: str):
        """更新心跳"""
        redis_client.setex(
            self._heartbeat_key(account_id),
            self.HEARTBEAT_TTL,
            str(time.time())
        )
        redis_client.hset(self._session_key(account_id), "last_heartbeat", time.time())
    
    async def get_heartbeat(self, account_id: str) -> Optional[float]:
        """获取最后心跳时间"""
        data = redis_client.get(self._heartbeat_key(account_id))
        if data:
            return float(data)
        return None
    
    async def is_online(self, account_id: str) -> bool:
        """检查是否在线"""
        session = await self.get_session(account_id)
        if not session:
            return False
        
        if session.get("status") != "online":
            return False
        
        # 检查心跳是否超时（超过5分钟无心跳视为离线）
        last_heartbeat = await self.get_heartbeat(account_id)
        if last_heartbeat:
            if time.time() - last_heartbeat > 300:
                return False
        
        return True
    
    async def get_sync_cursor(self, account_id: str) -> str:
        """获取同步游标"""
        cursor = redis_client.get(self._sync_key(account_id))
        return cursor.decode() if cursor else "0"
    
    async def update_sync_cursor(self, account_id: str, cursor: str):
        """更新同步游标"""
        redis_client.setex(self._sync_key(account_id), 86400, cursor)
    
    async def clear_session(self, account_id: str):
        """清除会话"""
        redis_client.delete(self._session_key(account_id))
        redis_client.delete(self._heartbeat_key(account_id))
        logger.info(f"Session cleared for account {account_id}")
```

## 📦 三、消息标准化处理器

#### `backend/app/adapters/clawbot/message_normalizer.py`
```python
import uuid
import time
from typing import Dict, Any, Optional

from app.core.event import Event

class MessageNormalizer:
    """
    消息标准化：ClawBot 格式 → WAOS 统一事件
    """
    
    # ClawBot 消息类型映射
    MSG_TYPE_MAP = {
        "text": "text",
        "image": "image",
        "voice": "voice",
        "video": "video",
        "file": "file",
        "system": "system"
    }
    
    @staticmethod
    def normalize(raw_msg: Dict[str, Any], account_id: str) -> Optional[Event]:
        """
        将 ClawBot 原始消息转换为 WAOS Event
        
        原始消息格式（ClawBot 通常返回）：
        {
            "msg_id": "xxx",
            "from": "wxid_xxx",
            "to": "wxid_yyy",
            "type": "text",
            "content": "你好",
            "time": 1700000000
        }
        """
        try:
            # 1. 提取基本字段
            msg_id = raw_msg.get("msg_id") or raw_msg.get("id")
            from_user = raw_msg.get("from") or raw_msg.get("sender")
            content = raw_msg.get("content") or raw_msg.get("text")
            msg_type = raw_msg.get("type", "text")
            timestamp = raw_msg.get("time", time.time())
            
            if not from_user or not content:
                return None
            
            # 2. 构造 Event
            return Event(
                user=from_user,
                content=content,
                platform="wechat",
                account_id=account_id,
                event_id=msg_id or str(uuid.uuid4()),
                timestamp=float(timestamp)
            )
            
        except Exception as e:
            import logging
            logging.error(f"Message normalize error: {e}, raw: {raw_msg}")
            return None
    
    @staticmethod
    def normalize_contact(raw_contact: Dict[str, Any]) -> Dict[str, Any]:
        """
        标准化联系人数据
        """
        return {
            "wx_id": raw_contact.get("wx_id") or raw_contact.get("id"),
            "nickname": raw_contact.get("nickname", ""),
            "remark": raw_contact.get("remark", ""),
            "avatar": raw_contact.get("avatar", ""),
            "gender": raw_contact.get("gender", 0),
            "province": raw_contact.get("province", ""),
            "city": raw_contact.get("city", ""),
            "signature": raw_contact.get("signature", ""),
            "raw": raw_contact
        }
```

## 📦 四、消息监听服务（持续运行）

#### `backend/app/services/wechat_listener.py`
```python
import asyncio
import time
from typing import List, Dict, Any
from datetime import datetime

from app.adapters.clawbot.adapter import ClawBotAdapter
from app.adapters.clawbot.session_manager import SessionManager
from app.adapters.clawbot.message_normalizer import MessageNormalizer
from app.core.pipeline import pipeline
from app.core.event_bus import publish_event
from app.core.context import set_tenant_id
from app.utils.logger import logger
from app.utils.redis_client import redis_client

class WeChatListener:
    """
    微信消息监听器（7x24 持续运行）
    
    功能：
    1. 多账号消息拉取
    2. 增量同步
    3. 自动重连
    4. 心跳保活
    """
    
    def __init__(self, adapter: ClawBotAdapter = None):
        self.adapter = adapter or ClawBotAdapter()
        self.session_manager = SessionManager()
        self.is_running = False
        self.poll_interval = 1.0  # 秒
    
    async def start(self):
        """启动监听器"""
        self.is_running = True
        logger.info("WeChat Listener started")
        
        # 获取所有活跃账号
        while self.is_running:
            try:
                accounts = await self._get_active_accounts()
                
                for account_id in accounts:
                    await self._process_account(account_id)
                
                await asyncio.sleep(self.poll_interval)
                
            except Exception as e:
                logger.error(f"Listener loop error: {e}")
                await asyncio.sleep(5)
    
    async def stop(self):
        """停止监听器"""
        self.is_running = False
        await self.adapter.close()
        logger.info("WeChat Listener stopped")
    
    async def _get_active_accounts(self) -> List[str]:
        """获取所有活跃账号"""
        # 从 Redis 获取已登录的账号列表
        keys = redis_client.keys("waos:wechat:session:*")
        accounts = []
        for key in keys:
            if isinstance(key, bytes):
                key = key.decode()
            account_id = key.replace("waos:wechat:session:", "")
            # 检查是否在线
            if await self.session_manager.is_online(account_id):
                accounts.append(account_id)
        return accounts
    
    async def _process_account(self, account_id: str):
        """处理单个账号的消息拉取"""
        try:
            # 1. 心跳保活
            await self.adapter.heartbeat(account_id)
            
            # 2. 获取同步游标
            since = await self.session_manager.get_sync_cursor(account_id)
            
            # 3. 拉取消息
            raw_messages = await self.adapter.get_messages(account_id, since=since)
            
            if not raw_messages:
                return
            
            # 4. 处理每条消息
            latest_cursor = since
            for raw_msg in raw_messages:
                # 标准化
                event = MessageNormalizer.normalize(raw_msg, account_id)
                if event:
                    # 处理消息（进入 Pipeline）
                    # 需要先设置租户上下文（从账号获取 tenant_id）
                    tenant_id = await self._get_tenant_by_account(account_id)
                    if tenant_id:
                        set_tenant_id(tenant_id)
                    
                    # 异步处理（不阻塞拉取）
                    asyncio.create_task(pipeline(event))
                
                # 更新游标
                msg_id = raw_msg.get("msg_id") or raw_msg.get("id")
                if msg_id:
                    latest_cursor = msg_id
            
            # 5. 保存最新游标
            if latest_cursor != since:
                await self.session_manager.update_sync_cursor(account_id, latest_cursor)
                
        except Exception as e:
            logger.error(f"Process account {account_id} error: {e}")
    
    async def _get_tenant_by_account(self, account_id: str) -> str:
        """根据账号获取租户ID"""
        # 从账号表查询 tenant_id
        # 实际从 DB 查询：SELECT tenant_id FROM accounts WHERE id = account_id
        # 这里简化，从 Redis 获取
        session = await self.session_manager.get_session(account_id)
        if session and session.get("extra"):
            return session["extra"].get("tenant_id")
        return None
```
