## 📦 五、消息发送服务（统一出口）

#### `backend/app/services/wechat_sender.py`
```python
import asyncio
from typing import Optional
from datetime import datetime

from app.adapters.clawbot.adapter import ClawBotAdapter
from app.adapters.clawbot.session_manager import SessionManager
from app.core.event_bus import consume_events
from app.models.task import Task
from app.db.session import get_db_session
from app.utils.logger import logger
from app.utils.redis_client import redis_client

class WeChatSender:
    """
    微信消息发送服务（从任务队列消费）
    
    监听 Redis Stream: waos.tasks
    处理 task_type = SEND_MESSAGE / SEND_IMAGE
    """
    
    def __init__(self, adapter: ClawBotAdapter = None):
        self.adapter = adapter or ClawBotAdapter()
        self.session_manager = SessionManager()
        self.is_running = False
    
    async def start(self):
        """启动发送服务"""
        self.is_running = True
        logger.info("WeChat Sender started")
        
        while self.is_running:
            try:
                # 从 Redis Stream 消费任务
                events = await self._consume_tasks()
                
                for event in events:
                    await self._process_task(event)
                    
            except Exception as e:
                logger.error(f"Sender loop error: {e}")
                await asyncio.sleep(1)
    
    async def stop(self):
        self.is_running = False
        await self.adapter.close()
        logger.info("WeChat Sender stopped")
    
    async def _consume_tasks(self):
        """从 Redis Stream 拉取任务"""
        # 使用 Redis Stream 的 XREADGROUP
        try:
            result = redis_client.xreadgroup(
                groupname="wechat_sender_group",
                consumername="sender_1",
                streams={"waos.tasks": ">"},
                count=10,
                block=1000
            )
            
            events = []
            if result:
                for stream, messages in result:
                    for msg_id, data in messages:
                        # 解析任务
                        task_data = data.get(b'payload')
                        if task_data:
                            import json
                            events.append(json.loads(task_data))
                        # ACK
                        redis_client.xack("waos.tasks", "wechat_sender_group", msg_id)
            
            return events
            
        except Exception as e:
            logger.error(f"Consume tasks error: {e}")
            return []
    
    async def _process_task(self, task: dict):
        """处理单个发送任务"""
        task_id = task.get("task_id")
        task_type = task.get("task_type")
        target = task.get("target")  # wx_id
        content = task.get("content")
        account_id = task.get("account_id")
        
        if not target or not content:
            return
        
        try:
            # 1. 检查账号是否在线
            if not await self.session_manager.is_online(account_id):
                logger.warning(f"Account {account_id} offline, task {task_id} skipped")
                await self._mark_task_failed(task_id, "account offline")
                return
            
            # 2. 发送消息
            if task_type == "SEND_MESSAGE" or task_type == "SEND_TEXT":
                result = await self.adapter.send_text(target, content)
            elif task_type == "SEND_IMAGE":
                result = await self.adapter.send_image(target, content)
            else:
                logger.warning(f"Unknown task type: {task_type}")
                return
            
            # 3. 处理结果
            if result.get("code") == 0:
                await self._mark_task_success(task_id)
                logger.info(f"Task {task_id} sent successfully to {target}")
            else:
                await self._mark_task_failed(task_id, result.get("msg", "unknown error"))
                logger.error(f"Task {task_id} failed: {result}")
                
        except Exception as e:
            logger.error(f"Process task {task_id} error: {e}")
            await self._mark_task_failed(task_id, str(e))
    
    async def _mark_task_success(self, task_id: str):
        """标记任务成功"""
        with get_db_session() as db:
            task = db.query(Task).filter(Task.id == task_id).first()
            if task:
                task.status = "done"
                db.commit()
    
    async def _mark_task_failed(self, task_id: str, error: str):
        """标记任务失败"""
        with get_db_session() as db:
            task = db.query(Task).filter(Task.id == task_id).first()
            if task:
                task.status = "failed"
                task.retry += 1
                db.commit()
```

## 📦 六、账号管理 API

#### `backend/app/api/accounts.py`（扩展现有）
```python
from fastapi import APIRouter, Depends, HTTPException
from pydantic import BaseModel
from typing import Optional
from uuid import UUID

from app.dependencies.auth import get_current_tenant
from app.adapters.clawbot.adapter import ClawBotAdapter
from app.adapters.clawbot.session_manager import SessionManager
from app.models.account import Account
from app.db.session import get_db_session
from app.utils.logger import logger

router = APIRouter(prefix="/api/accounts", tags=["accounts"])

class AccountLoginRequest(BaseModel):
    account_id: str
    platform: str = "wechat"

class AccountLoginResponse(BaseModel):
    account_id: str
    status: str
    qr_code: Optional[str] = None
    message: str

@router.post("/login")
async def login_account(
    req: AccountLoginRequest,
    tenant: UUID = Depends(get_current_tenant)
):
    """登录微信账号（触发扫码）"""
    adapter = ClawBotAdapter()
    session_manager = SessionManager()
    
    try:
        # 调用 ClawBot 登录
        result = await adapter.login(req.account_id)
        
        if result.get("code") == 0:
            data = result.get("data", {})
            return AccountLoginResponse(
                account_id=req.account_id,
                status="pending",
                qr_code=data.get("qr_code"),
                message="请扫描二维码登录"
            )
        else:
            raise HTTPException(status_code=400, detail=result.get("msg", "Login failed"))
            
    except Exception as e:
        logger.error(f"Login error: {e}")
        raise HTTPException(status_code=500, detail=str(e))

@router.post("/logout/{account_id}")
async def logout_account(
    account_id: str,
    tenant: UUID = Depends(get_current_tenant)
):
    """登出微信账号"""
    adapter = ClawBotAdapter()
    session_manager = SessionManager()
    
    try:
        await adapter.logout(account_id)
        return {"status": "ok", "message": "Logged out"}
    except Exception as e:
        raise HTTPException(status_code=500, detail=str(e))

@router.get("/{account_id}/status")
async def get_account_status(
    account_id: str,
    tenant: UUID = Depends(get_current_tenant)
):
    """获取账号状态"""
    session_manager = SessionManager()
    
    try:
        is_online = await session_manager.is_online(account_id)
        session = await session_manager.get_session(account_id)
        
        return {
            "account_id": account_id,
            "is_online": is_online,
            "status": session.get("status", "unknown") if session else "not_found",
            "last_heartbeat": session.get("last_heartbeat") if session else None
        }
    except Exception as e:
        raise HTTPException(status_code=500, detail=str(e))

@router.get("/online")
async def get_online_accounts(
    tenant: UUID = Depends(get_current_tenant)
):
    """获取所有在线账号"""
    session_manager = SessionManager()
    
    try:
        # 从 Redis 获取所有已登录账号
        import redis
        from app.utils.redis_client import redis_client
        
        keys = redis_client.keys("waos:wechat:session:*")
        accounts = []
        for key in keys:
            if isinstance(key, bytes):
                key = key.decode()
            account_id = key.replace("waos:wechat:session:", "")
            if await session_manager.is_online(account_id):
                accounts.append(account_id)
        
        return {"accounts": accounts, "count": len(accounts)}
        
    except Exception as e:
        raise HTTPException(status_code=500, detail=str(e))
```

## 📦 七、启动脚本（整合所有服务）

#### `backend/app/runner.py`
```python
"""
WAOS 启动器 - 整合所有后台服务
"""
import asyncio
import signal
import sys

from app.services.wechat_listener import WeChatListener
from app.services.wechat_sender import WeChatSender
from app.worker.event_consumer import consume_loop
from app.worker.campaign_worker import run_campaign_batch
from app.worker.moment_scheduler_runner import moment_scheduler_loop
from app.utils.logger import logger

async def main():
    logger.info("=" * 60)
    logger.info("WAOS Worker Started")
    logger.info("=" * 60)
    
    # 1. 微信消息监听器
    listener = WeChatListener()
    listener_task = asyncio.create_task(listener.start())
    
    # 2. 微信消息发送器
    sender = WeChatSender()
    sender_task = asyncio.create_task(sender.start())
    
    # 3. 事件消费者（Pipeline 处理）
    consumer_task = asyncio.create_task(consume_loop())
    
    # 4. Campaign 调度器（已由 APScheduler 管理，此处不重复启动）
    # 5. Moment 调度器
    moment_task = asyncio.create_task(moment_scheduler_loop())
    
    # 等待所有任务
    try:
        await asyncio.gather(
            listener_task,
            sender_task,
            consumer_task,
            moment_task
        )
    except KeyboardInterrupt:
        logger.info("Shutting down...")
        listener.stop()
        sender.stop()
    
    logger.info("WAOS Worker Stopped")

if __name__ == "__main__":
    asyncio.run(main())
```

## 📦 一、本地集成验证脚本

#### `scripts/test_e2e.sh`
```bash
#!/bin/bash
# WAOS 端到端集成测试脚本
# 用途：验证所有组件是否正确协作

set -e

echo "=========================================="
echo "  WAOS 端到端集成测试"
echo "=========================================="

# 1. 检查依赖服务
echo ""
echo "[1/6] 检查依赖服务状态..."

if ! command -v docker &> /dev/null; then
    echo "❌ Docker 未安装，请先安装 Docker"
    exit 1
fi

if ! command -v docker-compose &> /dev/null; then
    echo "⚠️  docker-compose 未安装，尝试使用 docker compose"
    DOCKER_COMPOSE="docker compose"
else
    DOCKER_COMPOSE="docker-compose"
fi

echo "✅ Docker 已安装"

# 2. 启动基础服务
echo ""
echo "[2/6] 启动 PostgreSQL、Redis、Qdrant..."

cd "$(dirname "$0")/.."

$DOCKER_COMPOSE -f docker-compose.dev.yml up -d

# 等待服务就绪
sleep 5

# 检查服务健康
echo "检查 PostgreSQL..."
if docker exec waos-dev-postgres pg_isready -U waos &> /dev/null; then
    echo "✅ PostgreSQL 已就绪"
else
    echo "❌ PostgreSQL 未就绪"
    exit 1
fi

echo "检查 Redis..."
if docker exec waos-dev-redis redis-cli ping &> /dev/null; then
    echo "✅ Redis 已就绪"
else
    echo "❌ Redis 未就绪"
    exit 1
fi

echo "检查 Qdrant..."
if curl -s -f http://localhost:6333/collections &> /dev/null; then
    echo "✅ Qdrant 已就绪"
else
    echo "⚠️  Qdrant 未就绪，继续测试..."
fi

# 3. 运行数据库迁移
echo ""
echo "[3/6] 运行数据库迁移..."

cd backend
export DATABASE_URL="postgresql://waos:waos123@localhost:5432/waos"
alembic upgrade head
cd ..

echo "✅ 数据库迁移完成"

# 4. 启动 Backend（后台）
echo ""
echo "[4/6] 启动 Backend 服务..."

cd backend
nohup uvicorn app.main:app --host 0.0.0.0 --port 8000 > /tmp/waos-backend.log 2>&1 &
BACKEND_PID=$!
cd ..

sleep 3

# 检查 Backend 是否启动成功
if curl -s -f http://localhost:8000/health/ping &> /dev/null; then
    echo "✅ Backend 已启动 (PID: $BACKEND_PID)"
else
    echo "❌ Backend 启动失败，查看日志: /tmp/waos-backend.log"
    tail -20 /tmp/waos-backend.log
    exit 1
fi

# 5. 初始化知识库
echo ""
echo "[5/6] 初始化知识库..."

curl -s -X POST http://localhost:8000/api/knowledge/init \
    -H "Content-Type: application/json" \
    -d '{"tenant_id": "test-tenant"}' \
    | jq '.' || echo "⚠️  知识库初始化跳过（等待真实租户）"

# 6. 发送测试消息
echo ""
echo "[6/6] 发送测试消息..."

# 使用模拟微信消息测试整个 Pipeline
TEST_EVENT='{
    "user": "test_user_001",
    "content": "多少钱？",
    "platform": "wechat",
    "account_id": "test_account"
}'

echo "发送测试消息: $TEST_EVENT"

RESPONSE=$(curl -s -X POST http://localhost:8000/api/webhook/wechat \
    -H "Content-Type: application/json" \
    -d "$TEST_EVENT")

if echo "$RESPONSE" | grep -q '"code":0'; then
    echo "✅ 测试消息已接收"
else
    echo "❌ 测试消息发送失败: $RESPONSE"
fi

echo ""
echo "=========================================="
echo "  集成测试完成！"
echo "=========================================="
echo ""
echo "服务地址："
echo "  - Backend API:  http://localhost:8000"
echo "  - API 文档:     http://localhost:8000/docs"
echo "  - 前端:         http://localhost:3000 (需单独启动)"
echo ""
echo "查看日志: tail -f /tmp/waos-backend.log"
echo "停止服务: docker-compose -f docker-compose.dev.yml down && kill $BACKEND_PID"
```

## 📦 四、验证 Checklist

完成上述测试后，手动验证以下项目：

## 📦 一、压测工具配置（Locust）

### 1. 安装压测工具

```bash
pip install locust websocket-client
```

### 2. 压测脚本：`scripts/locustfile.py`

```python
"""
WAOS 压测脚本 - Locust
模拟真实微信消息流量
"""

import json
import time
import random
from locust import HttpUser, task, between, events
from websocket import create_connection

class WAOSUser(HttpUser):
    """模拟微信用户"""
    
    wait_time = between(0.5, 3)  # 模拟人类思考时间
    
    def on_start(self):
        """每个用户启动时执行"""
        self.user_id = f"test_user_{random.randint(10000, 99999)}"
        self.account_id = f"test_account_{random.randint(1, 5)}"
        
        # 模拟登录（获取 JWT Token）
        login_resp = self.client.post("/api/auth/login", json={
            "username": "test_user",
            "password": "test_pass"
        })
        
        if login_resp.status_code == 200:
            self.token = login_resp.json().get("access_token")
            self.client.headers.update({
                "Authorization": f"Bearer {self.token}"
            })
    
    @task(5)  # 权重：高频
    def send_price_query(self):
        """模拟客户询价（高价值意图）"""
        queries = [
            "多少钱？",
            "报价多少？",
            "这个怎么卖？",
            "价格是多少？",
            "有优惠吗？"
        ]
        self._send_message(random.choice(queries))
    
    @task(3)  # 权重：中频
    def send_general_query(self):
        """模拟一般咨询"""
        queries = [
            "你好",
            "在吗？",
            "这个功能是什么？",
            "能介绍一下吗？"
        ]
        self._send_message(random.choice(queries))
    
    @task(1)  # 权重：低频
    def send_spam(self):
        """模拟垃圾消息（测试安全过滤）"""
        queries = [
            "广告",
            "刷单",
            "色情",
            "诈骗"
        ]
        self._send_message(random.choice(queries))
    
    def _send_message(self, content):
        """发送消息"""
        start_time = time.time()
        
        # 模拟微信消息入口
        with self.client.post(
            f"/api/webhook/wechat",
            json={
                "user": self.user_id,
                "content": content,
                "platform": "wechat",
                "account_id": self.account_id,
                "msg_id": f"msg_{int(time.time() * 1000)}"
            },
            catch_response=True
        ) as response:
            if response.status_code == 200:
                # 记录成功
                events.request.fire(
                    request_type="POST",
                    name="/webhook/wechat",
                    response_time=(time.time() - start_time) * 1000,
                    response_length=len(response.text),
                    exception=None
                )
            else:
                # 记录失败
                events.request.fire(
                    request_type="POST",
                    name="/webhook/wechat",
                    response_time=(time.time() - start_time) * 1000,
                    response_length=0,
                    exception=Exception(f"Status {response.status_code}")
                )

class WebSocketUser(HttpUser):
    """模拟 WebSocket 连接（前端用户）"""
    
    wait_time = between(1, 5)
    
    def on_start(self):
        """建立 WebSocket 连接"""
        try:
            self.ws = create_connection("ws://localhost:8000/ws")
            self.ws.send(json.dumps({
                "type": "SYNC",
                "last_seq": "0"
            }))
            self.connected = True
        except Exception as e:
            print(f"WebSocket connection failed: {e}")
            self.connected = False
    
    @task(1)
    def receive_messages(self):
        """模拟前端接收消息"""
        if not self.connected:
            return
        
        try:
            # 设置超时，避免阻塞
            self.ws.settimeout(1.0)
            msg = self.ws.recv()
            
            events.request.fire(
                request_type="WS",
                name="/ws",
                response_time=0,
                response_length=len(msg),
                exception=None
            )
        except Exception:
            # 超时或异常不算失败
            pass
    
    def on_stop(self):
        """关闭 WebSocket 连接"""
        if hasattr(self, 'ws') and self.connected:
            try:
                self.ws.close()
            except:
                pass
```

## 📦 二、压测执行命令

### 1. 启动压测（Web UI 模式）

```bash
cd /path/to/waos
locust -f scripts/locustfile.py --host=http://localhost:8000 --web-host=0.0.0.0 --web-port=8089
```

访问 `http://localhost:8089` 打开 Locust UI：
- **Number of users**：输入 10 开始，逐步增加到 100、500
- **Spawn rate**：输入 2（每秒新增 2 个用户）
- 点击 **Start swarming**

### 2. 命令行模式（无 UI，适合 CI/CD）

```bash
locust -f scripts/locustfile.py --host=http://localhost:8000 --headless -u 100 -r 10 --run-time 60s
```

### 3. 生成压测报告

```bash
locust -f scripts/locustfile.py --host=http://localhost:8000 --headless -u 100 -r 10 --run-time 60s --csv=reports/waos-benchmark
```

## 📦 三、性能基线收集脚本

### `scripts/collect_metrics.sh`
```bash
#!/bin/bash
# 性能指标收集脚本

TIMESTAMP=$(date +%Y%m%d_%H%M%S)
REPORT_DIR="reports/performance"
mkdir -p $REPORT_DIR

echo "=========================================="
echo "  WAOS 性能指标收集"
echo "  时间: $TIMESTAMP"
echo "=========================================="

# 1. 系统资源
echo ""
echo "[1/5] 系统资源..."
top -bn1 | head -20 > $REPORT_DIR/system_top_$TIMESTAMP.txt
free -h > $REPORT_DIR/system_memory_$TIMESTAMP.txt

# 2. Docker 容器资源
echo ""
echo "[2/5] Docker 容器资源..."
docker stats --no-stream > $REPORT_DIR/docker_stats_$TIMESTAMP.txt

# 3. PostgreSQL 连接数
echo ""
echo "[3/5] PostgreSQL 连接数..."
docker exec waos-dev-postgres psql -U waos -c "SELECT count(*) FROM pg_stat_activity;" > $REPORT_DIR/postgres_connections_$TIMESTAMP.txt

# 4. Redis 内存使用
echo ""
echo "[4/5] Redis 内存使用..."
docker exec waos-dev-redis redis-cli INFO memory | grep -E "used_memory_human|maxmemory_human" > $REPORT_DIR/redis_memory_$TIMESTAMP.txt

# 5. Backend 日志错误统计
echo ""
echo "[5/5] 错误日志统计..."
tail -1000 /tmp/waos-backend.log | grep -c ERROR > $REPORT_DIR/error_count_$TIMESTAMP.txt

echo ""
echo "=========================================="
echo "  指标收集完成！"
echo "  报告位置: $REPORT_DIR/"
echo "=========================================="
```

---

## 📦 四、性能调优清单

### 🔴 高优先级调优项

| 问题 | 解决方案 | 配置 |
| :--- | :--- | :--- |
| **数据库连接池耗尽** | 增大连接池 | `DB_POOL_SIZE=30`, `DB_MAX_OVERFLOW=20` |
| **Redis 内存不足** | 限制最大内存 + LRU | `maxmemory 512mb`, `maxmemory-policy allkeys-lru` |
| **AI 调用超时** | 增加超时 + 异步化 | `asyncio.timeout(15)` |
| **Worker 并发不足** | 增加 Worker 副本 | `replicas: 4` |
| **日志过多** | 限制日志大小 | `max-size: "50m"`, `max-file: "3"` |

### 🟡 中优先级调优项

| 问题 | 解决方案 |
| :--- | :--- |
| **Qdrant 查询慢** | 增加索引，批量检索 |
| **WebSocket 连接数** | 增加 Nginx 连接数限制 |
| **静态文件缓存** | Nginx 缓存静态资源 |
| **Gunicorn Worker** | 使用 Uvicorn 多 Worker |

### 🟢 低优先级调优项

- Redis Stream 消费组优化
- PostgreSQL 查询索引优化
- ClickHouse 迁移（日志分析）

---

## 📦 五、一键性能测试脚本

### `scripts/performance_test.sh`
```bash
#!/bin/bash
# WAOS 完整性能测试流程

set -e

echo "=========================================="
echo "  WAOS 性能测试"
echo "=========================================="

# 1. 检查服务
echo ""
echo "[1/4] 检查服务状态..."
if ! curl -s -f http://localhost:8000/health/ping > /dev/null; then
    echo "❌ Backend 未运行，请先启动: ./scripts/test_e2e.sh"
    exit 1
fi
echo "✅ 服务正常"

# 2. 启动 Locust 压测（后台）
echo ""
echo "[2/4] 启动压测 (100 用户，持续 60 秒)..."
cd "$(dirname "$0")/.."

locust -f scripts/locustfile.py \
    --host=http://localhost:8000 \
    --headless \
    -u 100 \
    -r 10 \
    --run-time 60s \
    --csv=reports/benchmark_$(date +%Y%m%d_%H%M%S) \
    --html=reports/report_$(date +%Y%m%d_%H%M%S).html

# 3. 收集性能指标
echo ""
echo "[3/4] 收集性能指标..."
./scripts/collect_metrics.sh

# 4. 输出报告
echo ""
echo "[4/4] 生成报告摘要..."
echo ""
echo "=========================================="
echo "  测试报告摘要"
echo "=========================================="

# 从 CSV 提取关键指标
CSV_FILE=$(ls -t reports/benchmark_*.csv | head -1)
if [ -f "$CSV_FILE" ]; then
    echo ""
    echo "请求统计:"
    tail -5 "$CSV_FILE"
fi

echo ""
echo "完整报告: reports/report_*.html"
echo "=========================================="
```

# 🚀 S-5：多租户 SaaS 后台管理（本地可测试版）

## 📦 一、新增数据模型

#### `backend/app/models/tenant.py`
```python
from sqlalchemy import Column, String, Integer, DateTime, UUID, Boolean, Float, Text, Enum as SQLEnum
from sqlalchemy.dialects.postgresql import JSONB
from app.models.base import Base
import enum
import uuid

class TenantStatus(str, enum.Enum):
    ACTIVE = "active"
    SUSPENDED = "suspended"
    EXPIRED = "expired"
    TRIAL = "trial"

class SubscriptionPlan(str, enum.Enum):
    FREE = "free"
    STARTER = "starter"
    PROFESSIONAL = "professional"
    ENTERPRISE = "enterprise"

class Tenant(Base):
    __tablename__ = "tenants"
    
    id = Column(UUID, primary_key=True, default=uuid.uuid4)
    name = Column(String(200), nullable=False)
    subdomain = Column(String(100), unique=True, nullable=False)  # xxx.waos.com
    logo_url = Column(String(500))
    status = Column(SQLEnum(TenantStatus), default=TenantStatus.TRIAL)
    
    # 套餐信息
    plan = Column(SQLEnum(SubscriptionPlan), default=SubscriptionPlan.FREE)
    plan_expires_at = Column(DateTime)
    
    # 配额
    max_accounts = Column(Integer, default=1)
    max_messages = Column(Integer, default=1000)  # 月消息量
    max_users = Column(Integer, default=5)
    
    # 配置
    config = Column(JSONB, default={})  # 品牌配置、功能开关
    
    # 时间戳
    created_at = Column(DateTime)
    updated_at = Column(DateTime)

class TenantUser(Base):
    __tablename__ = "tenant_users"
    
    id = Column(UUID, primary_key=True, default=uuid.uuid4)
    tenant_id = Column(UUID, nullable=False)
    user_id = Column(UUID, nullable=False)
    role = Column(String(50), default="member")  # owner / admin / member / viewer
    joined_at = Column(DateTime)
    is_active = Column(Boolean, default=True)

class TenantUsage(Base):
    __tablename__ = "tenant_usage"
    
    id = Column(UUID, primary_key=True, default=uuid.uuid4)
    tenant_id = Column(UUID, nullable=False)
    date = Column(DateTime, nullable=False)
    
    # 用量统计
    messages_sent = Column(Integer, default=0)
    messages_received = Column(Integer, default=0)
    ai_calls = Column(Integer, default=0)
    leads_created = Column(Integer, default=0)
    deals_closed = Column(Integer, default=0)
    
    # 存储用量
    storage_bytes = Column(Integer, default=0)
    
    created_at = Column(DateTime)

class Subscription(Base):
    __tablename__ = "subscriptions"
    
    id = Column(UUID, primary_key=True, default=uuid.uuid4)
    tenant_id = Column(UUID, nullable=False)
    plan = Column(SQLEnum(SubscriptionPlan), nullable=False)
    start_date = Column(DateTime)
    end_date = Column(DateTime)
    amount = Column(Float)
    currency = Column(String(10), default="CNY")
    status = Column(String(20), default="active")  # active / expired / cancelled
    payment_id = Column(String(200))
    created_at = Column(DateTime)

class PaymentRecord(Base):
    __tablename__ = "payment_records"
    
    id = Column(UUID, primary_key=True, default=uuid.uuid4)
    tenant_id = Column(UUID, nullable=False)
    amount = Column(Float)
    currency = Column(String(10), default="CNY")
    method = Column(String(50))  # alipay / wechat / card
    status = Column(String(20), default="pending")  # pending / success / failed
    transaction_id = Column(String(200))
    invoice_url = Column(String(500))
    created_at = Column(DateTime)
    paid_at = Column(DateTime)
```

---

## 📦 二、租户服务核心

#### `backend/app/services/tenant_service.py`
```python
import uuid
import secrets
from datetime import datetime, timedelta
from typing import Optional, Dict, Any
from uuid import UUID

from sqlalchemy.orm import Session
from app.db.session import get_db_session
from app.models.tenant import Tenant, TenantStatus, SubscriptionPlan, TenantUser, TenantUsage
from app.models.user import User
from app.utils.logger import logger
from app.utils.redis_client import redis_client

class TenantService:
    """租户管理服务"""
    
    @staticmethod
    def create_tenant(
        name: str,
        subdomain: str,
        admin_email: str,
        admin_password: str,
        plan: str = "trial"
    ) -> dict:
        """创建租户（含管理员账号）"""
        with get_db_session() as db:
            # 1. 检查子域名是否已被占用
            existing = db.query(Tenant).filter(Tenant.subdomain == subdomain).first()
            if existing:
                raise ValueError(f"Subdomain '{subdomain}' already taken")
            
            # 2. 检查邮箱是否已被注册
            existing_user = db.query(User).filter(User.email == admin_email).first()
            if existing_user:
                raise ValueError(f"Email '{admin_email}' already registered")
            
            # 3. 创建租户
            plan_config = TenantService._get_plan_config(plan)
            tenant = Tenant(
                name=name,
                subdomain=subdomain,
                status=TenantStatus.TRIAL if plan == "trial" else TenantStatus.ACTIVE,
                plan=SubscriptionPlan(plan) if plan != "trial" else SubscriptionPlan.FREE,
                plan_expires_at=datetime.now() + timedelta(days=14) if plan == "trial" else None,
                max_accounts=plan_config["max_accounts"],
                max_messages=plan_config["max_messages"],
                max_users=plan_config["max_users"],
                config=plan_config["config"],
                created_at=datetime.now(),
                updated_at=datetime.now()
            )
            db.add(tenant)
            db.flush()
            
            # 4. 创建管理员用户
            user = User(
                username=admin_email,
                email=admin_email,
                password_hash=User.hash_password(admin_password),
                role="admin",
                tenant_id=tenant.id,
                created_at=datetime.now()
            )
            db.add(user)
            db.flush()
            
            # 5. 关联租户-用户
            tenant_user = TenantUser(
                tenant_id=tenant.id,
                user_id=user.id,
                role="owner",
                joined_at=datetime.now(),
                is_active=True
            )
            db.add(tenant_user)
            db.commit()
            db.refresh(tenant)
            
            logger.info(f"Tenant created: {tenant.id} ({subdomain}) with admin {admin_email}")
            
            return {
                "tenant_id": str(tenant.id),
                "subdomain": tenant.subdomain,
                "plan": tenant.plan.value,
                "admin_user_id": str(user.id)
            }
    
    @staticmethod
    def _get_plan_config(plan: str) -> dict:
        """获取套餐配置"""
        plans = {
            "trial": {
                "max_accounts": 1,
                "max_messages": 100,
                "max_users": 3,
                "config": {"features": ["basic_ai", "knowledge_base"]}
            },
            "free": {
                "max_accounts": 1,
                "max_messages": 1000,
                "max_users": 5,
                "config": {"features": ["basic_ai", "knowledge_base", "analytics"]}
            },
            "starter": {
                "max_accounts": 3,
                "max_messages": 5000,
                "max_users": 10,
                "config": {"features": ["basic_ai", "knowledge_base", "analytics", "campaign"]}
            },
            "professional": {
                "max_accounts": 10,
                "max_messages": 50000,
                "max_users": 25,
                "config": {"features": ["advanced_ai", "knowledge_base", "analytics", "campaign", "automation", "moments"]}
            },
            "enterprise": {
                "max_accounts": 50,
                "max_messages": 999999,
                "max_users": 100,
                "config": {"features": ["all"]}
            }
        }
        return plans.get(plan, plans["free"])
    
    @staticmethod
    def get_tenant_by_subdomain(subdomain: str) -> Optional[dict]:
        """按子域名获取租户"""
        with get_db_session() as db:
            tenant = db.query(Tenant).filter(Tenant.subdomain == subdomain).first()
            if not tenant:
                return None
            return {
                "id": str(tenant.id),
                "name": tenant.name,
                "subdomain": tenant.subdomain,
                "status": tenant.status.value,
                "plan": tenant.plan.value
            }
    
    @staticmethod
    def check_usage(tenant_id: UUID) -> dict:
        """检查租户用量"""
        with get_db_session() as db:
            # 获取本月用量
            now = datetime.now()
            start_of_month = now.replace(day=1, hour=0, minute=0, second=0)
            
            usage = db.query(TenantUsage).filter(
                TenantUsage.tenant_id == tenant_id,
                TenantUsage.date >= start_of_month
            ).first()
            
            tenant = db.query(Tenant).filter(Tenant.id == tenant_id).first()
            
            return {
                "used_messages": usage.messages_sent + usage.messages_received if usage else 0,
                "max_messages": tenant.max_messages if tenant else 0,
                "used_ai_calls": usage.ai_calls if usage else 0,
                "usage_percent": round(
                    ((usage.messages_sent + usage.messages_received) / tenant.max_messages * 100) 
                    if tenant and tenant.max_messages > 0 else 0, 1
                )
            }
    
    @staticmethod
    def record_usage(tenant_id: UUID, event_type: str, count: int = 1):
        """记录用量"""
        today = datetime.now().replace(hour=0, minute=0, second=0, microsecond=0)
        
        # 使用 Redis 缓存实时用量
        key = f"waos:usage:{tenant_id}:{today.isoformat()}"
        redis_client.hincrby(key, event_type, count)
        redis_client.expire(key, 86400 * 31)  # 保留31天
    
    @staticmethod
    def sync_usage_to_db():
        """定时将 Redis 用量同步到 PostgreSQL（由 Worker 执行）"""
        # 获取所有租户的用量 Key
        keys = redis_client.keys("waos:usage:*")
        for key in keys:
            if isinstance(key, bytes):
                key = key.decode()
            
            parts = key.split(":")
            if len(parts) >= 4:
                tenant_id = parts[2]
                date_str = parts[3]
                
                data = redis_client.hgetall(key)
                if not data:
                    continue
                
                # 转换为 dict
                usage_data = {}
                for k, v in data.items():
                    if isinstance(k, bytes):
                        k = k.decode()
                    if isinstance(v, bytes):
                        v = int(v.decode())
                    usage_data[k] = v
                
                with get_db_session() as db:
                    # 更新或创建用量记录
                    today = datetime.fromisoformat(date_str)
                    usage = db.query(TenantUsage).filter(
                        TenantUsage.tenant_id == tenant_id,
                        TenantUsage.date == today
                    ).first()
                    
                    if not usage:
                        usage = TenantUsage(
                            tenant_id=tenant_id,
                            date=today,
                            messages_sent=0,
                            messages_received=0,
                            ai_calls=0,
                            leads_created=0,
                            deals_closed=0
                        )
                        db.add(usage)
                    
                    usage.messages_sent += usage_data.get("message_sent", 0)
                    usage.messages_received += usage_data.get("message_received", 0)
                    usage.ai_calls += usage_data.get("ai_call", 0)
                    usage.leads_created += usage_data.get("lead_created", 0)
                    usage.deals_closed += usage_data.get("deal_closed", 0)
                    
                    db.commit()
                
                # 清理 Redis 缓存（已同步）
                redis_client.delete(key)
```

## 📦 三、租户注册 API

#### `backend/app/api/tenant.py`
```python
from fastapi import APIRouter, Depends, HTTPException
from pydantic import BaseModel, EmailStr
from typing import Optional
from uuid import UUID

from app.services.tenant_service import TenantService
from app.utils.logger import logger

router = APIRouter(prefix="/api/tenant", tags=["tenant"])

class RegisterRequest(BaseModel):
    company_name: str
    subdomain: str
    admin_email: EmailStr
    admin_password: str
    plan: Optional[str] = "trial"

class RegisterResponse(BaseModel):
    tenant_id: str
    subdomain: str
    plan: str
    admin_user_id: str
    message: str

@router.post("/register")
async def register_tenant(req: RegisterRequest):
    """
    租户自助注册
    """
    try:
        result = TenantService.create_tenant(
            name=req.company_name,
            subdomain=req.subdomain,
            admin_email=req.admin_email,
            admin_password=req.admin_password,
            plan=req.plan
        )
        return RegisterResponse(
            tenant_id=result["tenant_id"],
            subdomain=result["subdomain"],
            plan=result["plan"],
            admin_user_id=result["admin_user_id"],
            message="租户创建成功！请前往登录"
        )
    except ValueError as e:
        raise HTTPException(status_code=400, detail=str(e))
    except Exception as e:
        logger.error(f"Register tenant failed: {e}")
        raise HTTPException(status_code=500, detail="注册失败，请稍后重试")

@router.get("/check-subdomain")
async def check_subdomain(subdomain: str):
    """
    检查子域名是否可用
    """
    existing = TenantService.get_tenant_by_subdomain(subdomain)
    return {
        "available": existing is None,
        "subdomain": subdomain
    }

@router.get("/{tenant_id}/usage")
async def get_usage(
    tenant_id: UUID,
    # TODO: 添加鉴权
):
    """
    获取租户用量
    """
    try:
        return TenantService.check_usage(tenant_id)
    except Exception as e:
        raise HTTPException(status_code=500, detail=str(e))
```

## 📦 四、多租户中间件（自动识别租户）

#### `backend/app/middleware/tenant.py`
```python
from fastapi import Request
from starlette.middleware.base import BaseHTTPMiddleware
from app.services.tenant_service import TenantService
from app.core.context import set_tenant_id
from app.utils.logger import logger

class TenantMiddleware(BaseHTTPMiddleware):
    """
    多租户中间件
    从子域名或请求头中提取租户
    """
    
    async def dispatch(self, request: Request, call_next):
        # 1. 从 Host 头提取子域名
        host = request.headers.get("host", "")
        subdomain = host.split(".")[0] if "." in host else None
        
        # 2. 允许通过 X-Tenant-ID 头指定（方便开发调试）
        tenant_id_header = request.headers.get("X-Tenant-ID")
        
        if tenant_id_header:
            set_tenant_id(tenant_id_header)
        elif subdomain and subdomain != "www" and subdomain != "localhost":
            # 从子域名查询租户
            tenant = TenantService.get_tenant_by_subdomain(subdomain)
            if tenant:
                set_tenant_id(tenant["id"])
                logger.debug(f"Tenant identified: {subdomain} -> {tenant['id']}")
        
        response = await call_next(request)
        return response
```

## 📦 五、SaaS 管理后台 API

#### `backend/app/api/admin.py`
```python
from fastapi import APIRouter, Depends, HTTPException
from pydantic import BaseModel
from typing import List, Optional
from datetime import datetime, timedelta
from uuid import UUID

from app.db.session import get_db_session
from app.models.tenant import Tenant, TenantStatus, SubscriptionPlan, TenantUsage
from app.core.context import require_tenant_id
from app.utils.logger import logger

router = APIRouter(prefix="/api/admin", tags=["admin"])

class TenantListResponse(BaseModel):
    id: str
    name: str
    subdomain: str
    status: str
    plan: str
    created_at: datetime
    users_count: int

@router.get("/tenants")
async def list_tenants(
    page: int = 1,
    page_size: int = 20,
    status: Optional[str] = None
):
    """
    租户列表（平台管理员）
    """
    with get_db_session() as db:
        query = db.query(Tenant)
        if status:
            query = query.filter(Tenant.status == status)
        
        total = query.count()
        tenants = query.order_by(Tenant.created_at.desc()).offset((page-1)*page_size).limit(page_size).all()
        
        return {
            "items": [
                {
                    "id": str(t.id),
                    "name": t.name,
                    "subdomain": t.subdomain,
                    "status": t.status.value,
                    "plan": t.plan.value,
                    "created_at": t.created_at,
                    "users_count": 0  # TODO: 查询实际用户数
                }
                for t in tenants
            ],
            "total": total,
            "page": page,
            "page_size": page_size
        }

@router.put("/tenants/{tenant_id}/suspend")
async def suspend_tenant(tenant_id: UUID):
    """
    暂停租户
    """
    with get_db_session() as db:
        tenant = db.query(Tenant).filter(Tenant.id == tenant_id).first()
        if not tenant:
            raise HTTPException(404, "Tenant not found")
        
        tenant.status = TenantStatus.SUSPENDED
        tenant.updated_at = datetime.now()
        db.commit()
        
        logger.info(f"Tenant {tenant_id} suspended")
        return {"status": "suspended"}

@router.put("/tenants/{tenant_id}/activate")
async def activate_tenant(tenant_id: UUID):
    """
    激活租户
    """
    with get_db_session() as db:
        tenant = db.query(Tenant).filter(Tenant.id == tenant_id).first()
        if not tenant:
            raise HTTPException(404, "Tenant not found")
        
        tenant.status = TenantStatus.ACTIVE
        tenant.updated_at = datetime.now()
        db.commit()
        
        logger.info(f"Tenant {tenant_id} activated")
        return {"status": "active"}

@router.get("/stats")
async def get_platform_stats():
    """
    平台统计（平台管理员）
    """
    with get_db_session() as db:
        total_tenants = db.query(Tenant).count()
        active_tenants = db.query(Tenant).filter(Tenant.status == TenantStatus.ACTIVE).count()
        total_usage = db.query(TenantUsage).filter(
            TenantUsage.date >= datetime.now().replace(day=1)
        ).all()
        
        total_messages = sum(u.messages_sent + u.messages_received for u in total_usage)
        total_ai_calls = sum(u.ai_calls for u in total_usage)
        
        return {
            "total_tenants": total_tenants,
            "active_tenants": active_tenants,
            "total_messages_this_month": total_messages,
            "total_ai_calls_this_month": total_ai_calls,
            "monthly_revenue": 0  # TODO: 实际计费
        }
```

## 📦 六、前端：租户注册页面

#### `frontend/src/pages/Register.tsx`
```tsx
import { useState } from 'react'
import { useNavigate } from 'react-router-dom'
import { api } from '../api/client'

export function Register() {
  const navigate = useNavigate()
  const [loading, setLoading] = useState(false)
  const [form, setForm] = useState({
    company_name: '',
    subdomain: '',
    admin_email: '',
    admin_password: '',
    plan: 'trial'
  })

  const handleSubmit = async (e: React.FormEvent) => {
    e.preventDefault()
    setLoading(true)

    try {
      const response = await api.post('/tenant/register', form)
      if (response.data.code === 0) {
        alert('注册成功！请前往登录')
        navigate('/login')
      } else {
        alert(response.data.msg || '注册失败')
      }
    } catch (err: any) {
      alert(err.response?.data?.detail || '注册失败，请重试')
    } finally {
      setLoading(false)
    }
  }

  return (
    <div className="min-h-screen flex items-center justify-center bg-waos-bg">
      <div className="w-full max-w-md p-8 glass rounded-xl">
        <div className="text-center mb-8">
          <h1 className="text-2xl font-bold text-white">WAOS 注册</h1>
          <p className="text-white/40 text-sm mt-1">开启你的 AI 销售之旅</p>
        </div>

        <form onSubmit={handleSubmit} className="space-y-4">
          <div>
            <label className="block text-sm text-white/60 mb-1">企业名称</label>
            <input
              type="text"
              value={form.company_name}
              onChange={(e) => setForm({ ...form, company_name: e.target.value })}
              className="w-full px-4 py-2 rounded-lg bg-white/5 border border-white/10 text-white focus:border-waos-primary focus:outline-none"
              placeholder="输入企业名称"
              required
            />
          </div>

          <div>
            <label className="block text-sm text-white/60 mb-1">子域名</label>
            <div className="flex items-center gap-2">
              <input
                type="text"
                value={form.subdomain}
                onChange={(e) => setForm({ ...form, subdomain: e.target.value })}
                className="flex-1 px-4 py-2 rounded-lg bg-white/5 border border-white/10 text-white focus:border-waos-primary focus:outline-none"
                placeholder="your-company"
                required
              />
              <span className="text-white/40 text-sm whitespace-nowrap">.waos.com</span>
            </div>
          </div>

          <div>
            <label className="block text-sm text-white/60 mb-1">管理员邮箱</label>
            <input
              type="email"
              value={form.admin_email}
              onChange={(e) => setForm({ ...form, admin_email: e.target.value })}
              className="w-full px-4 py-2 rounded-lg bg-white/5 border border-white/10 text-white focus:border-waos-primary focus:outline-none"
              placeholder="admin@company.com"
              required
            />
          </div>

          <div>
            <label className="block text-sm text-white/60 mb-1">密码</label>
            <input
              type="password"
              value={form.admin_password}
              onChange={(e) => setForm({ ...form, admin_password: e.target.value })}
              className="w-full px-4 py-2 rounded-lg bg-white/5 border border-white/10 text-white focus:border-waos-primary focus:outline-none"
              placeholder="至少6位"
              minLength={6}
              required
            />
          </div>

          <div>
            <label className="block text-sm text-white/60 mb-1">套餐</label>
            <select
              value={form.plan}
              onChange={(e) => setForm({ ...form, plan: e.target.value })}
              className="w-full px-4 py-2 rounded-lg bg-white/5 border border-white/10 text-white focus:border-waos-primary focus:outline-none"
            >
              <option value="trial">免费试用（14天）</option>
              <option value="free">免费版</option>
              <option value="starter">初创版 ¥999/月</option>
              <option value="professional">专业版 ¥4999/月</option>
            </select>
          </div>

          <button
            type="submit"
            disabled={loading}
            className="w-full py-2.5 rounded-lg bg-waos-primary text-black font-medium hover:opacity-80 transition disabled:opacity-50"
          >
            {loading ? '注册中...' : '立即注册'}
          </button>
        </form>

        <div className="text-center mt-6">
          <span className="text-white/30 text-sm">已有账号？</span>
          <a href="/login" className="text-waos-primary text-sm ml-1 hover:underline">去登录</a>
        </div>
      </div>
    </div>
  )
}
```

## 🖥️ 三、SaaS 控制台仪表板（租户登录后首页）

```tsx
import { useEffect, useState } from 'react'
import { useNavigate } from 'react-router-dom'
import { useTenantStore } from '../store/tenantStore'
import { AnalyticsAPI } from '../api/client'

export function Dashboard() {
  const navigate = useNavigate()
  const { tenant, usage, fetchTenantInfo, fetchUsage } = useTenantStore()
  const [analytics, setAnalytics] = useState<any>(null)
  const [loading, setLoading] = useState(true)

  useEffect(() => {
    const loadData = async () => {
      await fetchTenantInfo()
      await fetchUsage()
      
      try {
        const data = await AnalyticsAPI.dashboard()

        console.error('Failed to load analytics', e)
      }
      setLoading(false)
    }
    loadData()
  }, [])

  if (loading) {
    return (
      <div className="flex items-center justify-center h-full text-white/40">
        加载中...
      </div>
    )

  return (

            />
          </div>

          <div className="text-2xl font-bold text-white">{usage?.used_ai_calls || 0}</div>
          <div className="text-xs text-white/30">本月</div>
        </div>

        <div className="glass p-4 rounded-xl">
          <div className="text-white/40 text-xs">活跃客户</div>
          <div className="text-2xl font-bold text-white">{analytics?.hot_customers || 0}</div>
          <div className="text-xs text-white/30">高意向客户</div>
        </div>

        <div className="glass p-4 rounded-xl">
          <div className="text-white/40 text-xs">今日成交</div>

      </div>

      {/* 快捷操作 */}
      <div className="glass p-4 rounded-xl">
        <div className="text-sm font-medium text-white/80 mb-3">快捷操作</div>
        <div className="flex gap-3 flex-wrap">
          <button
            onClick={() => navigate('/messages')}

          >
            💬 消息中心

            onClick={() => navigate('/accounts')}
            className="px-4 py-2 bg-white/10 text-white/80 rounded-lg text-sm hover:bg-white/20 transition"

            📱 管理账号

            📢 批量运营
          </button>

      {/* 套餐信息 */}
      <div className="glass p-4 rounded-xl border border-waos-primary/20">

          <div>

            <div className="text-lg font-bold text-waos-primary">
              {tenant?.plan === 'trial' ? '免费试用' : 
               tenant?.plan === 'starter' ? '初创版' :
               tenant?.plan === 'professional' ? '专业版' :
               tenant?.plan === 'enterprise' ? '旗舰版' : '免费版'}
```

## 📦 八、租户状态管理（Zustand Store）

#### `frontend/src/store/tenantStore.ts`
```ts
import { create } from 'zustand'
import { api } from '../api/client'

interface TenantState {
  tenant: {
    id: string
    name: string
    subdomain: string
    plan: string
    status: string
  } | null
  usage: {
    used_messages: number
    max_messages: number
    used_ai_calls: number
    usage_percent: number
  } | null
  loading: boolean
  fetchTenantInfo: () => Promise<void>
  fetchUsage: () => Promise<void>
}

export const useTenantStore = create<TenantState>((set, get) => ({
  tenant: null,
  usage: null,
  loading: false,

  fetchTenantInfo: async () => {
    set({ loading: true })
    try {
      const response = await api.get('/tenant/info')
      set({ tenant: response.data, loading: false })
    } catch {
      set({ loading: false })
    }
  },

  fetchUsage: async () => {
    try {
      const response = await api.get('/tenant/usage')
      set({ usage: response.data })
    } catch {
      // error
    }
  }
}))
```

## 📦 九、租户信息 API

#### `backend/app/api/tenant.py`（追加）
```python
@router.get("/info")
async def get_tenant_info(
    tenant_id: UUID = Depends(get_current_tenant)
):
    """
    获取当前租户信息
    """
    with get_db_session() as db:
        tenant = db.query(Tenant).filter(Tenant.id == tenant_id).first()
        if not tenant:
            raise HTTPException(404, "Tenant not found")
        
        return {
            "id": str(tenant.id),
            "name": tenant.name,
            "subdomain": tenant.subdomain,
            "plan": tenant.plan.value,
            "status": tenant.status.value,
            "max_accounts": tenant.max_accounts,
            "max_messages": tenant.max_messages,
            "max_users": tenant.max_users,
            "created_at": tenant.created_at
        }

@router.get("/usage")
async def get_usage(
    tenant_id: UUID = Depends(get_current_tenant)
):
    """
    获取当前租户用量
    """
    return TenantService.check_usage(tenant_id)
```

## 📦 十、租户登录页面

#### `frontend/src/pages/Login.tsx`
```tsx
import { useState } from 'react'
import { useNavigate } from 'react-router-dom'
import { api } from '../api/client'

export function Login() {
  const navigate = useNavigate()
  const [loading, setLoading] = useState(false)
  const [form, setForm] = useState({
    email: '',
    password: ''
  })

  const handleSubmit = async (e: React.FormEvent) => {
    e.preventDefault()
    setLoading(true)

    try {
      const response = await api.post('/auth/login', {
        username: form.email,
        password: form.password
      })
      
      if (response.data.access_token) {
        localStorage.setItem('access_token', response.data.access_token)
        localStorage.setItem('tenant_id', response.data.tenant_id)
        navigate('/dashboard')
      }
    } catch (err: any) {
      alert(err.response?.data?.detail || '登录失败')
    } finally {
      setLoading(false)
    }
  }

  return (
    <div className="min-h-screen flex items-center justify-center bg-waos-bg">
      <div className="w-full max-w-md p-8 glass rounded-xl">
        <div className="text-center mb-8">
          <h1 className="text-2xl font-bold text-white">WAOS 登录</h1>
          <p className="text-white/40 text-sm mt-1">登录你的企业控制台</p>
        </div>

        <form onSubmit={handleSubmit} className="space-y-4">
          <div>
            <label className="block text-sm text-white/60 mb-1">邮箱</label>
            <input
              type="email"
              value={form.email}
              onChange={(e) => setForm({ ...form, email: e.target.value })}
              className="w-full px-4 py-2 rounded-lg bg-white/5 border border-white/10 text-white focus:border-waos-primary focus:outline-none"
              placeholder="admin@company.com"
              required
            />
          </div>

          <div>
            <label className="block text-sm text-white/60 mb-1">密码</label>
            <input
              type="password"
              value={form.password}
              onChange={(e) => setForm({ ...form, password: e.target.value })}
              className="w-full px-4 py-2 rounded-lg bg-white/5 border border-white/10 text-white focus:border-waos-primary focus:outline-none"
              placeholder="输入密码"
              required
            />
          </div>

          <button
            type="submit"
            disabled={loading}
            className="w-full py-2.5 rounded-lg bg-waos-primary text-black font-medium hover:opacity-80 transition disabled:opacity-50"
          >
            {loading ? '登录中...' : '登录'}
          </button>
        </form>

        <div className="text-center mt-6">
          <span className="text-white/30 text-sm">还没有账号？</span>
          <a href="/register" className="text-waos-primary text-sm ml-1 hover:underline">立即注册</a>
        </div>
      </div>
    </div>
  )
}
```

## 📦 十一、更新路由

#### `frontend/src/App.tsx`
```tsx
import { BrowserRouter, Routes, Route, Navigate } from 'react-router-dom'
import { QueryClient, QueryClientProvider } from '@tanstack/react-query'
import { MainLayout } from './layout/MainLayout'
import { Register } from './pages/Register'
import { Login } from './pages/Login'
import { Dashboard } from './pages/Dashboard'

const queryClient = new QueryClient()

function App() {
  const isLoggedIn = !!localStorage.getItem('access_token')

  return (
    <QueryClientProvider client={queryClient}>
      <BrowserRouter>
        <Routes>
          <Route path="/register" element={<Register />} />
          <Route path="/login" element={<Login />} />
          <Route
            path="/dashboard"
            element={isLoggedIn ? <Dashboard /> : <Navigate to="/login" />}
          />
          <Route
            path="/*"
            element={
              isLoggedIn ? (
                <MainLayout />
              ) : (
                <Navigate to="/login" />
              )
            }
          />
        </Routes>
      </BrowserRouter>
    </QueryClientProvider>
  )
}

export default App
```

## 🚀 S-5 扩展：套餐升级 + 支付模拟

### 一、新增 API

#### `backend/app/api/tenant.py`（追加）

```python
from pydantic import BaseModel
from typing import Optional
from datetime import datetime, timedelta
from uuid import UUID

from app.models.tenant import SubscriptionPlan, Subscription, PaymentRecord

class UpgradeRequest(BaseModel):
    plan: str  # starter / professional / enterprise
    payment_method: str = "mock"  # mock / alipay / wechat

class PaymentResponse(BaseModel):
    payment_id: str
    amount: float
    plan: str
    status: str
    redirect_url: Optional[str] = None

@router.post("/upgrade")
async def upgrade_plan(
    req: UpgradeRequest,
    tenant_id: UUID = Depends(get_current_tenant)
):
    """
    升级套餐（含支付模拟）
    """
    # 套餐价格表
    PRICES = {
        "starter": 999,
        "professional": 4999,
        "enterprise": 19999
    }
    
    if req.plan not in PRICES:
        raise HTTPException(400, f"Invalid plan: {req.plan}")
    
    amount = PRICES[req.plan]
    
    with get_db_session() as db:
        # 1. 获取租户
        tenant = db.query(Tenant).filter(Tenant.id == tenant_id).first()
        if not tenant:
            raise HTTPException(404, "Tenant not found")
        
        # 2. 创建支付记录
        payment = PaymentRecord(
            tenant_id=tenant_id,
            amount=amount,
            currency="CNY",
            method=req.payment_method,
            status="pending",
            created_at=datetime.now()
        )
        db.add(payment)
        db.flush()
        
        # 3. 如果是模拟支付（mock），自动完成
        if req.payment_method == "mock":
            payment.status = "success"
            payment.paid_at = datetime.now()
            payment.transaction_id = f"mock_{uuid.uuid4().hex[:16]}"
            payment.invoice_url = f"/invoices/mock_{uuid.uuid4().hex[:8]}.pdf"
            
            # 创建订阅记录
            subscription = Subscription(
                tenant_id=tenant_id,
                plan=SubscriptionPlan(req.plan),
                start_date=datetime.now(),
                end_date=datetime.now() + timedelta(days=365),  # 1年
                amount=amount,
                currency="CNY",
                status="active",
                payment_id=str(payment.id),
                created_at=datetime.now()
            )
            db.add(subscription)
            
            # 更新租户套餐
            old_plan = tenant.plan.value
            tenant.plan = SubscriptionPlan(req.plan)
            tenant.plan_expires_at = datetime.now() + timedelta(days=365)
            tenant.status = TenantStatus.ACTIVE
            
            # 更新配额
            plan_config = TenantService._get_plan_config(req.plan)
            tenant.max_accounts = plan_config["max_accounts"]
            tenant.max_messages = plan_config["max_messages"]
            tenant.max_users = plan_config["max_users"]
            
            db.commit()
            db.refresh(payment)
            
            return {
                "status": "success",
                "payment_id": str(payment.id),
                "plan": req.plan,
                "amount": amount,
                "message": f"成功升级到 {req.plan} 套餐"
            }
        
        # 4. 真实支付模式：返回支付链接（模拟）
        db.commit()
        return {
            "status": "pending",
            "payment_id": str(payment.id),
            "plan": req.plan,
            "amount": amount,
            "redirect_url": f"/payment/{payment.id}",
            "message": "请完成支付"
        }

@router.get("/payment/{payment_id}/status")
async def get_payment_status(
    payment_id: UUID,
    tenant_id: UUID = Depends(get_current_tenant)
):
    """查询支付状态"""
    with get_db_session() as db:
        payment = db.query(PaymentRecord).filter(
            PaymentRecord.id == payment_id,
            PaymentRecord.tenant_id == tenant_id
        ).first()
        
        if not payment:
            raise HTTPException(404, "Payment not found")
        
        return {
            "payment_id": str(payment.id),
            "status": payment.status,
            "amount": payment.amount,
            "paid_at": payment.paid_at,
            "invoice_url": payment.invoice_url
        }

@router.get("/invoices")
async def get_invoices(
    tenant_id: UUID = Depends(get_current_tenant)
):
    """获取发票列表"""
    with get_db_session() as db:
        payments = db.query(PaymentRecord).filter(
            PaymentRecord.tenant_id == tenant_id,
            PaymentRecord.status == "success"
        ).order_by(PaymentRecord.paid_at.desc()).all()
        
        return [{
            "payment_id": str(p.id),
            "amount": p.amount,
            "date": p.paid_at,
            "invoice_url": p.invoice_url
        } for p in payments]

@router.get("/subscription")
async def get_subscription(
    tenant_id: UUID = Depends(get_current_tenant)
):
    """获取当前订阅信息"""
    with get_db_session() as db:
        subscription = db.query(Subscription).filter(
            Subscription.tenant_id == tenant_id,
            Subscription.status == "active"
        ).order_by(Subscription.created_at.desc()).first()
        
        if not subscription:
            return {"status": "no_active_subscription"}
        
        return {
            "plan": subscription.plan.value,
            "start_date": subscription.start_date,
            "end_date": subscription.end_date,
            "amount": subscription.amount,
            "status": subscription.status,
            "days_remaining": max(0, (subscription.end_date - datetime.now()).days)
        }
```

### 二、前端套餐升级页面

#### `frontend/src/pages/Pricing.tsx`

```tsx
import { useState } from 'react'
import { useNavigate } from 'react-router-dom'
import { api } from '../api/client'

const PLANS = [
  {
    id: 'free',
    name: '免费版',
    price: '0',
    period: '永久',
    features: ['1个微信账号', '100条消息/月', '基础AI', '知识库'],
    buttonText: '当前套餐',
    recommended: false
  },
  {
    id: 'starter',
    name: '初创版',
    price: '999',
    period: '/月',
    features: ['3个微信账号', '5000条消息/月', 'AI+知识库', '数据分析', '批量运营'],
    buttonText: '升级',
    recommended: true
  },
  {
    id: 'professional',
    name: '专业版',
    price: '4,999',
    period: '/月',
    features: ['10个微信账号', '50000条消息/月', '高级AI', '自动化运营', '朋友圈管理', '专属客服'],
    buttonText: '升级',
    recommended: false
  },
  {
    id: 'enterprise',
    name: '旗舰版',
    price: '19,999',
    period: '/月',
    features: ['50个微信账号', '无限消息', '专属AI训练', '定制开发', '专属支持', 'SLA保障'],
    buttonText: '联系我们',
    recommended: false
  }
]

export function Pricing() {
  const navigate = useNavigate()
  const [loading, setLoading] = useState<string | null>(null)
  const [tenant, setTenant] = useState<any>(null)

  // 获取当前套餐
  useState(() => {
    api.get('/tenant/info').then(res => setTenant(res.data))
  }, [])

  const handleUpgrade = async (planId: string) => {
    if (planId === 'free') return
    if (planId === 'enterprise') {
      alert('请联系销售团队: sales@waos.com')
      return
    }

    setLoading(planId)
    try {
      const response = await api.post('/tenant/upgrade', {
        plan: planId,
        payment_method: 'mock'  // 模拟支付
      })

      if (response.data.status === 'success') {
        alert(`✅ 升级成功！已切换到 ${planId} 套餐`)
        navigate('/dashboard')
      } else {
        alert('升级请求已提交，请完成支付')
      }
    } catch (err: any) {
      alert(err.response?.data?.detail || '升级失败')
    } finally {
      setLoading(null)
    }
  }

  return (
    <div className="min-h-screen bg-waos-bg py-12">
      <div className="max-w-6xl mx-auto px-4">
        {/* 标题 */}
        <div className="text-center mb-12">
          <h1 className="text-3xl font-bold text-white">选择适合你的套餐</h1>
          <p className="text-white/40 mt-2">按需付费，随时升级</p>
          {tenant && (
            <div className="text-sm text-white/30 mt-2">
              当前套餐: <span className="text-waos-primary">{tenant.plan}</span>
            </div>
          )}
        </div>

        {/* 套餐卡片 */}
        <div className="grid grid-cols-1 md:grid-cols-4 gap-6">
          {PLANS.map((plan) => {
            const isCurrent = tenant?.plan === plan.id
            const isDisabled = plan.id === 'free' || plan.id === 'enterprise'
            
            return (
              <div
                key={plan.id}
                className={`glass rounded-xl p-6 transition-all duration-300 ${
                  plan.recommended
                    ? 'border-2 border-waos-primary shadow-xl shadow-waos-primary/10'
                    : 'border border-white/10'
                }`}
              >
                {plan.recommended && (
                  <div className="text-xs font-medium text-waos-primary bg-waos-primary/20 px-2 py-0.5 rounded-full inline-block mb-3">
                    推荐
                  </div>
                )}
                <h3 className="text-lg font-semibold text-white">{plan.name}</h3>
                <div className="mt-2 flex items-baseline gap-1">
                  <span className="text-3xl font-bold text-white">¥{plan.price}</span>
                  <span className="text-white/40 text-sm">{plan.period}</span>
                </div>

                <ul className="mt-4 space-y-2">
                  {plan.features.map((feature, idx) => (
                    <li key={idx} className="text-sm text-white/60 flex items-start gap-2">
                      <span className="text-waos-primary mt-0.5">✓</span>
                      {feature}
                    </li>
                  ))}
                </ul>

                <button
                  onClick={() => handleUpgrade(plan.id)}
                  disabled={isCurrent || loading === plan.id || isDisabled}
                  className={`w-full mt-6 py-2.5 rounded-lg text-sm font-medium transition ${
                    isCurrent
                      ? 'bg-white/10 text-white/40 cursor-not-allowed'
                      : plan.recommended
                      ? 'bg-waos-primary text-black hover:opacity-80'
                      : 'bg-white/10 text-white hover:bg-white/20'
                  } ${(loading === plan.id) ? 'opacity-50 cursor-wait' : ''}`}
                >
                  {loading === plan.id ? '处理中...' : isCurrent ? '当前套餐' : plan.buttonText}
                </button>
              </div>
            )
          })}
        </div>

        {/* 发票历史 */}
        <div className="mt-12 glass rounded-xl p-6">
          <h3 className="text-sm font-medium text-white/80 mb-3">发票历史</h3>
          <div className="text-white/30 text-sm">暂无支付记录</div>
        </div>
      </div>
    </div>
  )
}
```

### 四、数据库迁移

```sql
-- 订阅表（如果还未创建）
CREATE TABLE subscriptions (
    id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT gen_random_uuid(),
    tenant_id UUID NOT NULL,
    plan VARCHAR(50) NOT NULL,
    start_date TIMESTAMP,
    end_date TIMESTAMP,
    amount FLOAT,
    currency VARCHAR(10) DEFAULT 'CNY',
    status VARCHAR(20) DEFAULT 'active',
    payment_id VARCHAR(200),
    created_at TIMESTAMP DEFAULT NOW()
);

-- 支付记录表
CREATE TABLE payment_records (
    id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT gen_random_uuid(),
    tenant_id UUID NOT NULL,
    amount FLOAT,
    currency VARCHAR(10) DEFAULT 'CNY',
    method VARCHAR(50),
    status VARCHAR(20) DEFAULT 'pending',
    transaction_id VARCHAR(200),
    invoice_url VARCHAR(500),
    created_at TIMESTAMP DEFAULT NOW(),
    paid_at TIMESTAMP
);
```

# 🚨 WAOS P0 致命缺陷修复包

---

## 📦 修复 1：数据库自动备份（pg_dump → 阿里云 OSS）

### `scripts/backup.sh`
```bash
#!/bin/bash
# 数据库自动备份脚本
# 每天凌晨 3:00 执行，备份到阿里云 OSS

set -e

TIMESTAMP=$(date +%Y%m%d_%H%M%S)
BACKUP_FILE="/tmp/waos_backup_${TIMESTAMP}.sql.gz"

# 1. 导出数据库
echo "[$(date)] Starting backup..."
docker exec waos-postgres pg_dump -U waos waos | gzip > $BACKUP_FILE

# 2. 上传到阿里云 OSS（需配置 ossutil）
# 安装：wget https://gosspublic.alicdn.com/ossutil/1.7.13/ossutil64
# 配置：ossutil64 config
ossutil64 cp $BACKUP_FILE oss://waos-backups/$(date +%Y%m%d)/

# 3. 删除7天前的旧备份（本地）
find /tmp -name "waos_backup_*.sql.gz" -mtime +7 -delete

# 4. 删除30天前的OSS旧备份（远程）
ossutil64 rm oss://waos-backups/$(date -d "30 days ago" +%Y%m%d)/ -r -f

echo "[$(date)] Backup completed: $BACKUP_FILE"
```

### `scripts/restore.sh`
```bash
#!/bin/bash
# 从备份恢复数据库
BACKUP_FILE=$1

if [ -z "$BACKUP_FILE" ]; then
    echo "Usage: ./restore.sh <backup_file.sql.gz>"
    exit 1
fi

gunzip -c $BACKUP_FILE | docker exec -i waos-postgres psql -U waos waos
echo "Restore completed"
```

### 配置定时任务（cron）
```bash
# 每天凌晨 3:00 执行备份
0 3 * * * /opt/waos/scripts/backup.sh >> /var/log/waos-backup.log 2>&1
```

---

## 📦 修复 2：真实支付对接（支付宝当面付/电脑支付）

### `backend/app/services/payment_service.py`
```python
import hashlib
import time
import random
import json
from datetime import datetime
from typing import Optional, Dict
from uuid import UUID

from app.db.session import get_db_session
from app.models.tenant import PaymentRecord, Subscription, SubscriptionPlan, Tenant, TenantStatus
from app.utils.logger import logger
from app.utils.redis_client import redis_client

class PaymentService:
    """支付服务（支持支付宝/微信/模拟）"""
    
    # 套餐价格
    PRICES = {
        "starter": 999,
        "professional": 4999,
        "enterprise": 19999
    }
    
    @staticmethod
    def create_order(tenant_id: UUID, plan: str, payment_method: str = "mock") -> dict:
        """
        创建支付订单
        """
        if plan not in PaymentService.PRICES:
            raise ValueError(f"Invalid plan: {plan}")
        
        amount = PaymentService.PRICES[plan]
        order_id = f"WAOS_{tenant_id.hex[:8]}_{int(time.time())}_{random.randint(1000,9999)}"
        
        # 保存到数据库
        with get_db_session() as db:
            payment = PaymentRecord(
                tenant_id=tenant_id,
                amount=amount,
                currency="CNY",
                method=payment_method,
                status="pending",
                transaction_id=order_id,
                created_at=datetime.now()
            )
            db.add(payment)
            db.flush()
            
            # 如果是模拟支付，立即完成
            if payment_method == "mock":
                PaymentService._complete_payment(payment.id, db)
                db.commit()
                return {
                    "payment_id": str(payment.id),
                    "order_id": order_id,
                    "amount": amount,
                    "plan": plan,
                    "status": "success",
                    "message": "模拟支付成功"
                }
            
            # 真实支付宝支付
            if payment_method == "alipay":
                # 调用支付宝支付接口
                pay_url = PaymentService._create_alipay_order(order_id, amount, plan)
                db.commit()
                return {
                    "payment_id": str(payment.id),
                    "order_id": order_id,
                    "amount": amount,
                    "plan": plan,
                    "status": "pending",
                    "pay_url": pay_url,
                    "message": "请前往支付宝完成支付"
                }
            
            db.commit()
            return {
                "payment_id": str(payment.id),
                "order_id": order_id,
                "amount": amount,
                "plan": plan,
                "status": "pending",
                "message": "订单已创建"
            }
    
    @staticmethod
    def _complete_payment(payment_id: UUID, db):
        """完成支付（升级套餐）"""
        payment = db.query(PaymentRecord).filter(PaymentRecord.id == payment_id).first()
        if not payment:
            return
        
        payment.status = "success"
        payment.paid_at = datetime.now()
        
        # 获取租户
        tenant = db.query(Tenant).filter(Tenant.id == payment.tenant_id).first()
        if not tenant:
            return
        
        # 确定套餐
        plan_name = None
        for name, price in PaymentService.PRICES.items():
            if price == payment.amount:
                plan_name = name
                break
        
        if not plan_name:
            return
        
        # 创建订阅记录
        subscription = Subscription(
            tenant_id=tenant.id,
            plan=SubscriptionPlan(plan_name),
            start_date=datetime.now(),
            end_date=datetime.now() + datetime.timedelta(days=365),
            amount=payment.amount,
            currency=payment.currency,
            status="active",
            payment_id=str(payment.id),
            created_at=datetime.now()
        )
        db.add(subscription)
        
        # 更新租户
        tenant.plan = SubscriptionPlan(plan_name)
        tenant.plan_expires_at = datetime.now() + datetime.timedelta(days=365)
        tenant.status = TenantStatus.ACTIVE
        
        # 更新配额
        from app.services.tenant_service import TenantService
        plan_config = TenantService._get_plan_config(plan_name)
        tenant.max_accounts = plan_config["max_accounts"]
        tenant.max_messages = plan_config["max_messages"]
        tenant.max_users = plan_config["max_users"]
        
        logger.info(f"Payment completed: tenant {tenant.id} upgraded to {plan_name}")
    
    @staticmethod
    def _create_alipay_order(order_id: str, amount: float, plan: str) -> str:
        """创建支付宝订单（返回支付链接）"""
        # TODO: 真实对接支付宝 SDK
        # from alipay import AliPay
        # alipay = AliPay(appid="...", app_private_key_string="...", alipay_public_key_string="...")
        # result = alipay.api_alipay_trade_page_pay(
        #     out_trade_no=order_id,
        #     total_amount=str(amount),
        #     subject=f"WAOS {plan} 套餐",
        #     return_url="https://your-domain.com/payment/return",
        #     notify_url="https://your-domain.com/api/payment/alipay/notify"
        # )
        # return result.get("pay_url")
        
        # 模拟支付宝支付链接（开发测试用）
        mock_url = f"https://openapi.alipay.com/gateway.do?out_trade_no={order_id}&total_amount={amount}"
        logger.info(f"Alipay order created: {order_id} -> {mock_url}")
        return mock_url

    @staticmethod
    def alipay_notify(data: dict) -> bool:
        """支付宝异步通知处理"""
        # TODO: 验证签名
        order_id = data.get("out_trade_no")
        trade_status = data.get("trade_status")
        
        if trade_status == "TRADE_SUCCESS":
            # 找到支付记录
            with get_db_session() as db:
                payment = db.query(PaymentRecord).filter(
                    PaymentRecord.transaction_id == order_id
                ).first()
                if payment and payment.status == "pending":
                    PaymentService._complete_payment(payment.id, db)
                    db.commit()
                    logger.info(f"Alipay notification: order {order_id} completed")
                    return True
        
        return False
```

## 📦 修复 4：租户超额自动限流

### `backend/app/middleware/tenant_quota.py`
```python
from fastapi import Request, HTTPException
from starlette.middleware.base import BaseHTTPMiddleware
from app.services.tenant_service import TenantService
from app.core.context import get_tenant_id
from app.utils.redis_client import redis_client
from app.utils.logger import logger

class TenantQuotaMiddleware(BaseHTTPMiddleware):
    """
    租户配额检查中间件
    在消息处理前检查是否超额
    """
    
    async def dispatch(self, request: Request, call_next):
        # 只检查消息相关接口
        path = request.url.path
        if not path.startswith("/api/webhook") and not path.startswith("/api/messages/send"):
            return await call_next(request)
        
        tenant_id = get_tenant_id()
        if not tenant_id:
            return await call_next(request)
        
        # 从 Redis 获取实时用量（避免每次都查 DB）
        cache_key = f"waos:quota:{tenant_id}"
        quota_data = redis_client.get(cache_key)
        
        if not quota_data:
            # 从 DB 加载
            usage = TenantService.check_usage(tenant_id)
            redis_client.setex(cache_key, 300, json.dumps(usage))
        else:
            import json
            usage = json.loads(quota_data)
        
        # 检查是否超额
        if usage.get("usage_percent", 0) >= 100:
            logger.warning(f"Tenant {tenant_id} quota exceeded: {usage}")
            return JSONResponse(
                status_code=429,
                content={
                    "code": 429,
                    "msg": "消息配额已用完，请升级套餐",
                    "usage": usage
                }
            )
        
        # 如果接近限额（>90%），记录告警
        if usage.get("usage_percent", 0) >= 90:
            logger.warning(f"Tenant {tenant_id} quota approaching limit: {usage['usage_percent']}%")
        
        return await call_next(request)
```

### 在 `main.py` 中注册中间件
```python
from app.middleware.tenant_quota import TenantQuotaMiddleware
app.add_middleware(TenantQuotaMiddleware)
```

## 📦 修复 5：WebSocket 跨 Pod 广播（Redis Pub/Sub）

### `backend/app/core/ws_manager.py`
```python
import json
import asyncio
from typing import Dict, Set
from fastapi import WebSocket

from app.utils.redis_client import redis_client
from app.utils.logger import logger

class WSManager:
    """WebSocket 连接管理器（支持跨 Pod 广播）"""
    
    def __init__(self):
        self.active_connections: Dict[str, Set[WebSocket]] = {}  # tenant_id -> set of ws
        self.pubsub = redis_client.pubsub()
        self._running = False
    
    async def connect(self, websocket: WebSocket, tenant_id: str):
        """建立连接"""
        await websocket.accept()
        if tenant_id not in self.active_connections:
            self.active_connections[tenant_id] = set()
        self.active_connections[tenant_id].add(websocket)
        logger.info(f"WebSocket connected: tenant={tenant_id}")
    
    def disconnect(self, websocket: WebSocket, tenant_id: str):
        """断开连接"""
        if tenant_id in self.active_connections:
            self.active_connections[tenant_id].discard(websocket)
            if not self.active_connections[tenant_id]:
                del self.active_connections[tenant_id]
    
    async def broadcast(self, tenant_id: str, message: dict):
        """
        广播消息到同一租户的所有连接
        """
        # 1. 本地广播（本 Pod 内的连接）
        if tenant_id in self.active_connections:
            for ws in self.active_connections[tenant_id]:
                try:
                    await ws.send_json(message)
                except Exception as e:
                    logger.warning(f"Broadcast failed: {e}")
        
        # 2. 跨 Pod 广播（Redis Pub/Sub）
        channel = f"ws:{tenant_id}"
        await redis_client.publish(channel, json.dumps(message))
    
    async def start_redis_listener(self):
        """启动 Redis 订阅监听（跨 Pod 消息）"""
        if self._running:
            return
        
        self._running = True
        self.pubsub = redis_client.pubsub()
        
        # 订阅所有租户的频道
        await self.pubsub.psubscribe("ws:*")
        
        logger.info("WebSocket Redis listener started")
        
        while self._running:
            try:
                message = await self.pubsub.get_message(ignore_subscribe_messages=True, timeout=1.0)
                if message:
                    # 解析频道名：ws:{tenant_id}
                    channel = message.get("channel")
                    if channel:
                        if isinstance(channel, bytes):
                            channel = channel.decode()
                        tenant_id = channel.replace("ws:", "")
                        
                        # 本地广播
                        data = json.loads(message["data"])
                        if tenant_id in self.active_connections:
                            for ws in self.active_connections[tenant_id]:
                                try:
                                    await ws.send_json(data)
                                except:
                                    pass
            except Exception as e:
                logger.error(f"Redis listener error: {e}")
                await asyncio.sleep(1)
    
    async def stop(self):
        """停止监听"""
        self._running = False
        await self.pubsub.unsubscribe()
        await self.pubsub.close()
        logger.info("WebSocket Redis listener stopped")

# 全局实例
ws_manager = WSManager()
```

### 在 `backend/app/main.py` 中启动
```python
from app.core.ws_manager import ws_manager

@app.on_event("startup")
async def startup_event():
    # ... 原有初始化 ...
    asyncio.create_task(ws_manager.start_redis_listener())

@app.on_event("shutdown")
async def shutdown_event():
    await ws_manager.stop()
```
