## 📦 修复 7：Event Store 持久化到 PostgreSQL

### `backend/app/core/event_store.py`
```python
import json
from datetime import datetime
from typing import Optional
from uuid import UUID

from app.db.session import get_db_session
from app.models.event_log import EventLog
from app.core.context import get_tenant_id
from app.utils.logger import logger

class EventStore:
    """
    事件存储（持久化到 PostgreSQL）
    替代原先的 events.log 文本文件
    """
    
    @staticmethod
    def save(event_type: str, payload: dict, customer_id: Optional[str] = None):
        """保存事件"""
        tenant_id = get_tenant_id()
        if not tenant_id:
            # 如果没有租户上下文，使用默认
            tenant_id = "system"
        
        try:
            with get_db_session() as db:
                event_log = EventLog(
                    tenant_id=tenant_id,
                    event_type=event_type,
                    customer_id=customer_id,
                    payload=payload,
                    created_at=datetime.now()
                )
                db.add(event_log)
                db.commit()
        except Exception as e:
            logger.error(f"EventStore save failed: {e}")
    
    @staticmethod
    def get_events(
        event_type: Optional[str] = None,
        customer_id: Optional[str] = None,
        limit: int = 100,
        offset: int = 0
    ) -> list:
        """查询事件（用于审计/回放）"""
        tenant_id = get_tenant_id()
        if not tenant_id:
            return []
        
        with get_db_session() as db:
            query = db.query(EventLog).filter(
                EventLog.tenant_id == tenant_id
            )
            if event_type:
                query = query.filter(EventLog.event_type == event_type)
            if customer_id:
                query = query.filter(EventLog.customer_id == customer_id)
            
            events = query.order_by(EventLog.created_at.desc()).offset(offset).limit(limit).all()
            
            return [{
                "id": str(e.id),
                "event_type": e.event_type,
                "customer_id": e.customer_id,
                "payload": e.payload,
                "created_at": e.created_at.isoformat()
            } for e in events]
    
    @staticmethod
    def replay(customer_id: str, limit: int = 100) -> list:
        """回放客户事件（用于状态重建）"""
        return EventStore.get_events(
            customer_id=customer_id,
            limit=limit
        )
```

## 📦 修复 8：Grafana Dashboard 告警规则（Prometheus）

### `infra/prometheus/rules.yml`
```yaml
groups:
  - name: waos_alerts
    rules:
      - alert: HighErrorRate
        expr: sum(rate(waos_http_requests_total{status_code=~"5.."}[5m])) / sum(rate(waos_http_requests_total[5m])) > 0.05
        for: 5m
        labels:
          severity: critical
        annotations:
          summary: "WAOS 错误率超过 5%"
          description: "当前错误率: {{ $value }}%"

      - alert: HighLatency
        expr: histogram_quantile(0.95, sum(rate(waos_http_request_duration_seconds_bucket[5m])) by (le)) > 2
        for: 5m
        labels:
          severity: warning
        annotations:
          summary: "WAOS P95 延迟超过 2 秒"
          description: "当前 P95 延迟: {{ $value }}s"

      - alert: QueueLagging
        expr: redis_stream_lag > 100
        for: 2m
        labels:
          severity: warning
        annotations:
          summary: "Redis Stream 积压超过 100 条"
          description: "当前积压: {{ $value }} 条"

      - alert: HighMemoryUsage
        expr: container_memory_usage_bytes{container="waos-backend"} / container_spec_memory_limit_bytes > 0.85
        for: 5m
        labels:
          severity: warning
        annotations:
          summary: "Backend 内存使用超过 85%"
          description: "当前使用率: {{ $value | humanizePercentage }}"

      - alert: HighCPUUsage
        expr: rate(container_cpu_usage_seconds_total{container="waos-backend"}[5m]) > 0.8
        for: 5m
        labels:
          severity: warning
        annotations:
          summary: "Backend CPU 使用超过 80%"
```

## 📦 修复 1：JWT Refresh Token + 黑名单机制

### `backend/app/dependencies/auth.py`（追加）
```python
import uuid
import hashlib
from datetime import datetime, timedelta
from typing import Optional, Tuple

# ===== Refresh Token =====
REFRESH_TOKEN_EXPIRE_DAYS = 30

def create_refresh_token(user_id: UUID, tenant_id: UUID) -> str:
    """创建 Refresh Token（存储到 Redis）"""
    token_id = str(uuid.uuid4())
    token = f"rt_{token_id}_{user_id.hex[:8]}_{int(time.time())}"
    # 存储到 Redis
    redis_client.setex(
        f"waos:refresh:{token_id}",
        REFRESH_TOKEN_EXPIRE_DAYS * 86400,
        json.dumps({
            "user_id": str(user_id),
            "tenant_id": str(tenant_id),
            "created_at": time.time()
        })
    )
    return token

def verify_refresh_token(token: str) -> Optional[dict]:
    """验证 Refresh Token"""
    try:
        # 解析 token: rt_{token_id}_{user_id}_{timestamp}
        parts = token.split("_")
        if len(parts) != 4 or parts[0] != "rt":
            return None
        token_id = parts[1]
        
        data = redis_client.get(f"waos:refresh:{token_id}")
        if not data:
            return None
        
        return json.loads(data)
    except:
        return None

def revoke_refresh_token(token_id: str):
    """撤销 Refresh Token（登出时调用）"""
    redis_client.delete(f"waos:refresh:{token_id}")

def revoke_all_refresh_tokens(user_id: UUID):
    """撤销用户所有 Refresh Token"""
    # 使用 pattern 扫描（生产环境建议维护用户->token列表）
    keys = redis_client.keys(f"waos:refresh:*")
    for key in keys:
        data = redis_client.get(key)
        if data and json.loads(data).get("user_id") == str(user_id):
            redis_client.delete(key)

# ===== Access Token 黑名单 =====
class TokenBlacklist:
    @staticmethod
    def add(token: str, expires_in: int = 3600):
        """将 Token 加入黑名单（登出时调用）"""
        # 使用 SHA256 哈希存储（避免明文）
        token_hash = hashlib.sha256(token.encode()).hexdigest()
        redis_client.setex(f"waos:blacklist:{token_hash}", expires_in, "1")
    
    @staticmethod
    def is_blacklisted(token: str) -> bool:
        """检查 Token 是否在黑名单中"""
        token_hash = hashlib.sha256(token.encode()).hexdigest()
        return redis_client.exists(f"waos:blacklist:{token_hash}") > 0

# ===== 修改 get_current_tenant，加入黑名单检查 =====
async def get_current_tenant(
    credentials: HTTPAuthorizationCredentials = Depends(security)
) -> UUID:
    token = credentials.credentials
    
    # 1. 检查黑名单
    if TokenBlacklist.is_blacklisted(token):
        raise HTTPException(status_code=401, detail="Token revoked")
    
    # 2. 解码 Token（原有逻辑）
    payload = decode_token(token)
    # ... 后续逻辑不变 ...

# ===== 新增 Refresh Token 端点 =====
@router.post("/refresh")
async def refresh_token(refresh_token: str):
    """使用 Refresh Token 获取新的 Access Token"""
    data = verify_refresh_token(refresh_token)
    if not data:
        raise HTTPException(401, "Invalid refresh token")
    
    user_id = UUID(data["user_id"])
    tenant_id = UUID(data["tenant_id"])
    
    # 生成新 Token
    new_token = create_access_token(user_id, tenant_id)
    
    # 旧 Refresh Token 不变（可继续使用，或选择轮换）
    return {
        "access_token": new_token,
        "token_type": "bearer",
        "expires_in": JWT_EXPIRE_MINUTES * 60
    }

# ===== 修改登出端点 =====
@router.post("/logout")
async def logout(
    credentials: HTTPAuthorizationCredentials = Depends(security)
):
    """登出：撤销 Token"""
    token = credentials.credentials
    
    # 解码获取过期时间
    payload = decode_token(token)
    exp = payload.get("exp", int(time.time() + 3600))
    expires_in = exp - int(time.time())
    
    # 加入黑名单
    TokenBlacklist.add(token, max(expires_in, 60))
    
    # 可选：撤销 Refresh Token
    # revoke_refresh_token(...)
    
    return {"status": "logged out"}
```

## 📦 修复 2：租户数据导出（GDPR 合规）

### `backend/app/api/tenant.py`（追加）
```python
import json
import zipfile
import io
from fastapi import Response

@router.get("/export")
async def export_tenant_data(
    tenant_id: UUID = Depends(get_current_tenant),
    format: str = "json"
):
    """
    导出租户所有数据（GDPR 数据可携权）
    支持 JSON / ZIP 格式
    """
    with get_db_session() as db:
        # 1. 租户信息
        tenant = db.query(Tenant).filter(Tenant.id == tenant_id).first()
        
        # 2. 所有客户
        customers = db.query(Customer).filter(Customer.tenant_id == tenant_id).all()
        
        # 3. 所有会话
        conversations = db.query(Conversation).filter(Conversation.tenant_id == tenant_id).all()
        
        # 4. 所有消息
        messages = db.query(Message).filter(Message.tenant_id == tenant_id).all()
        
        # 5. 所有评论
        comments = db.query(Comment).filter(Comment.tenant_id == tenant_id).all()
        
        # 6. 所有线索
        leads = db.query(Lead).filter(Lead.tenant_id == tenant_id).all()
        
        # 7. 所有事件日志
        events = db.query(EventLog).filter(EventLog.tenant_id == tenant_id).all()
        
        export_data = {
            "tenant": {
                "id": str(tenant.id),
                "name": tenant.name,
                "subdomain": tenant.subdomain,
                "plan": tenant.plan.value,
                "created_at": tenant.created_at.isoformat()
            },
            "customers": [
                {
                    "id": str(c.id),
                    "wx_id": c.wx_id,
                    "name": c.name,
                    "stage": c.stage,
                    "score": c.deal_score,
                    "profile": c.profile,
                    "created_at": c.created_at.isoformat()
                }
                for c in customers
            ],
            "conversations": [...],
            "messages": [...],
            "comments": [...],
            "leads": [...],
            "events": [...]
        }
    
    if format == "json":
        return Response(
            content=json.dumps(export_data, ensure_ascii=False, indent=2, default=str),
            media_type="application/json",
            headers={"Content-Disposition": f"attachment; filename=waos_export_{tenant_id.hex[:8]}.json"}
        )
    
    elif format == "zip":
        # 打包为 ZIP
        zip_buffer = io.BytesIO()
        with zipfile.ZipFile(zip_buffer, "w", zipfile.ZIP_DEFLATED) as zf:
            zf.writestr("tenant.json", json.dumps(export_data, ensure_ascii=False, indent=2, default=str))
        
        return Response(
            content=zip_buffer.getvalue(),
            media_type="application/zip",
            headers={"Content-Disposition": f"attachment; filename=waos_export_{tenant_id.hex[:8]}.zip"}
        )
    
    raise HTTPException(400, "Unsupported format")

@router.delete("/tenant")
async def delete_tenant(
    tenant_id: UUID = Depends(get_current_tenant),
    confirm: str = None
):
    """
    删除租户（软删除 + 确认）
    """
    if confirm != "DELETE":
        raise HTTPException(400, '请确认删除: 传入 confirm="DELETE"')
    
    with get_db_session() as db:
        tenant = db.query(Tenant).filter(Tenant.id == tenant_id).first()
        if not tenant:
            raise HTTPException(404, "Tenant not found")
        
        # 软删除：标记状态，保留数据 30 天
        tenant.status = TenantStatus.SUSPENDED
        tenant.config = {
            **tenant.config,
            "deleted_at": datetime.now().isoformat(),
            "delete_scheduled": "30_days"
        }
        db.commit()
        
        # TODO: 30 天后执行硬删除（由定时任务执行）
        logger.info(f"Tenant {tenant_id} scheduled for deletion")
        
        return {
            "status": "deleted",
            "message": "租户已标记删除，数据将保留30天",
            "permanent_deletion_at": (datetime.now() + timedelta(days=30)).isoformat()
        }
```

## 📦 修复 3：ClickHouse 事件存储（替代 PG event_logs）

### `backend/app/core/clickhouse_client.py`
```python
import os
from typing import Optional, List, Dict, Any
from datetime import datetime
import aiohttp

from app.utils.logger import logger

class ClickHouseClient:
    """ClickHouse HTTP 客户端（用于事件存储）"""
    
    def __init__(self):
        self.host = os.getenv("CLICKHOUSE_HOST", "clickhouse")
        self.port = int(os.getenv("CLICKHOUSE_PORT", 8123))
        self.database = os.getenv("CLICKHOUSE_DATABASE", "waos")
        self.base_url = f"http://{self.host}:{self.port}"
        self._session = None
    
    async def _get_session(self):
        if self._session is None:
            self._session = aiohttp.ClientSession()
        return self._session
    
    async def execute(self, query: str) -> List[Dict]:
        """执行查询"""
        session = await self._get_session()
        url = f"{self.base_url}/?query={query.replace(' ', '%20')}"
        
        try:
            async with session.get(url) as resp:
                if resp.status == 200:
                    return await resp.json()
                else:
                    logger.error(f"ClickHouse error: {await resp.text()}")
                    return []
        except Exception as e:
            logger.error(f"ClickHouse query failed: {e}")
            return []
    
    async def insert_event(self, event: Dict[str, Any]):
        """插入事件（异步）"""
        tenant_id = event.get("tenant_id", "system")
        event_type = event.get("event_type", "unknown")
        customer_id = event.get("customer_id", "")
        payload = event.get("payload", {})
        
        query = f"""
        INSERT INTO {self.database}.events 
        (tenant_id, event_type, customer_id, payload, created_at)
        VALUES ('{tenant_id}', '{event_type}', '{customer_id}', 
                '{json.dumps(payload)}', now())
        """
        session = await self._get_session()
        url = f"{self.base_url}/?query={query}"
        
        try:
            async with session.post(url) as resp:
                if resp.status != 200:
                    logger.error(f"ClickHouse insert failed: {await resp.text()}")
        except Exception as e:
            logger.error(f"ClickHouse insert error: {e}")
    
    async def get_events(self, tenant_id: str, limit: int = 100) -> List[Dict]:
        """查询事件"""
        query = f"""
        SELECT * FROM {self.database}.events 
        WHERE tenant_id = '{tenant_id}' 
        ORDER BY created_at DESC 
        LIMIT {limit}
        """
        return await self.execute(query)
    
    async def close(self):
        if self._session:
            await self._session.close()

# 全局实例
clickhouse = ClickHouseClient()
```

### `migrations/clickhouse/001_events.sql`
```sql
-- ClickHouse 事件表
CREATE DATABASE IF NOT EXISTS waos;

CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS waos.events (
    tenant_id String,
    event_type String,
    customer_id String,
    payload String,
    created_at DateTime
) ENGINE = MergeTree()
ORDER BY (tenant_id, created_at)
PARTITION BY toYYYYMM(created_at)
TTL created_at + INTERVAL 365 DAY
SETTINGS index_granularity = 8192;

-- 物化视图：按天聚合
CREATE MATERIALIZED VIEW IF NOT EXISTS waos.events_daily
ENGINE = SummingMergeTree()
ORDER BY (tenant_id, date)
AS SELECT
    tenant_id,
    toDate(created_at) AS date,
    count() AS total_events,
    countIf(event_type = 'message.received') AS messages_received,
    countIf(event_type = 'message.sent') AS messages_sent,
    countIf(event_type = 'deal.closed') AS deals_closed
FROM waos.events
GROUP BY tenant_id, date;
```

### 1.3 迁移脚本 `migrations/clickhouse/001_events.sql`
```sql
-- 创建数据库
CREATE DATABASE IF NOT EXISTS waos;

-- 事件表（主表）
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS waos.events (
    event_id String,
    tenant_id String,
    event_type String,
    customer_id String,
    account_id String,
    payload String,
    trace_id String,
    created_at DateTime64(3)
) ENGINE = MergeTree()
ORDER BY (tenant_id, created_at)
PARTITION BY toYYYYMM(created_at)
TTL created_at + INTERVAL 365 DAY
SETTINGS index_granularity = 8192;

-- 消息事件表（子表，针对高频查询优化）
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS waos.message_events (
    tenant_id String,
    customer_id String,
    platform String,
    direction String,  -- in / out
    content String,
    is_ai Bool,
    created_at DateTime64(3)
) ENGINE = MergeTree()
ORDER BY (tenant_id, customer_id, created_at)
PARTITION BY toYYYYMM(created_at)
TTL created_at + INTERVAL 90 DAY;

-- 每日聚合物化视图
CREATE MATERIALIZED VIEW IF NOT EXISTS waos.events_daily
ENGINE = SummingMergeTree()
ORDER BY (tenant_id, date)
AS SELECT
    tenant_id,
    toDate(created_at) AS date,
    count() AS total_events,
    countIf(event_type = 'message.received') AS messages_received,
    countIf(event_type = 'message.sent') AS messages_sent,
    countIf(event_type = 'comment.received') AS comments_received,
    countIf(event_type = 'comment.converted_dm') AS dm_converted,
    countIf(event_type = 'deal.closed') AS deals_closed,
    countIf(event_type LIKE 'ai.%') AS ai_calls
FROM waos.events
GROUP BY tenant_id, date;

-- 月聚合物化视图
CREATE MATERIALIZED VIEW IF NOT EXISTS waos.events_monthly
ENGINE = SummingMergeTree()
ORDER BY (tenant_id, month)
AS SELECT
    tenant_id,
    toStartOfMonth(created_at) AS month,
    sum(messages_received) AS messages_received,
    sum(messages_sent) AS messages_sent,
    sum(comments_received) AS comments_received,
    sum(dm_converted) AS dm_converted,
    sum(deals_closed) AS deals_closed,
    sum(ai_calls) AS ai_calls
FROM waos.events_daily
GROUP BY tenant_id, month;

-- 实时聚合表
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS waos.realtime_metrics (
    tenant_id String,
    metric_type String,
    value Int64,
    updated_at DateTime
) ENGINE = ReplacingMergeTree(updated_at)
ORDER BY (tenant_id, metric_type);
```

### 1.4 增量同步 Worker `backend/app/worker/clickhouse_sync.py`
```python
import asyncio
import json
from datetime import datetime, timedelta
from app.db.session import get_db_session
from app.models.event_log import EventLog
from app.core.clickhouse_client import clickhouse
from app.utils.logger import logger
from app.utils.redis_client import redis_client

class ClickHouseSyncWorker:
    """将 PostgreSQL event_logs 增量同步到 ClickHouse"""
    
    BATCH_SIZE = 1000
    SYNC_INTERVAL = 60  # 秒
    
    async def run(self):
        """持续运行同步任务"""
        logger.info("ClickHouse sync worker started")
        
        while True:
            try:
                # 获取上次同步的游标
                last_id = redis_client.get("clickhouse:last_sync_id")
                if last_id:
                    last_id = int(last_id)
                else:
                    last_id = 0
                
                with get_db_session() as db:
                    # 查询增量数据
                    events = db.query(EventLog).filter(
                        EventLog.id > last_id
                    ).order_by(EventLog.id).limit(self.BATCH_SIZE).all()
                    
                    if events:
                        # 批量插入 ClickHouse
                        for event in events:
                            await clickhouse.insert_event({
                                "event_id": str(event.id),
                                "tenant_id": str(event.tenant_id),
                                "event_type": event.event_type,
                                "customer_id": event.customer_id,
                                "payload": json.dumps(event.payload or {}),
                                "created_at": event.created_at.isoformat()
                            })
                        
                        # 更新游标
                        redis_client.set("clickhouse:last_sync_id", events[-1].id)
                        logger.info(f"Synced {len(events)} events to ClickHouse")
                    
                    # 如果没有更多数据，等待
                    if len(events) < self.BATCH_SIZE:
                        await asyncio.sleep(self.SYNC_INTERVAL)
                    
            except Exception as e:
                logger.error(f"ClickHouse sync error: {e}")
                await asyncio.sleep(60)
```

### 2.3 集合自动清理脚本 `scripts/cleanup_qdrant.py`
```python
#!/usr/bin/env python3
"""
Qdrant 集合数据清理（按租户/时间）
"""
import os
import sys
from datetime import datetime, timedelta
from qdrant_client import QdrantClient
from qdrant_client.http import models

QDRANT_HOST = os.getenv("QDRANT_HOST", "localhost")
QDRANT_PORT = int(os.getenv("QDRANT_PORT", 6333))

def cleanup_old_vectors(collection_name: str, days_old: int = 90):
    """删除超过指定天数的向量"""
    client = QdrantClient(host=QDRANT_HOST, port=QDRANT_PORT)
    
    cutoff = (datetime.now() - timedelta(days=days_old)).timestamp()
    
    # 按时间戳删除（payload 中的 created_at 字段）
    filter_obj = models.Filter(
        must=[
            models.FieldCondition(
                key="created_at",
                range=models.Range(lt=cutoff)
            )
        ]
    )
    
    try:
        client.delete(
            collection_name=collection_name,
            points_selector=models.FilterSelector(filter=filter_obj)
        )
        print(f"Deleted old vectors from {collection_name}")
    except Exception as e:
        print(f"Cleanup failed: {e}")

if __name__ == "__main__":
    collections = ["knowledge_product", "knowledge_faq", "knowledge_case", "knowledge_memory"]
    for col in collections:
        cleanup_old_vectors(col, 90)
```

### 2.4 定时清理任务（cron）
```bash
# 每周日凌晨 4:00 清理 Qdrant 过期向量
0 4 * * 0 cd /opt/waos && python scripts/cleanup_qdrant.py >> /var/log/qdrant-cleanup.log 2>&1
```

### 3.2 压测报告生成脚本 `scripts/generate_report.py`
```python
#!/usr/bin/env python3
"""
从 Locust CSV 生成压测报告
"""
import csv
import json
import os
from datetime import datetime

def generate_report(csv_path: str):
    """生成压测报告"""
    # 读取 Locust CSV
    with open(f"{csv_path}_stats.csv", "r") as f:
        reader = csv.DictReader(f)
        rows = list(reader)
    
    total_requests = sum(int(r["Request Count"]) for r in rows if r["Name"] != "Aggregated")
    total_failures = sum(int(r["Failure Count"]) for r in rows if r["Name"] != "Aggregated")
    error_rate = (total_failures / total_requests * 100) if total_requests > 0 else 0
    
    # 读取汇总数据
    with open(f"{csv_path}_stats_history.csv", "r") as f:
        hist = list(csv.DictReader(f))
    
    if hist:
        last = hist[-1]
        qps = float(last.get("Total Requests per second", 0))
        p95_latency = float(last.get("95 percentile", 0)) * 1000  # 转 ms
    else:
        qps = 0
        p95_latency = 0
    
    # 判断结果
    qps_pass = qps >= 500
    latency_pass = p95_latency <= 2000
    error_pass = error_rate <= 1
    
    # 内存使用（从系统指标获取）
    memory_usage = 0
    try:
        with open("/proc/meminfo") as f:
            for line in f:
                if "MemAvailable" in line:
                    memory_usage = (int(line.split()[1]) / 1024)  # KB to MB
                    break
    except:
        memory_usage = 0
    
    memory_pass = memory_usage < 4096
    
    # 渲染 HTML
    with open("reports/performance_template.html") as f:
        template = f.read()
    
    template = template.replace("{{date}}", datetime.now().strftime("%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S"))
    template = template.replace("{{users}}", "100")
    template = template.replace("{{duration}}", "60")
    template = template.replace("{{total_requests}}", str(total_requests))
    template = template.replace("{{qps}}", f"{qps:.2f}")
    template = template.replace("{{qps_status}}", "pass" if qps_pass else "fail")
    template = template.replace("{{p95_latency}}", f"{p95_latency:.0f}")
    template = template.replace("{{latency_status}}", "pass" if latency_pass else "fail")
    template = template.replace("{{error_rate}}", f"{error_rate:.2f}")
    template = template.replace("{{error_status}}", "pass" if error_pass else "fail")
    template = template.replace("{{memory_usage}}", f"{memory_usage:.0f}")
    template = template.replace("{{memory_status}}", "pass" if memory_pass else "fail")
    
    if qps_pass and latency_pass and error_pass and memory_pass:
        template = template.replace("{{final_status}}", "✅ 所有指标通过")
        template = template.replace("{{final_status_color}}", "#7CFFB2")
        template = template.replace("{{final_message}}", "系统性能达标，可以上线！")
    else:
        template = template.replace("{{final_status}}", "❌ 部分指标未达标")
        template = template.replace("{{final_status_color}}", "#FF5C7A")
        template = template.replace("{{final_message}}", "请检查瓶颈，优化后重新压测。")
    
    output_path = f"reports/report_{datetime.now().strftime('%Y%m%d_%H%M%S')}.html"
    with open(output_path, "w") as f:
        f.write(template)
    
    print(f"Report generated: {output_path}")

if __name__ == "__main__":
    import sys
    if len(sys.argv) < 2:
        print("Usage: python generate_report.py <locust_csv_prefix>")
        sys.exit(1)
    generate_report(sys.argv[1])
```

### 最终 `docker-compose.prod.yml`（完整）
```yaml
version: "3.9"

services:
  postgres:
    image: postgres:15
    restart: always
    container_name: waos-postgres
    environment:
      POSTGRES_USER: waos
      POSTGRES_PASSWORD: ${DB_PASSWORD}
      POSTGRES_DB: waos
      POSTGRES_INITDB_ARGS: "--data-checksums"
    volumes:
      - pg_data:/var/lib/postgresql/data
    ports:
      - "5432:5432"
    healthcheck:
      test: ["CMD-SHELL", "pg_isready -U waos"]
      interval: 30s
      timeout: 10s
      retries: 5
    logging:
      driver: "json-file"
      options:
        max-size: "50m"
        max-file: "3"

  redis:
    image: redis:7-alpine
    restart: always
    container_name: waos-redis
    command: redis-server --appendonly yes --maxmemory 512mb --maxmemory-policy allkeys-lru --save 900 1 --save 300 10 --save 60 10000
    volumes:
      - redis_data:/data
    ports:
      - "6379:6379"
    healthcheck:
      test: ["CMD", "redis-cli", "ping"]
      interval: 30s
      timeout: 10s
    logging:
      driver: "json-file"
      options:
        max-size: "50m"
        max-file: "3"

  qdrant:
    image: qdrant/qdrant:latest
    restart: always
    container_name: waos-qdrant
    volumes:
      - qdrant_data:/qdrant/storage
      - ./infra/qdrant/config.yaml:/qdrant/config/config.yaml:ro
    ports:
      - "6333:6333"
      - "6334:6334"
    environment:
      - QDRANT__SERVICE__API_KEY=${QDRANT_API_KEY:-}
      - QDRANT__STORAGE__MMAP_THRESHOLD=10000
    ulimits:
      memlock:
        soft: -1
        hard: -1

  clickhouse:
    image: clickhouse/clickhouse-server:24.8
    restart: always
    container_name: waos-clickhouse
    ports:
      - "8123:8123"
      - "9000:9000"
    volumes:
      - clickhouse_data:/var/lib/clickhouse
      - ./infra/clickhouse/config.xml:/etc/clickhouse-server/config.d/config.xml:ro
    environment:
      - CLICKHOUSE_DB=waos
      - CLICKHOUSE_USER=waos
      - CLICKHOUSE_PASSWORD=${CLICKHOUSE_PASSWORD}
    ulimits:
      nofile:
        soft: 262144
        hard: 262144

  backend:
    build:
      context: ./backend
      dockerfile: Dockerfile
    restart: always
    container_name: waos-backend
    ports:
      - "8000:8000"
    depends_on:
      postgres:
        condition: service_healthy
      redis:
        condition: service_healthy
    environment:
      - DATABASE_URL=postgresql://waos:${DB_PASSWORD}@postgres:5432/waos
      - REDIS_URL=redis://redis:6379/0
      - QDRANT_HOST=qdrant
      - CLICKHOUSE_HOST=clickhouse
      - OPENAI_API_KEY=${OPENAI_API_KEY}
      - OPENAI_MODEL=${OPENAI_MODEL}
      - LLM_PROVIDER=${LLM_PROVIDER}
      - JWT_SECRET=${JWT_SECRET}
      - ENVIRONMENT=production
      - LOG_LEVEL=INFO
    healthcheck:
      test: ["CMD", "curl", "-f", "http://localhost:8000/health/ping"]
      interval: 60s
      timeout: 5s
      retries: 3
    logging:
      driver: "json-file"
      options:
        max-size: "50m"
        max-file: "3"

  worker:
    build:
      context: ./backend
      dockerfile: Dockerfile
    restart: always
    container_name: waos-worker
    command: python -m app.runner
    depends_on:
      redis:
        condition: service_healthy
    environment:
      - DATABASE_URL=postgresql://waos:${DB_PASSWORD}@postgres:5432/waos
      - REDIS_URL=redis://redis:6379/0
      - QDRANT_HOST=qdrant
      - CLICKHOUSE_HOST=clickhouse
      - OPENAI_API_KEY=${OPENAI_API_KEY}
      - OPENAI_MODEL=${OPENAI_MODEL}
      - LLM_PROVIDER=${LLM_PROVIDER}
      - JWT_SECRET=${JWT_SECRET}
      - ENVIRONMENT=production
      - LOG_LEVEL=INFO
    logging:
      driver: "json-file"
      options:
        max-size: "50m"
        max-file: "3"

  frontend:
    build:
      context: ./frontend
      dockerfile: Dockerfile
    restart: always
    container_name: waos-frontend
    ports:
      - "3000:3000"
    depends_on:
      - backend
    logging:
      driver: "json-file"
      options:
        max-size: "50m"
        max-file: "3"

  nginx:
    image: nginx:alpine
    restart: always
    container_name: waos-nginx
    ports:
      - "80:80"
      - "443:443"
    volumes:
      - ./infra/nginx/nginx.conf:/etc/nginx/nginx.conf:ro
      - ./infra/ssl:/etc/nginx/ssl:ro
    depends_on:
      - backend
      - frontend
    logging:
      driver: "json-file"
      options:
        max-size: "50m"
        max-file: "3"

volumes:
  pg_data:
    driver: local
  redis_data:
    driver: local
  qdrant_data:
    driver: local
  clickhouse_data:
    driver: local
```
